340. Cora dilê min corê, Yala melhema birîna min milê.
340. The pain of my heart is pain, O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

341. 3. Behzan û behzgîna,
341. 3. Falcons and falconers,

342. Şevê-rojê nêçîra,
342. Hunting night and day,

343. Nêçîra te heye dîndara mîra.
343. Your hunt belongs to the pious ones of the princes.

344. Cora dilê min corê, Yala melhema birîna min milê.
344. The pain of my heart is pain, O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

345. Meha kanûna paş sala 1977an li şeherê Abovyana Ermenistanê ji zarê Zaîlê Şêx Ahmedî hatiye nivîsîn.
345. In the month of December of the year 1977 in the city of Abovyan in Armenia it was written down from the mouth of Zaîl son of Şêx Ahmed.

346. Zaîl vî qewlî ji Erebê Şêx Avasî hîn bûye.
346. Zaîl learned this qewl from Ereb son of Şêx Avas.

347. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda". Cildê I., Yêrêvan, r. 452-457.
347. It was printed in "Folklore of the Kurds". Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 452-457.

348. Temûrê Meso di berhevoka bi navê "Newşe Dînê Êzdîyan" da hin versiyon dane ber hev.
348. Temûrê Meso in the collection named "Adornment of the Faith of the Yezidis" compared some versions.

349. Me li wê xebatê mêze kir û ya xwe jî da ber wan.
349. We looked at that work and compared ours with them.

350. Peyv û gotinên ku gumanên me li ser wan hene me bi kurteya berhema nav borî (bnb) ji wir ji bo baştir bê famkirin rûqalî hev kir.
350. Words and expressions about which we have doubts, we compared side by side with the abbreviation of the above-mentioned work (bnb) for better understanding.

351. Me bala xwe da peyvên ku bi tîpên mezin û biçûk hatine nivîsîn.
351. We paid attention to words written with capital and small letters.

352. 4. Xazka mi zaniya,
352. 4. Would that I had known,

353. Rengê behza kî alî ye,
353. Which side the color of the falcons is,

354. Min ê bigirta bi nijar e.
354. I would have caught it with a net.

355. Cora dilê min corê, Yala melhema birîna min milê.
355. The pain of my heart is pain, O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

356. 5. Nijar e, ne li ber e,
356. 5. It is a net, it is not before us,

357. Ne li ax e, mîna misk û maware,
357. It is not in the earth, like musk and ambergris,

358. Yala serê min defter e.
358. O my head is a register.

359. Cora dilê min corê, Yala melhema birîna min milê.
359. The pain of my heart is pain, O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

360. 6. Behz hatin, behz bihurîn,
360. 6. Falcons came, falcons passed,

361. Dilê min da kew û girî,
361. In my heart are bewailing and weeping,

362. Yala 'hewalê behza kirî.
362. O friend who acted like falcons.

363. Cora dilê min corê, Yala melhema birîna min milê.
363. The pain of my heart is pain, O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

364. 7. Behz hatin, behz diçûne,
364. 7. Falcons came, falcons were going,

365. Dilê min i [li] dû ne,
365. My heart is behind them,

366. Xazila hevalê behza bûma.
366. Would that I were a companion of falcons.

367. Cora dilê min corê, Yala melhema birîna min milê.
367. The pain of my heart is pain, O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

368. 8. Dehfa min bînin,
368. 8. Bring my snare,

369. Derê dirbê werînin,
369. Bring down the path of the track,

370. Behzîyê dûr dixûnin.
370. They call the distant falcon.

371. Cora dilê min corê, Yala melhema birîna min milê.
371. The pain of my heart is pain, O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

372. 9. Dehfa min e mû ye,
372. 9. My snare is of hair,

373. Derê dirbê danîye,
373. It is set upon the path of the track,

374. Behzîkê tê hilbîye,
374. A falcon is caught in it,

375. Behz firî min nizanîye.
375. The falcon flew, I did not know it.

376. Cora dilê min corê,
376. The pain of my heart is pain,

377. Yala melhema birîna min milê.
377. O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

378. 10. Dehfa min raxistî,
378. 10. My snare is spread,

379. Behzîkê tê nivistî,
379. A falcon is settled in it,

380. Behz firî nizanbû,
380. The falcon flew, I did not know,

381. Surra Amadîn, Sicadîn û Şemsê min î Êzdî.
381. It is the secret of Amadîn, Sicadîn and my Yezidi Şems.

382. Cora dilê min corê,
382. The pain of my heart is pain,

383. Yala melhema birîna min milê.
383. O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

384. 11. Dehfa min vedave,
384. 11. My snare springs shut,

385. Behzîkê ketîya nav e,
385. A falcon has fallen inside it,

386. Behz min girtî, min berdave.
386. The falcon I caught, I released.

387. Cora dilê min corê,
387. The pain of my heart is pain,

388. Yala melhema birîna min milê.
388. O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

389. 12. Mezela der nijînî,
389. 12. The lodge outside is built,

390. Behzîkê tê wetinî,
390. A falcon dwells in it,

391. Behz firî, kundê dewsê sekinî.
391. The falcon flew, the owl stood in its place.

392. Cora dilê min corê,
392. The pain of my heart is pain,

393. Yala melhema birîna min milê.
393. O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

394. 13. Mezela der girê da,
394. 13. The lodge outside is tied,

395. Behzîkê tê di pirê da,
395. A falcon is in the bridge,

396. Behz firî, kundê mabû dewsê da.
396. The falcon flew, the owl remained in its place.

397. Cora dilê min corê,
397. The pain of my heart is pain,

398. Yala melhema birîna min milê.
398. O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

399. 14. Mezela der dadaî,
399. 14. The lodge outside is closed,

400. Behzîkê tê di nemai,
400. A falcon did not remain in it,

401. Behz firî, kundê dewsê di maî.
401. The falcon flew, the owl remained in its place.

402. Cora dilê min corê,
402. The pain of my heart is pain,

403. Yala melhema birîna min milê.
403. O cure for my wound, my shoulder.

404. 15. Şerefa lawêd pîra,
404. 15. The honor of the sons of the pîrs,

405. Dil sotin qeda wî da,
405. Hearts burned in his affliction,

406. Şeref e, şebeq e, digerin nêçîrê cehdû da,
406. It is honor, it is dawn, they roam the hunt in striving,

407. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
407. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

408. Ew hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
408. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

409. 16. Şerefa lawêd 'incûza,
409. 16. The honor of the sons of the miraculous,

410. Dê û bavê xwe dikin naza,
410. They coax their mother and father,

411. Şeref e, şebeq e, digerin nêçîrêd behza.
411. It is honor, it is dawn, they roam the hunts of falcons.

412. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
412. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

413. Ew hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
413. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

414. 17. Şerefa tî axdar î,
414. 17. The honor is you are the lord of the land,

415. Cawa ti qadir î,
415. How mighty you are,

416. Bangîna ti hazir î.
416. At the call you are present.

417. Erhemdúlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda î,
417. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

418. Ew hémeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
418. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

419. 18. Şerefa rê nasí,
419. 18. The honor of knowing the way,

420. Behra tî xwas î,
420. You are the chosen of the sea,

421. 7. Ferdost: Ferdost bi maneya dostê ku fera wî/wê tune ye û yekta ye dide.
421. 7. Ferdost: Ferdost gives the meaning of a friend who has no match and is unique.

422. Tu Xidir î, yan Eylas î.
422. You are Xidir, or you are Eylas.

423. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
423. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

424. Ew hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
424. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

425. 19. Hatye bazirgan e,
425. 19. A merchant has come,

426. Danîye hewirdorê şeheran e,
426. He has set up around the cities,

427. Barê wana lal û durr û mircan e.
427. Their load is rubies and pearls and corals.

428. Xasê Şîx Adî dikirne gazî: "Ser bi ser, can bi can e,
428. The saint of Şîx Adî was calling out: "Head for head, soul for soul,

429. Barê wan sivik e ne arzan e."
429. Their load is light, it is not cheap."

430. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
430. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

431. Ew hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
431. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

432. 20. Hatye ser te bazar e,
432. 20. A market has come upon you,

433. Bazara xwe bike sitar e,
433. Make your market a shelter,

434. Bandê ba mîrê xwe nebe şermezar e.
434. Do not be ashamed as a servant before your prince.

435. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
435. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

436. Ew hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
436. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

437. 21. Hatye ser te bazareke boş,
437. 21. An abundant market has come upon you,

438. Durr hatine bi koş,
438. Pearls have come by the lapful,

439. Hew xazila min wî evdî durr baha bikire, arzan nefroş.
439. Would that that servant buy the pearl dearly, and not sell it cheap.

440. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
440. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

441. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
441. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

442. 22. We divê ela ye,
442. 22. You need what is supreme,

443. Heqê zikatê heye, dua ye,
443. There is the right of alms, it is a prayer,

444. Heçkê kesê serê zeremisqalê ser maye,
444. Whoever has a speck of gold left over,

445. Ew jî bandê pîr cefa ye.
445. He too is a servant of much suffering.

446. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
446. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

447. 8. Ilyas (bnb).
447. 8. Ilyas (bnb).

448. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
448. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

449. 23. Rojekê roj xoş dibe,
449. 23. One day the day becomes pleasant,

450. Xelq hemû xet xoş dibe,
450. All the people become pleasant of line,

451. Ne xazila ruhê derewînî inkoş' dibe.
451. Alas for the lying soul that is denied.

452. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
452. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

453. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, were me bî.
453. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

454. 24. Rojekê ser Pira Selatê,
454. 24. One day upon the Bridge of Sirat,

455. Xerqê here bûsatê,
455. The cloak will go to the judgment place,

456. Heçkê kesê ne ser sebeqa xerqe be, qalibê gunekarê here kişimate.
456. Whoever is not upon the stanza of the cloak, the body of the sinner will go to distress.

457. Erhemdúlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
457. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

458. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
458. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

459. 25. Rojekê ser pira nehîn e,
459. 25. One day upon the hidden bridge,

460. Xerqe ê here xezîn e,
460. The cloak will go to the treasury,

461. 'Hekê kesê ne ser sebeqa xerqe be, qalibê gunekarê here beytil mesîl e."
461. Whoever is not upon the stanza of the cloak, the body of the sinner will go to the house of torment."

462. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
462. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

463. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
463. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

464. 26. Rojekê li wê dibe,
464. 26. One day it happens there,

465. Kursi xarî erdê dibe,
465. The throne is lowered to the earth,

466. Kaxaza wan mistê dibe,
466. Their paper is in the fist,

467. Kêr 'emelê wan temam lê dibe.
467. The use of their deeds is completely upon them.

468. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
468. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

469. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
469. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

470. 9. inkar (bnb).
470. 9. inkar (bnb).

471. 10. hismatê (bnb).
471. 10. hismatê (bnb).

472. 11. Beyt il-Mesile (bnb).
472. 11. Beyt il-Mesile (bnb).

473. 27. Rojekê wê bive axirzeman e,
473. 27. One day it will be the end of time,

474. Hezêz [d]ê tê keve qebran e,
474. The shaking will fall into the graves,

475. Sunîê bavêne behran e.
475. The Sunnis will be thrown into the seas.

476. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
476. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

477. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
477. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

478. 28. Ne kesê kesan e, ne bavê pisan e,
478. 28. There is no person of persons, no father of sons,

479. Wê rojekê yar-birê axretê hewekê bidne ser biran e,
479. On that day the brotherly friend of the hereafter will give a breath to the brothers,

480. Tehrîê şeva derxin bînin ber ronkaya çiran e.
480. They will extract the darkness of the nights and bring it before the light of the lamps.

481. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
481. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

482. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
482. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

483. 29. Rojekê wê bive axir e,
483. 29. One day it will be the end,

484. Wê rabe ferxekî faxir e,
484. A glorious offspring will rise,

485. Ne kesê kesan e, ne bavê pisan e,
485. There is no person of persons, no father of sons,

486. Wê rojê yar-birê axretê hewekê bidne ser biran e.
486. On that day the brotherly friend of the hereafter will give a breath to the brothers.

487. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
487. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

488. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdoste, werê me bî.
488. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

489. 30. Wey li me wê rojê,
489. 30. Woe to us on that day,

490. Pêletîyê bi dojê,
490. Surging with hell,

491. Şivêvê gele camêr, cênîkê gele hurmet bigrin bavêne agirê dojê.
491. They will seize the mustaches of many gentlemen, the braids of many respectable women and throw them into the fire of hell.

492. Erhemdûlla her ya Rebî, her ya Rebî, her ya Xuda,
492. Praise be to God, always O Lord, always O Lord, always O God,

493. We hêmeta seydê me bî, yala ferdost e, werê me bî.
493. May that be the grace of our hunt, O unique friend, come to us.

494. ## BEYTA BEHZA-II
494. ## BEYT OF BEHZ-II

495. 1. Meste sêkranê,
495. 1. I am intoxicated, drunk,

496. Delavanê giranê.
496. Of the heavy bounty.

497. 2. Nêçîrvanê behza me,
497. 2. I am the hunter of falcons,

498. Derê tirbê ra tême,
498. I come along the path of the grave,

499. Rênga behza dûr dipême.
499. I measure the colors of the far falcons.

500. 3. Dehfa min e mî ye,
500. 3. My snare is of hair,

501. Derê tirbê raxistîye,
501. It is spread by the door of the grave,

502. Behzîngê hatibû tê nivistîye.
502. A falcon had come and settled in it.

503. Dilê mi şa bû,
503. My heart was glad.

504. Mala mi ava bû,
504. My house was built up.

505. Mi girtîbî, mi berdabî.
505. I had caught it, I had let it go.

506. 5. Çi behzîkî mezin e,
506. 5. What a great falcon,

507. Ketibû dehfa min e.
507. It had fallen into my snare.

508. Dilê mi şabû, mala mi ava bû,
508. My heart was glad, my house was built up,

509. Behzi firîn, mi nizanbû surra melek Şîxisn e.
509. The falcons flew, I did not know it is the secret of the angel Şîxisn.

510. 6. Çi behzîkî qewî ye,
510. 6. What a strong falcon,

511. Mi dehfa xwe dîye.
511. I saw my snare.

512. 12. Meha tebaxê sala 1975an li bajarê Tibilîsîyê ji zarê pîr Dodoê Xidirî hatîye nivisin.
512. 12. In the month of August of the year 1975 in the city of Tbilisi it was written down from the mouth of pîr Dodo son of Xidir.

513. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".
513. It was printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

514. Cildê I., Yêrêvan, r. 343-344
514. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 343-344.

515. 13. Mû.
515. 13. Hair.

516. Dilê mi şabû, mala mi ava bû,
516. My heart was glad, my house was built up.

517. Behzî firîn, mi nizanbû surra sultan Êzîd e.
517. The falcons flew, I did not know it is the secret of Siltan Êzîd.

518. 7. Çi behzîkî bikur,
518. 7. What a deep-seeing falcon,

519. Dinê deher bibû dikir.
519. It was passing through the world.

520. Dilê mi şa bû, mala mi ava bû,
520. My heart was glad, my house was built up,

521. Behzî firîn, mi nizanbû surra Şêxûbekir.
521. The falcons flew, I did not know it is the secret of Şêxûbekir.

522. 8. Behz hatin, behz bihurîn,
522. 8. Falcons came, falcons passed,

523. Dilê mi şa bû, mala mi ava bû,
523. My heart was glad, my house was built up,

524. Çevê mi pê ket, dil kewgirî,
524. My eyes fell upon it, the heart wept,

525. Xwazka hevalê behza dikirî.
525. Would that I acted as a companion of falcons.

526. 9. Behz hatin, behz diçûne,
526. 9. Falcons came, falcons were going,

527. Dilê mi şa bû, mala mi ava bû,
527. My heart was glad, my house was built up,

528. Çevê mi pê ket, dil bi dû ne,
528. My eyes fell upon it, the heart is behind them,

529. Xwezka hevalê behza dikeme.
529. Would that I became a companion of falcons.

530. 10. Şeref e lawê pîra,
530. 10. It is the honor of the sons of the pîrs,

531. Dil sotibûn eşqera wî da,
531. Hearts had burned in his open love,

532. Berbanga sibê şeref digere nêçîrê feqîra.
532. At the dawn of morning honor roams the hunt of the poor.

533. ## BEYTA BILBIL MISKINO
533. ## BEYT OF BILBIL MISKINO

534. Sibhan ji te sibhana, Çi hukmekî giran e, De em ê bidin methê bilbilê teyran e.
534. Glory to you, O Glory, what a heavy judgment it is, now we will give praise to the nightingale of the birds.

535. 2. Çiqas teyr lêk ce'm hatibûn,
535. 2. How many birds had gathered together,

536. Ser rehekî rawastîyabûn,
536. They had stood upon one path,

537. Belê, benda bilbilê miskin dama bûn.
537. Indeed, they were waiting for the poor nightingale.

538. 3. "Ya miro, xêr bêt bihar e,
538. 3. "O prince, let spring come with good,

539. Bilbil rojê dibêt hezar e,
539. The nightingale by day speaks a thousand,

540. Belê şevêd giran dixûne defter ji defterê mehr e.
540. Indeed in the heavy nights it reads register upon register of dowry.

541. 4. Ya miro, bihar xêr bêt,
541. 4. O prince, let spring come with good,

542. Bilbil rojê hin divêt,
542. The nightingale by day desires some,

543. Belê şevêd giran dengê xwe distirêt."
543. Indeed in the heavy nights it sings its voice."

544. 5. Silêman pêxamber go: "Ew teyrê hoyî pir gotin e,
544. 5. Prophet Solomon said: "That bird of so many words,

545. Yeqin hún bizanbin, ew jî ne ber hukmê mora min e."
545. Know for certain, it too is not under the command of my seal."

546. 14. Meha sibatê, sala 1975an li bajarê Tibilîsîyê ji zarê Ardaş Arabovî hatîye nivisin.
546. 14. In the month of February, in the year 1975 in the city of Tbilisi it was written down from the mouth of Ardaş Arabov.

547. Beyta Bilbil Miskinoyê Ardaş salên 1922-1924an ji qewal Huseynî, qewal Eylaz, qewal Xelîlî hîn bûye, yên ji berîyê hatibûn û li gundê Poştê ser nehîyeya Axbarané (niha Aragasa Ermanistanê) diman.
547. Ardaş learned the Beyt of Bilbil Miskino in the years 1922-1924 from qewal Huseyn, qewal Eylaz, and qewal Xelîl, who had come from the desert and lived in the village of Poşt in the district of Axbaran (now Aragas of Armenia).

548. Qewal Xelîl di mala bavê Ardaşî da miriye.
548. Qewal Xelîl died in the house of Ardaş's father.

549. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".
549. It was printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

550. Cildê I., Yêrêvan, 1.458-461.
550. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 458-461.

551. Şaxeka vi qewli: "Beyta Bilbilî û Silêman Pêxember" çap bûye li kovara "Laliş"ė, Num. 4, 1994, r. 60-62.
551. A variant of this qewl: "The Beyt of the Nightingale and Prophet Solomon" was printed in the journal "Laliş", No. 4, 1994, pp. 60-62.

552. 24 sebeqe ne.
552. It consists of 24 stanzas.

553. Nivîsîye Mişûr Şemoyî.
553. Mişûr Şemo wrote it.

554. Wergêra vi qewlî li ser zimanê erebî Bedel Feqîr Hecî li kovara "Bizav"ê çap kirîye.
554. The translation of this qewl into the Arabic language was printed by Bedel Feqîr Hecî in the journal "Bizav".

555. 1. Silêman-pêxamber go: "Ew teyrê hoyî axî ye,
555. 1. Prophet Solomon said: "That bird is of the earth,

556. Xazila min bizanbîya cî-wetenê bilbilê miskin, ku dibîye?"
556. Would that I knew the place and homeland of the poor nightingale, where is it?"

557. 7. Wa dibêje qomsîyê teyran e:
557. 7. Thus speaks the talkative one of the birds:

558. "Ya mîro, ew erdê bilbilê miskîn lê kirîye mikan e,
558. "O prince, that land where the poor nightingale has made its place,

559. Wê li ada hevt behra, nav baxê gulan e."
559. It is on the island of the seven seas, amidst the garden of roses."

560. 8. Silêman-pêxamber wa dikire ferman e,
560. 8. Prophet Solomon thus gave the command,

561. Ji teyra, bazî dijar e,
561. From among the birds, the fierce falcon,

562. Kir qasid pey bilbilê miskîn dinare.
562. He made a messenger and sends it after the poor nightingale.

563. "Bazio, here bilbil bîne, Tek ruhê şîrin jê nestîne, Belê saxî bigre ji min ra bîne."
563. "O falcon, go and bring the nightingale, only do not take its sweet soul from it, indeed catch it alive and bring it to me."

564. 10. Bazi wa difirî,
564. 10. The falcon flew thus,

565. Welat ber welat digerî,
565. It roamed country after country,

566. Cî-wetenê bilbilê miskîn dipirsî.
566. Asking of the place and homeland of the poor nightingale.

567. 11. Bazi firîbû çûbû pişt av e,
567. 11. The falcon had flown and gone beyond the water,

568. Welat ber welat dîtibû her du çeve,
568. With both eyes it had seen country after country,

569. Dît baxê gula da bilbilê miskînî nav e.
569. It saw in the garden of roses the poor nightingale is inside.

570. 12. Bazi firîbû çûbû cîêd bestî,
570. 12. The falcon had flown and gone to the places of the plains,

571. Dît baxê gula da bilbilê miskîn text danî, sorgul ser ra dişkestî,
571. It saw in the garden of roses the poor nightingale had set its throne, a red rose breaking over it,

572. 15. Qomsi: Ji bo kesê pirxeber, kesê laqirdîyan dike dibêjin.
572. 15. Qomsi: It is said for a very talkative person, a person who jokes.

573. 16. Dijwar e.
573. 16. Dijwar e.

574. Dijmare (bnb).
574. Dijmare (bnb).

575. 17. Dinare: Hinartin.
575. 17. Dinare: To send.

576. Dihinare.
576. He sends.

577. We li nav baxê gula da nivistî.
577. Thus it slept amidst the garden of roses.

578. 13. Bazi firîbû çûbû cîêd xalî,
578. 13. The falcon had flown and gone to empty places,

579. Dît baxed gula da bilbilê miskîn text danî, sorgul ser ra dipalî,
579. It saw in the garden of roses the poor nightingale had set its throne, leaning upon the red rose,

580. Wê li nav baxê gula da dine'lî.
580. It was wailing amidst the garden of roses.

581. 14. Bazi go: "Bilbilo, hey bilbilo,
581. 14. The falcon said: "O nightingale, hey nightingale,

582. Heyrano, soti dil o,
582. O wondrous one, burned heart,

583. Tê li nav baxê gula da hizretîya te çima gul o?"
583. Why amidst the garden of roses is your longing for the rose?"

584. 15. Bazi go: "Bilbilê dil dewrêşo,
584. 15. The falcon said: "O nightingale of dervish heart,

585. Min xeta te anîye pêş o,
585. I have brought your letter forward,

586. Belê Silêman pêxember te dike tewtêş o."
586. Indeed Prophet Solomon is investigating you."

587. 16. Bazi "Bilbilê dil şerqio, go:
587. 16. The falcon said: "O nightingale of eastern heart,

588. Pey te bûye hizêz û gazî o,
588. After you there has been shaking and calling,

589. Belê Silêman pêxember te dixazîo."
589. Indeed Prophet Solomon asks for you."

590. 17. Bilbil Go: "Ez wî kim rehmanî,
590. 17. The nightingale said: "I make him merciful,

591. Ruhê şîrin ji qalibî bikşînî gi[y]anî,
591. Even if he pulls the sweet soul from the body and spirit,

592. Belê, naême diwana mîr Silêmanî."
592. Indeed, I will not come to the court of prince Solomon."

593. 18. Bazi go: "Bilbilo, bese bike van gefa,
593. 18. The falcon said: "O nightingale, enough of these threats,

594. Tu ne teyrekî ji hemû refa,
594. You are not a bird from all the flocks,

595. Ez ê te bigrim her du kefa,
595. I will catch you in both hands,

596. Hésir bikim ji welat û terefa."
596. I will make you a captive from country and region."

597. 19. Bilbil gel baê didet xeber e,
597. 19. The nightingale gives word to the wind,

598. Bilbil gel baê didet xeber e:
598. The nightingale gives word to the wind:

599. 20. "Bao, amanet, sed amanet,
599. 20. "O wind, a trust, a hundred trusts,

600. Amanet heye taqet,
600. A trust as long as there is strength,

601. Ew gula ez lê dibûm hizret,
601. That rose for which I was longing,

602. Bira paşî min gul nav bax da nebişkivtin qet bi qet."
602. May the rose never, never blossom in the garden after me."

603. 21. Bilbil teyrekî namûs e,
603. 21. The nightingale is a bird of honor,

604. Ji teyra ketibû kapûs e,
604. From among the birds it had fallen into a nightmare,

605. Bilbil firîbû çûbû hindirîsî Taûs e,
605. The nightingale had flown and gone into the presence of the Peacock,

606. 22. Gava diçû nav e,
606. 22. When it went inside,

607. Hemûşka ron dibû dil û çev e.
607. The heart and eyes of all became bright.

608. 23. Silêman-pêxember go: "Hûn binêrin bilbil û rengî,
608. 23. Prophet Solomon said: "Look at the nightingale and its color,

609. Şirin û şîrin hiltîne dengî,"
609. Sweetly, sweetly it raises its voice,"

610. Bilbilê miskîn go: "Miro, bixûne bira xenîmê min bêne çengî."
610. The poor nightingale said: "O prince, call out, let my enemies be brought to the claw."

611. 24. Silêman pêxember go: “Hûn binêrin bilbil û xeberdanê."
611. 24. Prophet Solomon said: "Look at the nightingale and its speaking."

612. Silêman pêxember teyr xandibû dîwanê,
612. Prophet Solomon had called the birds to the court,

613. Bilbilê miskin go: "Miro, xenîmê min kanê?"
613. The poor nightingale said: "O prince, where is my enemy?"

614. 25. Wa dibêje tot e:
614. 25. Thus speaks the parrot:

615. "Ya miro, heçê mêra û meleka birîn û sote,
615. "O prince, whoever of men and angels is wounded and burned,

616. Belê şevêd giran xew pêşê gaê cot e."
616. Indeed in the heavy nights sleep is the work of the plow ox."

617. 18. Xew pîşeyê gayê cot e, ango karê wî ye.
617. 18. Sleep is the profession of the plow ox, that is to say its work.

618. 26. Wa dibêje totak e:
618. 26. Thus speaks the little parrot:

619. "Ya miro, heçê mêra û meleka sotibû mêlak e,
619. "O prince, whoever of men and angels had their liver burned,

620. Belê şevêd giran xewê nake."
620. Indeed in the heavy nights does not sleep."

621. 27. Wa dibêje hendelîb e:
621. 27. Thus speaks the nightingale:

622. "Ya miro, heçê ragirt dilêt xerîb e,
622. "O prince, whoever has endured an exiled heart,

623. Bahişta baqin par tê hebet nesîb e."
623. An eternal paradise will surely be their portion."

624. 28. Wa dibêje şalul e:
624. 28. Thus speaks the blackbird:

625. "Ya miro, bilbil teyrekî nûr e,
625. "O prince, the nightingale is a bird of light,

626. Xelat bike, bide destûr e."
626. Reward it, give it permission to leave."

627. 29. Silêman-pêxember bilbil xelat dikir, dida destûre,
627. 29. Prophet Solomon was rewarding the nightingale, giving it permission to leave,

628. Ji gula ketibûn gulê sor û zer e.
628. From the roses they had fallen into the red and yellow rose.

629. 30. Gulê sor û zer baxa dibişkivtîn,
629. 30. The red and yellow roses were blossoming in the gardens,

630. Xweşî hatin, tehlî nixivtîn,
630. Gladness came, bitterness was covered over,

631. Birînê bilbilê miskîn kûr bûn serî hildan, nû axivtîn.
631. The wounds of the poor nightingale became deep, rose up, and spoke anew.

632. 31. Bilbil teyrê dewletê,
632. 31. The nightingale is the bird of fortune,

633. Xeriqîbû behra muhbetê,
633. It was drowned in the sea of love,

634. Sed rehmet dê û bavê hosta û cime'tê.
634. A hundred mercies upon the mother and father of the master and the assembly.

635. 19. Bihuşta baqi (bnb).
635. 19. Eternal paradise (bnb).

636. ## Bervedan
636. ## Comparison

637. Beyta Bilbil Miskino, poemeka sûfîtê ya naskirî ye.
637. The Beyt of Bilbil Miskino is a well-known Sufi poem.

638. Di edebîyata farisan a sûfîtîyê da cihê xwe girtîye.
638. It has taken its place in the Sufi literature of the Persians.

639. Xudanê vê nivîsarê hozanê farisan ê mîstîk Ettar e [Farid al-Din Muhamed B. Ibrahim Ettar].
639. The author of this text is the Persian mystic poet Attar [Farid al-Din Muhammad b. Ibrahim Attar].

640. Ettar sala 513 H.1119an ji dayik bûye û li sala 627 H. 1230an li bajarê Nîşabûrê bi destê monxolan hatîye kuştin.
640. Attar was born in the year 513 A.H. / 1119 A.D. and in the year 627 A.H. / 1230 A.D. in the city of Nishapur was killed at the hands of the Mongols.

641. Li ser sala mirina wî dîtinên cuda û ne wekî hev hene.
641. Concerning the year of his death there are different and varied views.

642. Bandora Ettarî mezin e li ser belavbûna bîr û bawerîya sûfîzmê li nava gelên Rojhilata Nêzîk û Navîn.
642. Attar's influence is great upon the spread of the thought and belief of Sufism among the peoples of the Near and Middle East.

643. Dibêjin ew kalê zemana Ettar xudanê pênc sed zêdetir nivîsar û poeman bûye.
643. They say that old man of his time, Attar, was the author of more than five hundred texts and poems.

644. Wî li ser jîyana mêrên xas û bihurtî, derwêş û sûfîyên binavûdeng çîrok û efsane civandine, kirine bingeha nivîsarên xwe.
644. He gathered stories and legends concerning the lives of pure and passed holy men, renowned dervishes and Sufis, making them the foundation of his writings.

645. Ji nivîsarên wî yên ku ji alîyê zanyaran hatine naskirin ev in: Mantik el-Tayr, Maqamat el-Tuyûr, Muxtâr-Nâma, Musîbet-name, Dîwan, Îlahî-name, Esrar-name, Xusrew-name, Pend-name, Bulbul-name, Tedqîret el-ewlîya, Mîrac-name, Uştur-name, Cewer el-Zat, Bîser-name û yên mayîn.
645. Among his writings that have been recognized by scholars are these: Mantik al-Tayr, Maqamat al-Tuyur, Mukhtar-Nama, Musibat-name, Diwan, Ilahi-name, Asrar-name, Khusraw-name, Pand-name, Bulbul-name, Tadhkirat al-Awliya, Miraj-name, Ushtur-name, Jawahir al-Zat, Bisar-name and the rest.

646. Beyta Bilbil Miskînoyê, şaxeka ji nivîsara Bulbul-nameya Ettar e bi zimanê kurdî.
646. The Beyt of Bilbil Miskino is a variant of the text of Attar's Bulbul-name in the Kurdish language.

647. Naveroka poema Ettarî, ku Y.E. Bertels di pirtûka xwe da dide, ev e: hemû teyr û tû, yên di bin bandora Silêman pêxemberî da bûn, rojekê dicivin cem wî û xeyba bilbilî li ber dikin, wekî ew bûye evîndarê bax û bostanan, bi kar û kirên xirab ve mijûl e.
647. The content of Attar's poem, which Y.E. Bertels gives in his book, is this: all the birds, who were under the influence of Prophet Solomon, one day gather near him and speak ill of the nightingale before him, that it has become the lover of gardens and orchards, and is occupied with bad deeds and actions.

648. Ew yekî pozbilind e, dengê wî ji hemîyan bilindtir e û her ji bona gulê distrê.
648. It is an arrogant one, its voice is higher than all others and it always sings only for the rose.

649. Silêman pêxember teyrê bazî dişîne pey û bi destê zorê dê wî bîne dîwanê.
649. Prophet Solomon sends the falcon bird after it to bring it to the court by force.

650. Bilbil mecbur e bax û baxçê rengîn bihêle, destê xwe ji gulê bibire here dîwana Silêman pêxemberî.
650. The nightingale is compelled to leave the colorful garden and orchard, to cut its hand from the rose and go to Prophet Solomon's court.

651. Îcar bilbil xatirê xwe ji gula evînê dixwaze.
651. Then the nightingale bids farewell to the rose of love.

652. Dema li hewayê dikevin bilbil silav û temînên xwe bi bayî ra dişîne ji gulê ra, ku ew di evîna xwe da helal û herher bimîne.
652. When they take to the air the nightingale sends its greetings and assurances with the wind to the rose, that it may remain pure and eternal in its love.

653. Di baxçê Silêman pêxember da bilbil miskînî û evîndarîya xwe dîyar dike û axaftina wê ji bona parastina heqîya xwe hemû teyran, yên li dijî wî bûne bi dilê pêxemberî tê û destûra wî dide vegere baxê xwe, cem gula xemgîn."
653. In the orchard of Prophet Solomon the nightingale expresses its wretchedness and its love and its speech for the defense of its rightness against all the birds who were opposed to it pleases the heart of the prophet, and he gives it permission to return to its garden, near the sorrowful rose."

654. 20. Encyklopaedia Islam, new Edition, vol. I, 1.752.
654. 20. Encyclopaedia of Islam, New Edition, vol. I, p. 752.

655. Di poema xwe da Ettar, çend çîrok û serpêhatî jî bi devê bilbilî dinivise.
655. In his poem Attar also writes a few stories and adventures through the mouth of the nightingale.

656. Wekî em dibînin bi giştî poema Ettarî û beyta êzdîyan bi naveroka xwe wekî hev in.
656. As we see, in general Attar's poem and the Yezidis' beyt are the same in their content.

657. Helbet şaxê ku gihîştîye destê me hinek bend jê kûvî bûne, beyt kêmsebeqe bûne.
657. Of course, from the variant that has reached our hands some stanzas have gone wild (been lost), the beyt has become reduced in stanzas.

658. Lê bê şik e, ku ev her du nivîsar ji bingeha wan yek e.
658. But it is without doubt that these two texts are one in their foundation.

659. Beyta Bilbil Miskîno, careka din dide isbatkirin pêwendîya edebiyata her du gelan, kurd û farisan di sedsalîyên navîn da, kamilbûna fena poezîya kurdî berî ku navên klasîkên kurdan Feqîyê Teyran, Melayê Cizîrî, Ehmedê Xanî û yên mayîn bêne ser esmana çand û edebiyata kurdan.
659. The Beyt of Bilbil Miskino once again proves the connection of the literature of the two peoples, Kurds and Persians, in the Middle Ages, the perfection of the art of Kurdish poetry before the names of the Kurdish classics Feqîyê Teyran, Melayê Cizîrî, Ehmedê Xanî and the rest came into the sky of Kurdish culture and literature.

660. Bilbil wekî sifeta evîndarîyê, helalî û rindîyê di edebîyata Rojhilatê da gelek caran, hîn ji dema kevn ve hatîye bikaranîn.
660. The nightingale as an attribute of love, purity and beauty has been used many times in Eastern literature, even since ancient times.

661. Di edebîyata sufiyan da jî ev tradisyon hatîye parastin.
661. In Sufi literature too this tradition has been preserved.

662. Evîn, helalî û bi giştî xwe-pêşkêşkirina hezkirîya xwe, motîfeka bingehîn bûye ji bona sufiyan.
662. Love, purity and in general the self-presentation of one's beloved has been a fundamental motif for the Sufis.

663. Evîna mezin li hemberî Xwedê bi gelek formên nihênî û alegorî di nava qewl û beytên êzdîyan da jî tê ber çavan.
663. The great love toward God comes before the eyes in many hidden and allegorical forms within the qewls and beyts of the Yezidis as well.

664. Beyta Bilbil Miskînoyê mînakek e ji vê evîna mezin ra.
664. The Beyt of Bilbil Miskino is an example for this great love.

665. Ji bona evînê kesên navber û navçê ne gerek in.
665. For love, intermediaries and mediators are not necessary.

666. Dewrêş û sûfî divê jiyana xwe bi ibadetê, di miskînîyê û azarê da derbas bikin, ku hêjayî evîna mezin bin.
666. The dervish and the Sufi must spend their lives in worship, in wretchedness and suffering, so that they may be worthy of the great love.

667. Bilbil di vê poemê da, wekî Bertelsî dide xuyakirin, Ettar bi xwe ye," sûfîkî şikestî ye ku li hemberî gelek hozanên jixwerazî û têrxwarî, helbestvanên dîwana mîr û hakiman, hozanên xwepesindar derketiye.
667. The nightingale in this poem, as Bertels reveals, is Attar himself, a broken Sufi who came out against many self-satisfied and over-fed bards, the poets of the court of princes and rulers, the self-praising bards.

668. Ewana hemû ew teyr û tûyên geveze ne ku xeyba wî li ber Silêman pêxemberî kirine.
668. They are all those babbling birds who spoke ill of him before Prophet Solomon.

669. Armanca poemê ew e, ku heqî û rastî, dawîya dawî bi ser dikeve.
669. The aim of the poem is that rightness and truth, in the very end, triumph.

670. 21. Bertels, Y. E., Suffizm i sufisskaja literatura, r. 343-353.
670. 21. Bertels, Y. E., Sufism and Sufi Literature, pp. 343-353.

671. 22. Her li wê, r. 342.
671. 22. Ibid., p. 342.

672. ## BEYTA DEWRÊŞ ADEM
672. ## BEYT OF DERVISH ADEM

673. 1. Çi subekê neder e,
673. 1. What a rare morning,

674. Nava xasa dibe xeber e,
674. Word spreads among the saints,

675. Dewrêş Adem wê here sefer e.
675. Dervish Adem will go on a journey.

676. 2. Çi subekê nîşan e,
676. 2. What a manifest morning,

677. Nava xasê dîwana Şîx Adî wê bive beyan e,
677. Among the saints of Şîx Adî's court it will be declared,

678. Dewrêş Adem wê here Xurêsan e.
678. Dervish Adem will go to Khorasan.

679. 3. Wey derwêşê min î delîl e,
679. 3. Oh my guided dervish,

680. Bê qal e û bê qîl e,
680. He is without word and without talk,

681. Rûniştîye ser rîya xêran û sexîl e.
681. He has sat upon the road of good deeds and charity.

682. 4. Mîrê Xurêsanê wa dibêye:
682. 4. The Prince of Khorasan says thus:

683. "Qasid, here binhêre ew çi dewrêşe wê ye,
683. "Messenger, go and look what dervish is there,

684. Ew dewrêşî çi dibêye?"
684. What is that dervish saying?"

685. 5. Qaside diçûye, dewrêş pirsîye:
685. 5. The messenger was going, he asked the dervish:

686. “Derwêş baba, nesîheta te wan erda çi ye?”
686. "Father dervish, what is your counsel in those lands?"

687. Ey dewrêş wa dibêye:
687. O dervish speaks thus:

688. "Qasid, fermaneke hatye ji Xwedê ye,
688. "Messenger, a command has come from God,

689. Derwêş dota mîrê we dibêye."
689. The dervish speaks for the daughter of your prince."

690. 23. Meha tebaxa sala 1975an li bajarê Tibilîsîyê ji zarê Tefûrê Şêx Mehmûd hatîye nivîsîn.
690. 23. In the month of August of the year 1975 in the city of Tbilisi it was written down from the mouth of Tefûr son of Şêx Mehmûd.

691. Çap bûye: Li Zargotina kurda.
691. Printed: In Folklore of the Kurds.

692. Cildê I., Yêrêvan, r. 307 - 311.
692. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 307 - 311.

693. 24. Xoristan (bnb).
693. 24. Khoristan (bnb).

694. 25. sebîl e (bnb).
694. 25. sebîl e (bnb).

695. 26. ew (bnb).
695. 26. ew (bnb).

696. 6. Qasidê min î jîr e,
696. 6. My clever messenger,

697. Divêje dewrêşê delîl e:
697. Says to the guided dervish:

698. "Derwêş, te çî ye ji dota mîr e?"
698. "Dervish, what is your business with the prince's daughter?"

699. 7. Qasidê vedigerîye,
699. 7. The messenger returns,

700. Mîr jê pirsîye:
700. The prince asked him:

701. "Qasid tu hatî, derwêş çima mabû cî ye?"
701. "Messenger you have come, why did the dervish remain in his place?"

702. 8. Qasidê min î zer e,
702. 8. My golden messenger,

703. Dibê: "Çi dewrêşekî xweyî ser e,
703. Says: "What a commanding dervish,

704. Ez caba dewrêş nikarim bikim der e."
704. I cannot deliver the answer of the dervish outside."

705. 9. Ey qasid wa dibêye:
705. 9. O messenger speaks thus:

706. "Mîrê min, dewrêş dibê fermanek hatye boy Xwedê ye,
706. "My prince, the dervish says a command has come from God,

707. Ez dota mîrê we dibêye."
707. I speak for the daughter of your prince."

708. 10. Mîrê min wê xeberê mabû dilmaî,
708. 10. My prince was offended at that word,

709. Fericîbû hukumê padşaî,
709. He was amazed at the command of the king,

710. Go: "Binêrin derwêşê cemlaî."
710. He said: "Look at the gathering dervish."

711. 11. Wê hebû xelqê merîfetî Yasîn e:
711. 11. There was a people of the gnosis of Yasin:

712. "Mîrê min, bişîne dewrêş bîne,
712. "My prince, send for and bring the dervish,

713. Çika aqil e, yanê sewdênî ye?"
713. Is he wise, or is he crazy?"

714. 12. Mîr dişand dewrêş dihate,
714. 12. The prince sent and the dervish came,

715. Derwêş rê va diaxavte,
715. The dervish spoke along the way,

716. 12. 42
716. 12. 42

717. Mîr go: "Derwêş baba, tê qelena keça min çi bikî xevat e?"
717. The prince said: "Father dervish, what will you work for my daughter's bride price?"

718. 13. Ey dewrêş wa dibêye:
718. 13. O dervish speaks thus:

719. "Mîrê min, çiqa zêra dixazî te ra bînim dinê ye,
719. "My prince, however much gold you want, I will bring it for you from the world,

720. Çiqa cewahira dixazî te ra bînim ji behrê ye."
720. However many jewels you want, I will bring them for you from the sea."

721. 14. Wey dewrêşê minî jîr e,
721. 14. Oh my clever dervish,

722. Tu dewrêş bîne, bawarî yêqîn e,
722. Bring the dervish, belief is certain,

723. Çiqa cewahira dixazî ji te ra bînim behra ezmî n
723. However many jewels you want, I will bring them for you from the sea of the sky

724. e.
724. .

725. 15. Wey dewrêşê min î xas e,
725. 15. Oh my pure dervish,

726. Vedixar kas e,
726. He drank from the cup,

727. Qest kir, çû dîwana Xidir Nebî, Xidir Eylas e.
727. He set out, went to the court of Xidir Nebî, Xidir Eylas.

728. 16. Derwêş divê, "Xidiro, tu heqder î,
728. 16. The dervish says, "O Xidir, you are the rightful owner,

729. Hêmeta qadir î,
729. You are the power of the mighty,

730. Tu ber vî dergeî hedir î."
730. You are present before this gate."

731. 17. Derwêş dibê: "Xidiro, here mi ra durra bîne,
731. 17. The dervish says: "O Xidir, go and bring me the pearl,

732. Pêşma dara xasa va dayne,
732. Set it before the tree of the saints,

733. Tê roja qiyametê herî serê Kela Xurêsanî daynî."
733. You will go on the day of resurrection and set it upon the fortress of Khorasan."

734. 18. Xidirê min î sêfîl î sergerdan e,
734. 18. My wretched and wandering Xidir,

735. Qest kir behra bêbinyan e.
735. He set out for the bottomless sea.

736. 27. Tu yê.
736. 27. You will.

737. 28. hadêrî (bnb).
737. 28. hadêrî (bnb).

738. 19. Xidirê wa dike gazî:
738. 19. Xidir calls out thus:

739. "Heçî xuleqetê behrê, serê xwe bikin hewrazî,
739. "Whatever creations of the sea, raise your heads upwards,

740. Derwêş Adem durra we dixazî."
740. Dervish Adem asks for your pearl."

741. 20. Heçî xuleqetê wê ye,
741. 20. Whatever creations of it there are,

742. Qest kirin çûne behrê ye,
742. They set out and went to the sea,

743. Hatin, her yek durrek lê ye.
743. They came, each had a pearl on them.

744. 21. Wey dewrêşê min î bav durr e,
744. 21. Oh my dervish of the pearl father,

745. Wan durra hildabû sê durr e,
745. He had picked up those pearls, three pearls,

746. Danî destê mîrê Xurêsanî bi surr e.
746. He placed them in the hand of the prince of Khorasan with the secret.

747. 22. Mîr go: "Werin binêrin vê ecêbê,
747. 22. The prince said: "Come and look at this wonder,

748. Mêşê girtîye defterê û kitêbê,
748. The fly has taken hold of the register and the book,

749. Xebera gel dewrêş girte lêvê."
749. It held the word with the dervish on the lip."

750. 23. Wey mîrê minî xudan qirar e,
750. 23. Oh my prince of decisions,

751. Destê keça xwe girt dewrêş va hinare,
751. He took the hand of his daughter and sent her to the dervish,

752. Keça xwe dewrêş ra kire mar e.
752. He married his daughter to the dervish.

753. 24. Wey dewrêşê min î jar e,
753. 24. Oh my poor dervish,

754. Firî nolanî teyar e,
754. He flew like a bird,

755. Qesrê pencerê ra hatibû xar e,
755. He had come down from the window of the palace,

756. Hine xerqê xwe keçê va spare.
756. He entrusted some of his cloak to the girl.

757. 25. Dabû keçê xerqe ye,
757. 25. He had given the girl the cloak,

758. 29. xulyaqet (bnb).
758. 29. xulyaqet (bnb).

759. Go: "Xilmeta we kirîye layiqî we ye, Ez diçim, pêy mi va silavê bike bavê xwe ye.
759. He said: "Your service you have done is worthy of you, I am going, after me give greetings to your father."

760. 26. Pêj mi va silavê bike bavê ye,
760. 26. After me give greetings to the father,

761. Herge ewledek paş mi dibêye,
761. If a child is born after me,

762. Bira nesekine lê xe bêye."
762. Let it not wait, let it set out and come."

763. 27. Wê heye xelqê merîfetî jîr e,
763. 27. There is a clever people of gnosis,

764. Pev ketin çûne ba mîr e,
764. They clashed and went to the prince,

765. Divê: "Mîr, ka dewrêşê me yî xudan nedîr e?"
765. They say: "Prince, where is our dervish, the lord of the rare?"

766. 28. Mîr wê diçûye,
766. 28. The prince was going there,

767. Keçê pirsîye:
767. He asked the girl:

768. "Lao, ka dewrêşê me yî xudan ewlîye?"
768. "Child, where is our dervish, the lord of saints?"

769. 29. Keçê dibê: "Bavo, wey li qewla, wey li qirara,
769. 29. The girl says: "Father, alas for the promise, alas for the decision,

770. Dewrêş qesrê pencerê da hate xar e,
770. The dervish came down from the window of the palace,

771. Kete nava kezîyan û guhar e,
771. He fell amidst the braids and earrings,

772. Hine xerqê xwe mi va spare.
772. He entrusted some of his cloak to me.

773. 30. Dabû mi xerqe ye,
773. 30. He gave me the cloak,

774. Go, xilmeta we kirî layiqî we ye,
774. He said, your service you have done is worthy of you,

775. Ez diçim, pêş mi va silavê bike bavê ye.
775. I am going, give greetings from me to the father.

776. 31. Pêş mi va silavê bike bavê xwe ye,
776. 31. Give greetings from me to your father,

777. Herge paşî min ewlek dibêye,
777. If a child is born after me,

778. Bira nesekine lê xe bêye."
778. Let it not wait, let it set out and come."

779. 30. Xizmet.
779. 30. Service.

780. 32. Dibe, neh meh hatin buhurîn,
780. 32. It happens, nine months passed by,

781. Mîr Birahîmê Ademî li wê nixtê xuliqî,
781. Mîr Birahîm son of Adem was created from that drop,

782. Hemûşka lê anî bawarî û yêqînî.
782. Everyone brought belief and certainty to him.

783. 33. Wey dewrêşê minî çê ye,
783. 33. Oh my good dervish,

784. Sevê, rojê seyrê ye,
784. Night and day he is on a journey,

785. Çima tu nizanî, bavê te feqîr e, xerqê Şîx Adî lê ye.
785. Why do you not know, your father is poor, the cloak of Şîx Adî is upon him.

786. ## BEYTA GILAVÎYÊ
786. ## BEYT OF GILAVÎ

787. 1. Hatye qasidê çîyan e,
787. 1. The messenger of the mountains has come,

788. Were em ê bikin xeberyan e,
788. Come, we will talk together,

789. Ax li minê, seraya rê me biryane.
789. Alas for me, the palace of the path has cut us off.

790. 2. Hatye qasidê derda,
790. 2. The messenger of sorrows has come,

791. Soranîkê sore berda,
791. He released a red lament,

792. Ax li minê, reşxeteke reşe ser da.
792. Alas for me, a black letter is upon it.

793. 3. Hatye qasidê zêî,
793. 3. The messenger of the river has come,

794. Reşxeteke reşe lê î,
794. A black letter is upon him,

795. Ax li minê, navê Gilavîya min e lê î.
795. Alas for me, the name of my Gilavî is upon it.

796. 4. Ez ê wê reşxetê dixûnim,
796. 4. I will read that black letter,

797. Qe tî pak tê navînim,
797. I see nothing pure in it at all,

798. Davêjim, berê xwe didime, pişta xwe lê vedigerînim.
798. I throw it away, I turn my face, I turn my back on it.

799. 31. Meha îlona sala 1976an li gundê Tsaraşatê yê li ser nehîyeya Hoktêmbêryana Ermenistanê ji zarê Seyrana Şêx Keleşî hatîye nivîsîn.
799. 31. In the month of September of the year 1976 in the village of Tsaraşat in the Hoktemberyan district of Armenia it was written down from the mouth of Seyran daughter of Şêx Keleş.

800. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".
800. It was printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

801. Cildê I., Yêrêvan, r. 400-403.
801. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 400-403.

802. Eva beyta H.Temoyan bi wergera ser zimanê ermenî çap kirîye û ne gotîye ji ku hildaye.
802. H. Temoyan has printed this beyt with a translation into the Armenian language and did not say where he took it from.

803. Binêre: H. Temoyan, Tekstên ola êzdîya.
803. See: H. Temoyan, Texts of the Yezidi religion.

804. Yêrêvan 2000, r. 52-59.
804. Yerevan 2000, pp. 52-59.

805. 32. Mîr Etlas pêşîyê mala mîrê şêxa di Şengalê çû bû eskerîyê çawa [wekî] qomender.
805. 32. Mîr Etlas, formerly from the house of the prince of the sheikhs in Sinjar, had gone to the military as a commander.

806. Jinek, navê we Gilavî anîbû ser jina xwe ya kevin bona vê yekê jina wî zaro nedanya.
806. He had brought a woman, her name Gilavî, over his old wife because his wife had not borne a child.

807. Wextê jin anî sê roja sekinî, paşê gazî kirê, bire eskerîyê çawa [wekî] qomender.
807. When he brought the woman he stayed three days, then they called him, took him to the military as a commander.

808. Paşê birina wî jina wî ye kewin çawa [wekî] hewi jehr da jina teze, Gilavî.
808. After his taking, his old wife as a co-wife gave poison to the new wife, Gilavî.

809. Hijdeh roja ma Gilavî bi wê jehrê mir.
809. Gilavî remained for eighteen days and died from that poison.

810. Paşê elametî dane mîr Etlas wekî jina te mirîye!
810. Then they gave the sign to Mîr Etlas that your wife has died!

811. Mîr Etlas çû destûra xwe ji mezinê xwe stand, borê xwe siwar bû û ber bi mala xwe hat, go:...
811. Mîr Etlas went and took his permission from his superior, mounted his steed and came toward his house, he said:...

812. Me ev bend ji wê berhema navborî girt ku wekî şirove lê hatiye zêdekirin û naverokê ronî dike û benda piştî wê bi vê ve girêdayî ye.
812. We took this paragraph from that aforementioned work which has been added as a commentary and illuminates the content, and the paragraph after it is connected to this.

813. 5. Go: "Here, boro, eslê te î li xas,
813. 5. He said: "Go, O steed, your origin is from the pure,

814. De tu bajo qewata Xidirnebî-Xidirilyas,
814. Drive on by the power of Xidirnebî-Xidirilyas,

815. Ax li minê, tirba xerîba mi dûr va bike nas."
815. Alas for me, recognize the grave of my exile from afar."

816. Çûme hafa goristîn e,
816. I went to the edge of the graveyard,

817. Pirsekê xastyê dergewîn e,
817. I asked a question of the gatekeeper,

818. Ax, go: "Gelo, tirba xerîba kî bi kî ne?"
818. Alas, he said: "I wonder, whose grave of the exile is with whom?"

819. Çûme hafa goristanî,
819. I went to the edge of the graveyard,

820. Pirsekê kirîye dergewanî,
820. I asked a question of the gatekeeper,

821. Ax, min go: "Gelo, tirba xerîba min kîjan î?"
821. Alas, I said: "I wonder, which one is the grave of my exile?"

822. Derî tirbê li min vekir,
822. He opened the door of the grave for me,

823. Gilaviyê ax û berê sar da reng guhêrîbû, min nas nekir,
823. Gilavî had changed color in the cold earth and stone, I did not recognize her,

824. Ax li minê, Gilavîyê xeyîdî pişt min ve kir.
824. Alas for me, Gilavî angrily turned her back to me.

825. 9. Mîr go: "Qudreta yekê di xefûr e,
825. 9. The prince said: "The power of the one is forgiving,

826. Hafa tirba Gilavîya min kişîya nûr e,
826. The edge of the grave of my Gilavî has drawn light,

827. Eva yeka ne qebûl e."
827. This one thing is not accepted."

828. 10. Qudreta yekê di rehmanê,
828. 10. The power of the one is in the merciful,

829. Ruhê hatye dest û piyanê,
829. The soul has come to the hands and feet,

830. Gilavî rûniştîye mîr hewes ra dike xeverdanê.
830. Gilavî has sat up, she eagerly converses with the prince.

831. 11. Mîr go: "Gilaviyê ji Suxinê,
831. 11. The prince said: "Gilavî of Suxin,

832. Hela bêje pirsa vê gotinê,
832. Tell me the meaning of this word,

833. Hela çika çi hawalê te mirinê?"
833. What is the circumstance of your dying?"

834. 12. Mîr go: "Sed heyfa te î dêmê narî,
834. 12. The prince said: "A hundred pities for your face of fire,

835. Gerdenê morî mircan û karibarî,
835. Your neck of pearls, corals and amber,

836. Ax li minê, ew jî çûne ax û berê gorane tarî."
836. Alas for me, they too have gone into the earth and stone of dark graves."

837. 13. Mîr go: "Gilaviyê, sed heyfa te wî devî, wa dirana,
837. 13. The prince said: "Gilavî, a hundred pities for that mouth, those teeth,

838. Te wa morîya, wa mircana,
838. For you of those pearls, those corals,

839. Sed heyfa te, tu jî çûyî ax û berê goristana."
839. A hundred pities for you, you too have gone into the earth and stone of graveyards."

840. 14. Gilaviyê go: "Mîro, te ez hênare,
840. 14. Gilavî said: "Prince, you sent me,

841. Te ez nava zêr û ziv da wez dijbare,
841. You loaded me among gold and silver,

842. Te ez destê zalimeke zal va dispare,
842. You entrusted me to the hand of a cruel tyrant,

843. Ev ê zalima ber serê siva da min kase jehr e."
843. This tyrant gave me a cup of poison early in the morning."

844. 15. Go: "Hijde şevê havînê,
844. 15. She said: "Eighteen nights of summer,

845. Nexaş bûm, ketime nav nivînê,
845. I was sick, I fell into the bed,

846. Ax li minê, qe nehate ser min lêzimekî xûnê."
846. Alas for me, no blood relative came over me at all."

847. 16. Go: "Hijde şevê havînê jimar e,
847. 16. She said: "Count eighteen nights of summer,

848. Min ne xarîye, ne vexare,
848. I have neither eaten nor drank,

849. Ax, xurê xwe av û hêsira da dibhare."
849. Alas, she spends herself in water and tears."

850. 17. Mîr go: "Gilaviyê, xazil tu bihatay li kirrînê,
850. 17. The prince said: "Gilavî, would that you came to be bought,

851. Min berenberî te zêr bavîta nav mêzînê,
851. I would have thrown gold into the scale equal to you,

852. Bona di qirara vê evînê."
852. For the sake of the decision of this love."

853. 18. Gilaviyê go: "Mîro, here bira tu î xaş bî,
853. 18. Gilavî said: "Prince, go, may you be well,

854. Sorgulaneke nava baxane geş bî,
854. May you be a bright red rose amidst the gardens,

855. Bira cîyê Gilaviyê ax û fers bî."
855. Let Gilavî's place be earth and dust."

856. 19. Gilaviyê go: "Mîro, here bira tu î sax bî,
856. 19. Gilavî said: "Prince, go, may you be alive,

857. Sorgulaneke nava bax bî,
857. May you be a red rose amidst the garden,

858. Bira cîyê Gilaviyê xalî, ax bî."
858. Let Gilavî's place be empty, be earth."

859. 20. Mîr go: "Bero, li ser bera,
859. 20. The prince said: "O stone, upon the stones,

860. Tu Xwedê kî, pêxembera,
860. By God, by the prophets,

861. Tê ax û berê sar da xirab nekî xweş neder e."
861. Do not ruin the pleasant rarity in the cold earth and stone."

862. 21. Mîr go: "Here bero ser sêkînê,
862. 21. The prince said: "Go, O stone, upon the knife,

863. Tu Xwedê kî, vê asînê,
863. By God, by this iron,

864. Tê Xweda xirav nekî çev û birîyêd belek, vê nevsînê."
864. By God do not ruin the beautiful eyes and eyebrows, this soul."

865. 22. Li duaê van qenca, li van xasa,
865. 22. At the prayer of these good ones, of these saints,

866. Gilavî bû stîkê, çû malî şemsa.
866. Gilavî became a lady, she went to the house of Şems.

867. ## BEYTA HESENÊ CÊLÊ
867. ## BEYT OF HESENÊ CÊLÊ

868. Mêrekî zêrek ij [ji] erdê hilda, zanibû wekî zêr malê Şêx Şims e, anî da Şêx Şims, go: "Şêx Şimso, eva malê te ye."
868. A man picked up a gold piece from the ground, he knew that the gold is the property of Şêx Şims, he brought it and gave it to Şêx Şims, he said: "O Şêx Şims, this is your property."

869. Şêx Şims zêr dêst girt anî mal, da Cêlê.
869. Şêx Şims took the gold in his hand, brought it home, and gave it to Cêlê.

870. Cêlê kevanîya mala Şêx Şims bû, ewê gavê destê Cêlê ne vala bû, hevîr distira.
870. Cêlê was the housewife of Şêx Şims's house, at that moment Cêlê's hands were not empty, she was kneading dough.

871. Cêlê gote Şêx Şims go: "Zêr tê ke devê min, hetanî destê min vala dive, ez hildim."
871. Cêlê spoke to Şêx Şims and said: "Put the gold in my mouth, until my hand becomes empty, I will take it."

872. Hetanî Cêlê hevîr stira, zêr devê Cêlê da helya çû xarê.
872. While Cêlê kneaded the dough, the gold melted in Cêlê's mouth and went down.

873. Cêlê qe texmîn nekir ew zêr çewa bû, ku da çû, qe nehate bîrê jî.
873. Cêlê did not guess at all how that gold was, that it went down, and it did not even come to her mind.

874. Wehde derbaz bû, Cêlê hemle derket, Şêx Şims seva wira dilteng bû, gote Cêlê, got: "Tu kevanîya mala min, xizmetkara mala min, wekî mala mi da şuxulê wa qewimîye ne rast e."
874. Time passed, Cêlê turned out pregnant, Şêx Şims became upset because of that, he spoke to Cêlê, he said: "You are the housewife of my house, the servant of my house, that such a thing has happened in my house is not right."

875. Hingê kete bîra Cêlê, wekî ew zêr devê wê da helîyaye, Cêlê gote Şêx Şims, go: "Şêx Şimso, ew zêrê te daye min, ew zêr devê mi da helîyaye çûye, heger tiştek heve ji wî zêrî ye, hergê ji dêv welidîm, wekî usa ne ji wî zêrî ye."
875. Then it came to Cêlê's mind that the gold had melted in her mouth, Cêlê spoke to Şêx Şims, she said: "O Şêx Şims, that gold you gave me, that gold melted in my mouth and went down, if there is anything it is from that gold, if I give birth from the mouth, if not it is not from that gold."

876. Wext, wehde temam bûn, nêzîkîya welidandinê Cêlê gote Şêx Şims go: "Destê xwe bigre."
876. The time, the term was completed, near the birthing Cêlê spoke to Şêx Şims and said: "Hold your hands out."

877. Şêx Şims destê xwe girt, Cêlê dêv ra welidî, kurek kete destê Şêx Şims, batin da deste guharê zêr guha da pê ve kirin.
877. Şêx Şims held his hands out, Cêlê gave birth from her mouth, a boy fell into Şêx Şims's hands, in secret they attached sets of gold earrings to his ears.

878. Şêx Şims îdî bawar kir, wekî kur ji wî zêrî bûye.
878. Şêx Şims then believed that the boy was from that gold.

879. Navê kur danîn Hesen, Hesenê Cêlê.
879. They named the boy Hesen, Hesenê Cêlê.

880. Hesen mezin bû, wextê dest damina bû, batin da xelatê zêrîn jê ra hatin.
880. Hesen grew up, when it was time to hold the hem, in secret golden rewards came to him.

881. Mêra gişka hevsûdî xelatê Hesenê Cêlê dikirin.
881. All the men envied the reward of Hesenê Cêlê.

882. Rojekê Şêx Şims gote Hesen, go: "Te ra lazim e dest û damin."
882. One day Şêx Şims spoke to Hesen, he said: "You need a hand and a hem."

883. 33. Meha kanûna paş sala 1976an li gundê Tsaraşatê yê li ser nehîyeya Hoktêmbêryana Ermenistanê ji zarê Xeza Şêx Reşo hatîye nivîsîn.
883. 33. In the month of January of the year 1976 in the village of Tsaraşat in the Hoktemberyan district of Armenia it was written down from the mouth of Xeza daughter of Şêx Reşo.

884. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".
884. It was printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

885. Cildê I., Yêrêvan, r. 429-433.
885. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 429-433.

886. Şaxeka vî qewlî: "Qewlê Hesenê Cêlê" çap bûye li kov.
886. A variant of this qewl: "The Qewl of Hesenê Cêlê" was printed in the journal

887. "Laliş"ê, Num. 7, 1997 Dihok, r. 107-112, 29 sebeqe ne.
887. "Laliş", No. 7, 1997 Dohuk, pp. 107-112, it consists of 29 stanzas.

888. Nivîsîye Derman Xelefî.
888. Derman Xelef wrote it.

889. 1. Çi hukumeta Xwedê ye,
889. 1. What a judgment of God,

890. Nazil bûye rûerdê ye,
890. It has descended to the face of the earth,

891. Bona Hesenê Cêlê ye,
891. It is for Hesenê Cêlê,

892. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
892. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

893. 2. Çi hukumeta giran e,
893. 2. What a heavy judgment,

894. Nazil bûye rûerdan e,
894. It has descended to the face of the earths,

895. Halê min Heseno,
895. My state, Hesen,

896. Bona Hesenê Cêlan e,
896. It is for Hesen of Cêlan,

897. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
897. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

898. 3. Heseno tî dîn î,
898. 3. Hesen, you are crazy,

899. Şiva qudretê 'hulê ezîz melek Ferxedîn ra dikşînî,
899. You draw the rod of power for the dear angel Ferxedîn,

900. Halê min Heseno,
900. My state, Hesen,

901. Malxirav, tu nizanî,
901. Wretch, do you not know,

902. Şêx Şims ser kursîyê heqîyê rûniştîyê,
902. Şêx Şims is seated upon the throne of truth,

903. Maşê mêra dide, hew distîne.
903. He gives the livelihood of men, he then takes it away.

904. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
904. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

905. 4. Heseno bê dewleto,
905. 4. Hesen, without fortune,

906. Aqil û fem sêrî hereto,
906. Mind and understanding go from the head,

907. Halê min Heseno,
907. My state, Hesen,

908. Malxirav, tu nizanî,
908. Wretch, do you not know,

909. Şêx Şims ser kursîyê heqîyê rûniştîyê,
909. Şêx Şims is seated upon the throne of truth,

910. Maşê mêra distîne, hew dideto.
910. He takes the livelihood of men, he then gives it.

911. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
911. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

912. 5. Hesenê Cêlê ye,
912. 5. It is Hesenê Cêlê,

913. Ketîye berê pêlê ye,
913. He has fallen before the wave,

914. 34. hikmeta (bnb).
914. 34. hikmeta (bnb).

915. Di berhema navborî da, peyv di benda diduyan di jî derbas dibe.
915. In the aforementioned work, the word also passes in the second stanza.

916. Halê min Heseno,
916. My state, Hesen,

917. Malxirav nizane nifirîya wî ye ji birê ye,
917. The wretch does not know his curse is from the brother,

918. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
918. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

919. 6. Çi xelatê hevreng in,
919. 6. What multicolored rewards,

920. Derketine sûkeke teng in,
920. They have gone out to a narrow market,

921. Halê min Heseno,
921. My state, Hesen,

922. Mêrê dîwanê ser oxirme ne, ser ceng in,
922. The men of the court are in a crowd, they are in a fight,

923. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
923. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

924. 7. Borê Hesenê min î şê ye,
924. 7. My Hesen's steed is dun,

925. Sûkê merîfetê da têye,
925. It comes in the market of gnosis,

926. Halê min Heseno,
926. My state, Hesen,

927. Hesenê Cêlê î, hêsîrî î û ney lê ye,
927. Hesen of Cêlan is a captive, and a reed is upon him,

928. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
928. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

929. 8. Borê Hesenê min î çal e,
929. 8. My Hesen's steed is roan,

930. Sûkê merîfetê da hatye xar e,
930. It has come down in the market of gnosis,

931. Halê min Heseno,
931. My state, Hesen,

932. Hesenê Cêlê hêsîr lê ne î sîyar e,
932. Captive Hesenê Cêlê is not mounted upon it,

933. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
933. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

934. 9. Borê Hesenê min î mor e,
934. 9. My Hesen's steed is brown,

935. Sûkê merîfetê da tê di mor e,
935. It comes in brown in the market of gnosis,

936. Halê min Heseno,
936. My state, Hesen,

937. Hesenê Cêlê hêsîr hol xwe nebirîye ser hole,
937. Captive Hesenê Cêlê has not led himself into the arena,

938. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
938. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

939. 10. Borê Hesenê min î reş e,
939. 10. My Hesen's steed is black,

940. Sûkê merîfetê da tê dimeşe,
940. It comes walking in the market of gnosis,

941. Halê min Heseno,
941. My state, Hesen,

942. Halê Hesenê Cêlê hêsîr destê Şêx Şims da qe ne î xweş e,
942. Captive Hesenê Cêlê's state in the hand of Şêx Şims is not pleasant at all,

943. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
943. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

944. 11. Ewa xelatê zêrîn in,
944. 11. Those are golden rewards,

945. Şêx Şims destê xwe Hesenê Cêlê distîne,
945. Şêx Şims takes the hand of Hesenê Cêlê,

946. Kirîye mala defê avîtîye erşê ezmîn e,
946. He put them in the house of the drum and threw them to the throne of the sky,

947. Halê min Heseno,
947. My state, Hesen,

948. Go: "Mêrê dîwanê kesekî reda pê nîne."
948. He said: "No man of the court is behind him."

949. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
949. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

950. 12. Go: "Em ê herne cem Istîa [Stîya] Zîn e,
950. 12. He said: "We will go to Lady Zîn,

951. Bira here bike reca-dileka xelatê Hesenê Cêlê zêrîn e,"
951. Let her go and make a petition-plea for the golden reward of Hesenê Cêlê,"

952. Halê min Heseno,
952. My state, Hesen,

953. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
953. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

954. 13. Dê go: "Lao, şîrê berê dê kî,
954. 13. The mother said: "Child, by the mother's breast milk,

955. Tu ji gulîê Ferxê kî,
955. You are from the braid of Ferxê,

956. Halê min Heseno,
956. My state, Hesen,

957. Tî ê xelatê Hesenê Cêlê lê kî."
957. You will put the reward of Hesenê Cêlê upon him."

958. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
958. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

959. 14. Go: "Daê, ez şîrê berê dê kim,
959. 14. He said: "Mother, I swear by the mother's breast milk,

960. Ji gulîê Ferxê kim,
960. I swear by the braid of Ferxê,

961. Halê min Heseno,
961. My state, Hesen,

962. Xelatê Hesenê Cêlê hew lê kim."
962. I will surely put the reward of Hesenê Cêlê upon him."

963. Miskîn halê min pîr Heseno.
963. Poor is my state, old Hesen.

964. 35. fexrê (bnb).
964. 35. fexrê (bnb).

965. 15. The mother said: "Child, when, until when?"

968. Then Hesenê Cêlê will take color with his reward,"

970. ## BEYTA ÎBRAHÎMÊ BIRA
970. ## BEYT OF ÎBRAHÎM THE BROTHER

971. Rojekê rojan e,
971. One day of days,

972. Îbrahîmê bira rabûye ser banan e,
972. Îbrahîm the brother stood upon the roofs,

973. Qurana mezin danîye ser çokan e,
973. He placed the great Quran upon his knees,

974. Divê: "Dayê, serê min dêşe ber mêvan e."
974. He says: "Mother, my head aches before the guests."

975. Divê, axî Cibrahîlê axî ye,
975. He says, ah earth, Cibrahîl is of earth,

976. Firî çû bihişta baqî ye,
976. He flew and went to eternal paradise,

977. Bûye mêvanê Nebî ye.
977. He became the guest of the Prophet.

978. [Divê]: "Lê Fatimê, dilbirînê,
978. [He says]: "O Fatimê, wounded heart,

979. Cahabekê bide dewrêşê Medînê,
979. Give a message to the dervishes of Medina,

980. Divê Îbrahîmê bira me qelandîyê dengê Quranê, sewta Yasînê."
980. He says Îbrahîm the brother has consumed us with the voice of the Quran, the sound of Yasin."

981. Divê, "Lê Fatimê, dilkovanê,
981. He says, "O Fatimê, sorrowful heart,

982. Rabe cahabekê bide dewrêşê dîwanê,
982. Rise and give a message to the dervishes of the court,

983. Îbrahîmê bira me qelandîye dengê Yasînê, sewta Quranê."
983. Îbrahîm the brother has consumed us with the voice of Yasin, the sound of the Quran."

984. Nevî divê: "Bilêlî Hebeş, bike bilezîne,
984. The prophet says: "Bilal of Habesh, hurry up,

985. Xwe Medînê ra bigehîne,
985. Reach Medina,

986. Bêje Fatimê, bê Îbrahîmê bira nexaş e, halê xwe tinîne."
986. Tell Fatimê, tell her Îbrahîm the brother is sick, he has no strength."

987. Bilêlî Hebeş dike dilezîne,
987. Bilal of Habesh hurries up,

988. Xwe Medînê ra digehîne,
988. He reaches Medina,

989. Fatim dûr va Bilêlî Hebeş dibîne,
989. Fatimê sees Bilal of Habesh from afar,

990. Xwe Bilêlî Hebeş ra digehîne.
990. She reaches Bilal of Habesh.

991. Divê: "Bilêlî Hebeş tu wî kî Îlahî ye,
991. She says: "Bilal of Habesh, I swear by God,

992. Tê mi ra bêjî pirsa rastî ye,
992. You will tell me the true word,

993. Qe halê Îbrahîmê biraê min çî ye?"
993. What is the state of my brother Îbrahîm?"

994. Bilêlî Hebeş go: "Ez wî kim Îlahî ye,
994. Bilal of Habesh said: "I swear by God,

995. Ez ê te ra bêjim pirsa rastî ye,
995. I will tell you the true word,

996. Îbrahîmê biraê te dêşe dest û ser û pê ye,
996. Your brother Îbrahîm's hands and head and feet ache,

997. Divê tu bigihîjî ser e,
997. He says you may reach him,

998. Divê tu negihîjî ser e.
998. He says you may not reach him.

999. Fatim dike dilezîne,
999. Fatim hurries up,

1000. Hesen, Husêîn her du kurê xwe mal tîne,
1000. She brings her two sons Hesen and Husêîn to the house,

1001. Xwe Îbrahîmê biraê xwe ra digehîne.
1001. She reaches her brother Îbrahîm.

1002. Divê: “Axî Cibrahîl, ruhê Îbrahîmê birê min nestîne, Rûhê Hesen, Husêînê min ber xîne."
1002. She says: "Earthly Cibrahîl, do not take the soul of my brother Îbrahîm, cast down the souls of my Hesen and Husêîn instead."

1003. Axî Cibrahîl go: "Fatim, ez axî Cibrahîlê perkur im.
1003. Earthly Cibrahîl said: "Fatim, I am the short-winged earthly Cibrahîl.

1004. Şaî şalûla difirim, Ez ne hatime ruhê ber ruha xînim, Ez hatime destê bav û kur hev dabirrim."
1004. I fly like the king of the birds, I have not come to exchange soul for soul, I have come to cut the hands of father and son from each other."

1005. Go: "Fatim, ez axi Cibrahîlê perkęsk im, Ez şaî şalûla dikime qest e.
1005. He said: "Fatim, I am earthly Cibrahîl of the green wings, I make my aim like the king of the birds.

1006. Ez nehatime ruhu ber ruha xînim, Ez hatime ruhê Îbrahîmê biraê te meqes kim."
1006. I have not come to exchange soul for soul, I have come to cut the soul of your brother Îbrahîm like scissors."

1007. Fatimê go: “Bînin, bînin darê çardarê bînin, Cinîyazê Îbrahîmê ser daynin."
1007. Fatimê said: "Bring, bring, bring the wood of the four poles, set the corpse of Îbrahîm upon it."

1008. Anîn, anîn, anîn, Darê çardarê anîn nivastin, Cinîyazê Îbrahîmê bira ser dawastin.
1008. They brought it, brought it, brought it, they brought the bier and set it down, they placed the corpse of brother Îbrahîm upon it.

1009. Go, hilda yek û du û sê û çar e, Birne nav mezelê giran e.
1009. She said, one and two and three and four lifted it, they took it into the heavy graveyard.

1010. Fatimê go: "Daê dêranê, tirsa min mehrê belek e,"
1010. Fatimê said: "Mother of sorrows, my fear is the spotted snake,"

1011. 36. Mehr: Mar.
1011. 36. Mehr: Snake.

1012. Ditirsim wê here derê merzelê Îbrahîmê biraê min veke,
1012. I fear it will go and open the door of the grave of my brother Îbrahîm,

1013. Mehro, bextê te da me, çev û birîyê belek xwe ra xirav neke."
1013. O snake, I am in your grace, do not ruin his beautiful eyes and eyebrows for yourself."

1014. Fatime go: "Daê delîlê, tirsa min tîremehr e, Wê tirba Îbrahîmê biraê mi da here xar e, We bixwe goştê nazik i nazdar e."
1014. Fatime said: "O guiding mother, my fear is the arrow-snake, it will go down into the grave of my brother Îbrahîm, it will eat the tender and delicate meat."

1015. Mişka gote li van mehra: "Me herne li van wara, Em ê bixun xwe ra goştê nazik nazdara."
1015. The mouse said to these snakes: "Let us go to these places, we will eat for ourselves the tender delicate meat."

1016. Divê, miska gote li vi mehrî: "Me herne goristanê giran li herî tehrî, Em ê bixun goştê nazik î serê zimanî."
1016. He says, the mouse said to this snake: "Let us go to the heavy graveyard in every manner, we will eat the tender meat of the tip of the tongue."

1017. Fatimê got: "Daê, dilê min dibêye, Rabe em serxweşîyê bidne bavê ye, Îbrahîmê bira terk kirîye dinê ye."
1017. Fatimê said: "Mother, my heart speaks, arise, let us give condolences to the father, brother Îbrahîm has abandoned the world."

1018. Fatimê got: "Daê, dile min ê kînekîn e, Îbrahîmê biraê min mirîye, bavê min tenê dimîne, Dike nake herd' kurê xwe jî anîye, Nikare ruhê Îbrahîmê biraê xwe vegerîne."
1018. Fatimê said: "Mother, my heart is full of grief, my brother Îbrahîm has died, my father remains alone, whatever she does she has brought both her sons too, she cannot return the soul of her brother Îbrahîm."

1019. Bavê Fatimê divê: "Lao, dilê min dibêye,
1019. The father of Fatimê says: "Child, my heart speaks,

1020. Îbrahîmê bira ço [çû], bavê te ma tenê ye,
1020. Brother Îbrahîm went, your father remained alone,

1021. Ez ê ça kim zêrê xeznê, malê dinê ye?"
1021. What will I do with the gold of the treasury, the wealth of the world?"

1022. ## BEYTA MÊZÎNÊ
1022. ## BEYT OF MÊZÎNÊ

1023. 1. Heça têlê mêzînê xar8 bikşîne,
1023. 1. Whoever pulls the wire of the scale down,

1024. Donzde pût hesin, hevt sala ser pişta xwe digerîne,
1024. Carries twelve poods of iron on his back for seven years,

1025. Mîrê mezin divê: "Hela heqê wî temam nîne."
1025. The great prince says: "Still his punishment is not complete."

1026. 2. Heça darê mêzînê bigre xar e,
1026. 2. Whoever holds the beam of the scale down,

1027. Bandê li ber mîrê xwe bê zar e,
1027. The servant before his prince is without voice,

1028. Xenîmê wî mehrekî har e.
1028. His enemy is a rabid snake.

1029. 3. Dive têl û dezmal e,
1029. 3. It becomes wire and cloth,

1030. Binê niga heta sêrî diale,
1030. It wraps from the bottom of the feet to the head,

1031. Rojê sê cara xûna wî dixare.
1031. Three times a day it drinks his blood.

1032. 4. Ji ezmana mêzîn hate xar e,
1032. 4. The scale came down from the sky,

1033. Têlê mêzînê kete destê bendan e,
1033. The wire of the scale fell into the hands of the servants,

1034. Heçî kesê qelpîa mêzînê dil da ne,
1034. Whoever sets his heart on the falseness of the scale,

1035. Cîyê wî ne erd e û ne ezman e.
1035. His place is neither earth nor sky.

1036. 5. Mêzîn ew e li erşan e,
1036. 5. That scale is in the heavens,

1037. Kirîye nexş û danîye ber çevê bendan e,
1037. He has painted it and placed it before the eyes of the servants,

1038. Ez divêjime ew şêxan û pîra û koçek û beden miskinan e:
1038. I say to those sheikhs and pirs and kocheks and poor bodies:

1039. "Xêra Şîx Adî, mi ra bêjin, çika têlê mêzînê kê badane?"
1039. "By the grace of Şîx Adî, tell me, who has twisted the wire of the scale?"

1040. 37. Meha kanûna pêş sala 1977an li gundê Qamişlûyê -niha Yêxêgnût- yê li ser nehîyeya Hoktêmbêryana Ermenistanê ji zarê Feremezê Ezdoyî hatîye nivîsîn.
1040. 37. In the month of December of the year 1977 in the village of Qamişlû - now Yeghegnut - in the Hoktemberyan district of Armenia it was written down from the mouth of Feremez son of Ezdo.

1041. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".
1041. Printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

1042. Cildê I., Yêrêvan, r. 433-434.
1042. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 433-434.

1043. 38. Xwar.
1043. 38. Downward.

1044. 1. Mêzîn heye du bira ne,
1044. 1. There is a scale of two brothers,

1045. Bi nîrekî hevt têlan e,
1045. With a yoke of seven wires,

1046. Têlê mêzînê destê horiya" Bin 'Henan e.
1046. The wire of the scale is in the hands of the houris of Bin Henan.

1047. 7. Mêzîna min ya biçûk e,
1047. 7. My small scale,

1048. Li ber qulix dike yeke cahil e, bûk e,
1048. A young one, a bride, serves before it,

1049. Bi gumana Xwedê ewê dergê cinetê bi destê xwe, ruhê xwe veke.
1049. By the hope of God she will open the door of paradise with her own hand, with her soul.

1050. 8. Mêzîna min ya mezin e, Li ber qulix dike yeke pîrejin e, Lê cîyê wê tu yêr û welata tune ne.
1050. 8. My large scale, an old woman serves before it, but her place is in no land or country.

1051. 9. Mêzîna min ya mezin e,
1051. 9. My large scale,

1052. Ji erşê ezîm nazil bû, hate erdan e,
1052. Descended from the great throne, came to the earths,

1053. Ez divêjime şêxa û pîran e:
1053. I say to the sheikhs and pirs:

1054. "Ew çi mêr e, ku şiklê mêzînê sehetekê da bela[v] kir her çar qulban e?"
1054. "What man is that, who distributed the shape of the scale in one hour to all four corners?"

1055. 10. Çi mêzîneke helal e,
1055. 10. What a lawful scale,

1056. Malê dinîyalikê dikşîne misqal misqal e,
1056. It weighs the wealth of the worldly realm mithqal by mithqal,

1057. Mêzîn rast e, ne derew e,
1057. The scale is true, not a lie,

1058. Heçî kesê mêzînê rast bikşîne,
1058. Whoever pulls the scale truthfully,

1059. Ewê cinetê bi çevê xwe bivîne.
1059. He will see paradise with his own eyes.

1060. 39. Horiya (bnb).
1060. 39. Horiya (bnb).

1061. 40. Yer: Cih. (bi tirki).
1061. 40. Yer: Place. (in Turkish).

1062. ## BEYTA MISKÎN
1062. ## BEYT OF THE POOR

1063. 1. Ka evika, ka emîya?
1063. 1. Where are the saints, where are the prophets?

1064. Ewan jî axê girt totîya,
1064. The earth took them completely too,

1065. Miskino, jaro, ya ademî.
1065. O poor one, O wretched one, O child of Adam.

1066. 2. Kanên xasê li vir di xas? Kanê Hemze, kanê Ebas? Ew jî ber mirinê nebûn xilas, Miskino, jaro, ya ademî.
1066. 2. Where are the pure ones here in purity? Where is Hemze, where is Ebas? They too were not saved from death, O poor one, O wretched one, O child of Adam.

1067. 3. Kanên xasê li vir di zor?
1067. 3. Where are the pure ones here in power?

1068. Ka Nevîyê sehbe li dor?
1068. Where is the Prophet with the companions around him?

1069. Ew jî çûne hidreta yekê li jor,
1069. They too went to the presence of the one above,

1070. Miskino, jaro, ya ademî.
1070. O poor one, O wretched one, O child of Adam.

1071. 4. Kanên xasê li vir hezîm?
1071. 4. Where are the pure ones here in greatness?

1072. Kanên heçka me dî?
1072. Where is whoever we saw?

1073. Ew jî çûne hidreta yekê hebîb,
1073. They too went to the presence of the beloved one,

1074. Miskino, jaro, ya ademî.
1074. O poor one, O wretched one, O child of Adam.

1075. 5. Kanên Ûsiv, Ûsivê Nebî?
1075. 5. Where is Ûsiv, the Prophet Ûsiv?

1076. Ka salixê çev 'erebî?
1076. Where is the beauty of the Arabian eyes?

1077. 41. Meha kanûna pêş sala 1977an li gundê Qamişlûyê -niha Yêxêgnût- yê li ser nehîyeya Hoktêmbêryana Ermenistanê ji zarê Feremezê Ezdoyî hatîye nivîsîn.
1077. 41. In the month of December of the year 1977 in the village of Qamişlû - now Yeghegnut - in the Hoktemberyan district of Armenia it was written down from the mouth of Feremez son of Ezdo.

1078. It was printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

1081. 33 sebeqe ne.
1081. There are 33 stanzas.

1082. Xêyrî Bozanî wrote it.

1083. 42. Kanê 'elim, kanê enbîya (bnb).
1083. 42. Where are the scholars, where are the prophets (bnb).

1084. Ew ji zane diniyaê da mirin hebî, Miskino, jaro, ya ademî.
1084. He too knows that in the world there was death, O poor one, O wretched one, O child of Adam.

1085. 6. Kanên Silêman pêxemberê hukum dikir? Ka Bilqiza nav û dikir? Ew jî çûn, dinîya terk kir, Miskino, jaro, ya ademî.
1085. 6. Where is Prophet Solomon who used to rule? Where is Bilqiz who made a name? They too went, abandoned the world, O poor one, O wretched one, O child of Adam.

1086. 7. Erê bendeo, sed salî li dinê bî,
1086. 7. Yes O servant, though you be a hundred years in the world,

1087. Bi zêr û ziv dinê xinê bî,
1087. Though you be dyed in the world with gold and silver,

1088. Axir rojekê bendaê mirinê bî,
1088. Finally one day you will be the servant of death,

1089. Miskino, jaro, ya ademî.
1089. O poor one, O wretched one, O child of Adam.

1090. 8. Diniya heye xana tijî,
1090. 8. The world is a full inn,

1091. Hin dimire û hin dijî,
1091. Some die and some live,

1092. Rojekê bê siriya me jî,
1092. One day our turn will come too,

1094. 9. The world is an inn and a dwelling,

1095. Isan tê da bazirgan e,
1095. Man in it is a merchant,

1096. Bazirgan diçe, xan cî da ne,
1096. The merchant goes, the inn stays in its place,

1099. Gelek aşiq hatin-çûne ew hal,
1099. Many lovers have come and gone in that state,

1100. Miskino, jaro, ya ademí.
1100. O poor one, O wretched one, O child of Adam.

1101. 11. Tirba min e li ser kanîyê,
1101. 11. My grave is upon the spring,

1102. Xudan dikse ji 'enîyê,
1102. The owner pulls from the forehead,

1103. 43. Siri: Turn.

1105. 12. My grave is between the two waters,

1110. I asked, why did you not give it?

1111. Ew jî bû ezapê hevt sala,

1113. 14. Mendo, megrî heqê te ye,"

1114. Şîn û girî bê feyde ye,
1114. Mourning and crying is useless,

1117. 15. Take me to the meadow with a cypress in the middle,

1118. Belgê sewlê zêr û dirav,

1121. 16. Ez birme mêrga sewlek bi rast,
1121. 16. Take me to the meadow of a true cypress,

1122. Belgê sewlê zêrê kesk,
1122. The leaves of the cypress are green gold,

1123. Ez miskîn bûm, mi neda li dest,
1123. I was poor, I did not give into the hand,

1124. Miskino, jaro, ya ademî.
1124. O poor one, O wretched one, O child of Adam.

1125. 44. Ev qewl li ser mirina melek Fexredînî hatîye gotin.
1125. 44. This qewl was spoken upon the death of the angel Fexredîn.

1126. Loma li vir dibêje, "Mendo megrî, heqê te ye."
1126. Therefore it says here, "Mendo do not cry, it is your due."

1127. Mendo Şêx Mend kurê melek Fexredînî ye.
1127. Mendo is Şêx Mend, the son of the angel Fexredîn.

1128. Li ser mirîyan tê gotin.
