1129. Lazim e hefteyêkê her roj, êvaran çend gavan bibêjin.
1129. It is necessary to say it a few times every day, in the evenings, for a week.

1130. ## BEYTA MUSA PÊXEMBER
1130. ## BEYT OF PROPHET MUSA

1131. 1. Rojekê rojan e,
1131. 1. One day of days,

1132. Musai bin 'emran e,
1132. Musa son of Emran,

1133. Axi Cibrahîl lê bîye mêvan e.
1133. Axi Cibrahîl became a guest to him.

1134. 2. Rojekê kêmtaqet e,
1134. 2. One day he is weak,

1135. Riya axi Cibrahîl mala Musa pêxamber dikete,
1135. Axi Cibrahîl's path fell to the house of Prophet Musa,

1136. Go: "Musa, tu qe napirsî axî çi xizmet e?"
1136. He said: "Musa, do you not ask at all what service the earthly one needs?"

1137. 3. Musa go: "Wi kim yekê xefûr e,
1137. 3. Musa said: "I swear by the one who is forgiving,

1138. Ez ruhê xwe te ra nakim destûre,
1138. I do not grant permission for my soul to you,

1139. Ez î tenê me, hêsîrê min î hûr e."
1139. I am alone, my captives are small."

1140. 4. Go: "Musaê bin 'emrano,
1140. 4. He said: "O Musa son of Emran,

1141. Tu xwe meke hûnano,
1141. Do not make yourself small,

1142. Risqê hêsîr ne ser milê min û te o."
1142. The provision of the captive is not upon my shoulders and yours."

1143. 5. Músa derda çûye mal e,
1143. 5. Musa went home in sorrow,

1144. Ber da hat dayîka helal e,
1144. The lawful mother came before him,

1145. Go: "Musao, lawo, her ro bengzê te mi xaş e, îro çima wa mi tehl e?"
1145. She said: "Musa, child, every day your face is pleasant to me, why is it so bitter to me today?"

1146. 6. Go: "Dayika min e pîr e,
1146. 6. He said: "My old mother,

1147. 45. Meha kanuna paş sala 1976an li gundê Tsaraşatê ser nehiyeya Hoktêmbéryana Ermenistanê ji zarê Memê Şêx Reşoyî hatiye nivîsîn.
1147. 45. In the month of January of the year 1976 in the village of Tsaraşat in the Hoktemberyan district of Armenia it was written down from the mouth of Mem son of Şêx Reşo.

1148. Çap büye li "Zar gotina kurda".
1148. Printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

1149. Cildê I., Yêrêvan, r.438-440.
1149. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 438-440.

1150. Mi helal ke şîr e, Hatye ser min ferwara mîr e."
1150. Make your milk lawful to me, the decree of the prince has come upon me."

1151. 7. Divê Mûsa ravû mal revîyê,
1151. 7. They say Musa arose and fled the house,

1152. Ber ketin deşt û zozan, çîya û banîyê,
1152. Plains and highlands, mountains and heights lay before him,

1153. Músa pêxember çû ser du canê qîmetîyê.
1153. Prophet Musa went upon two precious souls.

1154. 8. Mûsa lê dipirse, divê: "Ew çi mezel e, hûn vedidin?"
1154. 8. Musa asks them, he says: "What grave is that, that you are digging?"

1155. Wana got, go: "Mûsaê min, mirîke me heye malê meke,
1155. They spoke, they said: "My Musa, we have a dead person of the house of Mecca,

1156. Bejnê û balê, qedemê te ke,
1156. Whose height and stature, is the size of you,

1157. Go, hela were tê kevê, çika wek e, yan ne wek e?"
1157. He said, come now get into it, is it a match, or is it not a match?"

1158. 9. "Serê tirbê min kin e,
1158. 9. "The head of my grave is short,

1159. Berê tirbê min kin e,
1159. The front of my grave is short,

1160. Bîn-buxsa vê tirbê mi xine."
1160. The breath and scent of this grave suffocates me."

1161. 10. "Serê tirbê min zer e,
1161. 10. "The head of my grave is golden,

1162. Berê tirbê min zer e,
1162. The front of my grave is golden,

1163. Bîn-buxsa vê tirbê mi were."
1163. May the breath and scent of this grave come to me."

1164. 11. "Serê tirbê min reş e,
1164. 11. "The head of my grave is black,

1165. Berê tirbê min reş e,
1165. The front of my grave is black,

1166. Bîn-buxsa vê tirbê çiqa mi xweş e."
1166. How pleasant the breath and scent of this grave is to me."

1186. ## BEYTA NEVÎYÊ OMETÊ
1186. ## BEYT OF THE PROPHET OF THE UMMAH

1187. Rojekê rojan e, Nevî Mehemed e, Elî ye, Emer e, Abûbekir e, Etman e, Nêvîyê Ometê go: "Îro gîhanê min î giran e."
1187. One day of days, it is Prophet Muhammad, it is Elî, it is Emer, it is Abûbekir, it is Etman, the Prophet of the Ummah said: "Today my soul is heavy."

1188. Nevio ji madera, Were em surr bidne xebera, Werin em herin gîhanê Nêvîyê Ometê bidin bang û sera.
1188. O prophets from the mothers, come let us give the secret to the words, come let us go and give call and voice to the soul of the Prophet of the Ummah.

1189. Nevio ji civata, Surr bidin hikyata, Werin em herin gîhanê Nêvîyê Ometê bidin bang û serata.
1189. O prophets from the assembly, give the secret to the story, come let us go and give call and voice to the soul of the Prophet of the Ummah.

1190. Nevî Medînê rabû, Çendîk çend sehva," [y]a pê bûn, Sidq bawarîkê, lev cihê bûn.
1190. The Prophet arose in Medina, several companions were with him, in truth and belief, they were separated from each other.

1191. Nevî Medînê wa diwastîya, Çendîk çend sehva pêj va dadiwestîya.
1191. The Prophet was resting thus in Medina, several companions were resting behind him.

1192. Qudreta yekê hal e, Nevî çûye mal e, Nevî nexaşekî bedhal e.
1192. The power of the one is a state, the Prophet has gone home, the Prophet is a sick one in a bad state.

1193. Nevî go: "Eyşê, Rave raxe xal û ferîşê, Îro gîhanê Nêvîyê Ometê dêşê."
1193. The Prophet said: "Eyşê, get up and spread the rugs and carpets, today the soul of the Prophet of the Ummah aches."

1194. Eyşê xal û ferîşa raxiste,
1194. Eyşê spread the rugs and carpets,

1195. Belgî pê va hilperiste,
1195. She folded the pillows onto them,

1196. Nêvîyê Ometê nexaş e, nav da niviste.
1196. The Prophet of the Ummah is sick, he lay down in them.

1197. Ew in her çar xasê ya Rebî,
1197. They are the four pure ones, O Lord,

1198. 48. Meha kanûna paş sala 1976an li gundê Tsaraşatê li ser nehîyeya Hoktêmbêryana Ermenistanê ji zarê Memê Şêx Reşo hatîye nivîsîn.
1198. 48. In the month of January of the year 1976 in the village of Tsaraşat in the Hoktemberyan district of Armenia it was written down from the mouth of Mem son of Şêx Reşo.

1199. 49. Sehva: Sehabe.
1199. 49. Sehva: Companions.

1200. Pev ketin hatine ser Nevî, Gotin: "Nevio, hemetîya Xwedê mêra te hevî."
1200. They rushed and came to the Prophet, they said: "O Prophet, may the grace of God and the men be with you."

1201. Ew in her çar xasê xefûr, Sekinîne ber yekê jur, Go: "Ya Rebî, me her çara yekî bidî destur."
1201. They are the four pure forgiving ones, they have stood before the one above, he said: "O Lord, give permission to one of us four."

1202. Etman dicehdîne wê ye, Digri şevî û rojê ye, Go: "Ya Rebî heye Nêvîyê Ometê vê carê jî rave ji pê ye?"
1202. Etman strives for this, he cries night and day, he said: "O Lord, is it possible the Prophet of the Ummah will rise to his feet this time too?"

1203. We divêje Abubekir, Go: "Nevio, çî te li me kir? Te [li] me tehl kirîye şirin û şekir."
1203. Abubekir speaks thus, he said: "O Prophet, what have you done to us? You have made sweet and sugar bitter for us."

1204. Emer deyn dike bi zêr e, Go: "Xaska ez bimirama li hêre, Nevi rabiya nav ometa xwe silamet û xêr e."
1204. Emer makes a pledge with gold, he said: "Would that I had died right here, that the Prophet might rise among his Ummah in safety and goodness."

1205. Eli go: "Nevio, tu î mamê min î rast, Ez wî kim Mekke, Medînê dibîrast, Tu rabe ez tirba te da nivast."
1205. Eli said: "O Prophet, you are my true uncle, I swear by Mecca and true Medina, you rise and I will sleep in your grave."

1206. Nevi go: "Elio, her ça[r] divêje ne we ye, Bende heye pey bende ye, Her kesek me ber dora xwe ye."
1206. The Prophet said: "O Elio, it is not as all four say, there is a servant after a servant, each person is before his own turn."

1207. Nevi go: "Elio, her ça[r] divêje we nave, Wekî eva dinîya hana gi cimha ve, Gi rakê rawastave, Tivdira Xwedê jor bike, jêr betal nave."
1207. The Prophet said: "O Elio, it will not be as all four say, even if this world were entirely gathered, and entirely stood up, the plan God makes above cannot be undone below."

1208. Nevi go: "Bişinin Hesen, Husêîn bînin, Ez ê çend westîyeteka lê wesînim."
1208. The Prophet said: "Send for and bring Hesen and Husêîn, I will bequeath a few wills to them."

1322. Look now too, what is the miracle of men, in whose hand is it?"

1334. 29. Re'bîyê go: "Wekî mi wêrîbya cobêr e, Min ê derê dojê girê da berwêr e, Min nedihişt gunekara pêştir kese biçya li hêr e."
1334. 29. Re'bî said: "If I had dared as a warrior, I would have tied the door of hell as a barrier, I would not have let anyone, especially sinners, go here."

1337. I would have shaken the door of hell, Besides the sinners I would not have let anyone else go through it.

1338. 31. Xana, xanane mezin e, Tè da rûniştîye Re'bîya 'Edebî, komek jin e, Şix Adî xwe lutfê xwe yî şîrin kire gazîyê, go: "Xêra Re'bîyê, xêrane mestir e."
1338. 31. The inn, is a great inn, Re'bî of Edeb is seated in it, a group of women, Şix Adî with his sweet grace called out, he said: "The goodness of Re'bî, is the greatest goodness."

1353. ## Bervedan
1353. ## Comparison

1354. Efsaneya kurdî dibêje: Rebîya jiyana xwe, demeka dirêj li şikeftekê, dûrî mirovan, di halê xewê da derbas kirîye, Çiqas sal derbas bûne kes nizane.
1354. The Kurdish legend says: Rebîya spent her life, for a long time in a cave, far from people, in a state of sleep, how many years passed no one knows.

1355. Gelek şêxên navdar hatine şikeftê serdana Rebîyayê, ku wê ji xewê rakin, Rebîya hişyar nebûye.
1355. Many famous sheikhs came to the cave to visit Rebîya, to wake her from sleep, Rebîya did not wake up.

1356. Carekê qelfeka jinan bo serdanê tê şikeftê.
1356. Once a group of women comes to the cave for a visit.

1357. Bi hatina wan ra Rebîya hişyar dibe û radibe ser xwe.
1357. With their arrival Rebîya wakes up and stands upon her feet.

1358. Di nava êzdîyan da Rebîyaya Edawî wek piştovan û xudana jinan tê dîtin.
1358. Among the Yazidis, Rebîya of Edaw is seen as a supporter and patron of women.

1359. Eva efsane dîyar dike pevgirêdana Rebîyayê bi jinan ve.
1359. This legend shows the connection of Rebîya with women.

1360. Ji bona bibîranîna Rebîyayê jinên êzdî her sal, demeka taybet, xêra wê derdixin, li nava şêx û pîran belav dikin.
1360. To commemorate Rebîya, Yazidi women every year, at a specific time, give out offerings for her, they distribute them among the sheikhs and pirs.

1361. Her kevanîyek, jinek, xêra ku ji bona Rebîyayê derdixe, divê ji heft teaman be, mînak birinc, nan, rûn, û hwd her çi ku di malê da peyda dibe.
1361. Every housewife, every woman, who brings out an offering for Rebîya, must make it from seven foods, for example rice, bread, butter, etc. whatever is found in the house.

1362. Rebîyaya 'Edawî naveke dîrokî ye.
1362. Rebîya of Edaw is a historical name.

1363. Ew di dîroka Rojhilata Nêzîk û Navîn da wekî mîstîk, sûfî hatîye naskirin.
1363. She is known in the history of the Near and Middle East as a mystic, a Sufi.

1364. Bîrûbawerîya wê li ser dîndarîyê bala gelek sûfî, hozan û şêxan kişandîye ser xwe.
1364. Her belief regarding religiosity has drawn the attention of many Sufis, poets and sheikhs to itself.

1365. Jîyannivîsên sûfîyan li ser jiyana Rebîyayê dinivîsin, wekî ew jineka aza û serbixwe bûye.
1365. The biographers of the Sufis write about the life of Rebîya, that she was a free and independent woman.

1366. Eslê wê ji eşîra ereban "keys bin adi" ye.
1366. Her origin is from the Arab tribe "Qays bin Adi".

1367. Du salên ji dayikbûnê gihîştine ber destê me: hinek dibêjin sala 713-714an xaçparêzî, hinek jî dibêjin sala 717-718an.
1367. Two birth years have reached our hands: some say the year 713-714 AD, and some say the year 717-718.

1368. Mirîye li sala 801ê li Besrayê.
1368. She died in the year 801 in Basra.

1369. Dê û bavê wê hejar û belangaz bûne.
1369. Her mother and father were poor and destitute.

1370. Hîn di zaroktîyê da hinekan ew dizîye û wekî hêsîr firotîye.
1370. While still in childhood some stole her and sold her as a captive.

1371. Taybetîya şexsê Rebîyayê hebûye.
1371. The persona of Rebîya had a special quality.

1372. Bi saya kiryametê ew ji hêsîrbûnê, xwe azad dike.
1372. Thanks to a miracle, she frees herself from captivity.

1373. Pey serxwebûnê Rebîya jiyana xwe li qûmistanê ji mirovan dûr derbas dike, paşê tê bajarê Besrayê û mirîdan li dora xwe dicivîne.
1373. After independence Rebîya spends her life in the desert far from people, then she comes to the city of Basra and gathers disciples around her.

1374. Gorî gotina jîyannivîsan şagirt û peyçûyên wê gelek bûn.
1374. According to the words of the biographers, her students and followers were many.

1375. Hemû dihatin cem wê bona alîkarîyê, yan jî şêwrekê, guh didan maneya axaftinên wê.
1375. All came to her for help, or for advice, they listened to the meaning of her speeches.

1376. Têkilîya Rebîyayê tevî sûfîyên navdar: Bazîdê Bastami, Malîk bîn Dinar, Rabax al-Kays, Al-
1376. The relationship of Rebîya with famous Sufis: Bayazid Bastami, Malik bin Dinar, Rabah al-Qays, Al-

1377. Tawarî û yên mayîn hebû.60 Di nava êzdîyan da fonksiyona "Qewlê Rebiya 'Edawî" ya rituel jî heye.
1377. Tawari and the rest existed. Among the Yazidis, the "Qewl of Rebiya of Edaw" also has a ritual function.

1378. Tirêq wê diwînin li ser jinên miri.
1378. They perform the rite over dead women.

1379. Bi vê ewana jina mirî li hêvîya Rebîyayê dihêlin, ku ew li axretê xweyîtîyê lê bike.
1379. With this they leave the dead woman to the hope of Rebîya, so that she will take care of her in the hereafter.

1380. Şêx û pîr qewl dibêjin wisa jî li roja bîranîna miriyan, gava salê carekê xêra mirîyan derdixin.
1380. Sheikhs and pirs recite the qewl likewise on the day of remembering the dead, when once a year they bring out an offering for the dead.

1381. Li ser vê di sebeqeyên dawîyê da tê gotin.
1381. This is spoken about in the final stanzas.

1382. Bi qedandina qewlê Rebîyaya 'Edawî xêra mirîyan qebûl dibe.
1382. With the completion of the qewl of Rebîya of Edaw, the offering for the dead is accepted.

1383. Qewl bi awazeka nerm û dilkovan tê gotin.
1383. The qewl is recited with a soft and sorrowful melody.

1384. Awaz bi xisûsîyeta xwe ya muzîkî, nêzîkî stranên dilkovanîyê û yên şînê ye.
1384. The melody, with its musical characteristic, is close to songs of sorrow and mourning.

1385. Li gorî gotina jiyannivîsan Rebîya bi kerametên xwe gelekî bi nav û deng bû.
1385. According to the words of the biographers, Rebîya was very famous with her miracles.

1386. Evê taybetmendîya mîstîk û sûfîyan ji Besrayê di naveroka qewlê êzdîyan da bi hêz hatîye nîşandan.
1386. This characteristic of mystics and Sufis from Basra has been strongly shown in the content of the qewls of the Yazidis.

1387. Di qewlan da du armancên giring hene, ku qewlhuner dema sêwirandinê xwastîye biparêze.
1387. In the qewls there are two important goals, which the qewl-creator wanted to protect during the composition.

1388. Yek rehmbûn û dilovanîya Rebîyayê li hemberî hemû ruhberan, çi mirov be, çi heywan.
1388. One is the mercy and compassion of Rebîya towards all living beings, whether human, or animal.

1389. Ya diduyan, kerameta ku pê ra hebû, ji keramet û karîna hemû şêx û sûfîyên mayîn bêhtir bi hêz bûye.
1389. The second, the miracle that was with her, was stronger than the miracles and abilities of all the other sheikhs and Sufis.

1390. Ji bona armanca pêşîn epizoda rasthatina Rebîyayê li berîyê li ber bîrê tevî dêla tî hatîye nîşandan: Rebîyayê bê fikara dûrûdirêj gulîyên xwe dibire, li hev dihûne, dike şerît, şimika xwe pê girê dide û pê ji bîrê avê dikişîne, dide dêla tî.
1390. For the first goal the episode of Rebîya's encounter in the desert at the well with the thirsty bitch has been shown: Rebîya without long thought cuts her braids, weaves them together, makes a rope, ties her shoe with it and draws water from the well with it, gives it to the thirsty bitch.

1391. Nîyeta giring li vê epizodê ew e, ku mirov divê qencîyê bike bêyî ku li hêvîya bersivdanê bimîne, qencî divê ji dil derê, bêyî bandora mecbûrîyê.
1391. The important intention in this episode is that, a person must do good without waiting for a response, goodness must come from the heart, without the influence of compulsion.

1392. Ev xisûsîyet, ev fikir di nava gelek qewl-beyt û nesîhetên êzdîyan da derbas dibe; ya diduyan hilavêtina şerbika bi avê tijî ye.
1392. This characteristic, this idea passes through many qewls-beyts and advice of the Yazidis; the second is the throwing up of the jug full of water.

1393. Gava şêx şerbik bi avê hildiavêje û bi wekazê xwe lê dixe şerbikê û di hewayê da dişikîne, av û Şerbik tev tên xwarê, lê gava Rebîya 'Edawî bi wekazê li şerbikê dixe, şerbik dişike, parçeyê wî dikevin erdê, lê av li hewayê maliq dimine.
1393. When the sheikh throws up the jug with water and hits the jug with his staff and breaks it in the air, the water and the jug all come down together, but when Rebîya of Edaw hits the jug with the staff, the jug breaks, its pieces fall to the ground, but the water remains suspended in the air.

1394. Bêguman nav û dikrê Rebîyaya 'Edawî ji nava ereban, sûfîzma îslametîyê hatiye nava kurdên êzdî.
1394. Undoubtedly the name and mention of Rebîya of Edaw have come from among the Arabs, the Sufism of Islam, among the Yazidi Kurds.

1395. Di tradisyonên sûfî zma ereban da Rebîya zêde bi evîndarîya xwe li hemberî Xwedê va binavûdeng e.
1395. In the traditions of Sufism of the Arabs, Rebîya is highly renowned for her love towards God.

1396. 60. Short Encyclopaedia of Islam, p.462; Y.E. Bertels "Suffizm û edebyeta suffiya" bi zimanê rúsí. Moskova, 1965, r. 17 -18.
1396. 60. Short Encyclopaedia of Islam, p. 462; Y.E. Bertels "Sufism and Sufi literature" in the Russian language. Moscow, 1965, pp. 17-18.

1397. Axaftinên wê, fikrên filozofî ku di destivîsandan mane, giş dora vê evîna mezin, zelal û bêqisûr difitilin.
1397. Her speeches, the philosophical thoughts that have remained in manuscripts, all revolve around this great, clear and flawless love.

1398. Li qewlê ku di nava êzdîyan da li ser Rebîyayê hatine hûnandin, ev bîrûbawerî cih negirtîye.
1398. In the qewls that have been woven among the Yazidis about Rebîya, this belief has not taken place.

1399. Mitolojîya li ser Rebîyayê her li ser jîyana wê ya paqij e, ku hêjatîya wê wekî askêt û mîstîk- sûfîya navdar îsbat dike.
1399. The mythology about Rebîya is entirely about her pure life, which proves her worth as a famous ascetic and mystic-Sufi.

1400. Dîdemên axaftina wê tevî şivan, rastpêhatina wê tevî sûkê li ber bîrê û ava maliq li hewayê zêde bi tradisyona mitolojîya kurdan a kevnveşop tên girêdan û cihê pêberz û taybet didine wê li nava cêrga sûfîyên êzdîyan.
1400. The scenes of her speaking with the shepherd, her encounter with the dog at the well and the suspended water in the air are mostly connected to the ancient tradition of Kurdish mythology and give her a prominent and special place in the ranks of the Yazidi Sufis.

1401. Qelê Rebîyaya 'Edawî, çawa ez dibînim bi kurtkirina gihîştîye destê me.
1401. The Qewl of Rebîya of Edaw, as I see it, has reached our hands in a shortened form.

1402. Tunebûna şaxên mayîn ber dest, karê lêkolînê û hemberkirina sebeqeya ber destê me girê dide.
1402. The absence of other variants at hand, binds our work of research and the comparison of the stanzas at hand.

1457. Sibê zu diheretim."
1457. Tomorrow early I will depart."

1458. nezan im,
1458. I am ignorant,

1459. Şe'rê go: "Şev e, şevereş e, bilqetehv e, Borê min hindeki reht e, Ez nizanim eva çi erd e, çi welat e?"
1459. Şe'rê said: "It is night, it is pitch black, it is pitch dark, my steed is a little tired, I do not know what earth this is, what land?"

1460. Şe'rê go: "Lao, bajo pêş va bîne, Qewî çêr-kilamê te mi şirin e."
1460. Şe'rê said: "Child, ride and bring yourself forward, your words and speech are very sweet to me."

1461. Şe'rê Mehemed xwe kiribû mêvan e, Hahanga dabû ber sirfe û nan e, "Lao, navê te çi ye?" go.
1461. Şe'rê had made Mehemed a guest for herself, she had immediately set the table and bread before him, "Child, what is your name?" she said.

1462. Go: "Navê mi Mirad e."
1462. He said: "My name is Mirad."

1463. Go: "Şehded be ne tu nav e, Eslê te ku ye?"
1463. She said: "Witness, this is no name, where is your origin?"

1464. Go: "Eslê min mezin e, Mekke, Medine hemû pismamê min e."
1464. He said: "My origin is great, Mecca and Medina are all my cousins."

1465. Some û Selat e,
1465. It is fasting and prayer,

1466. Ewan sê destê şevê diparete,63
1466. They pass three parts of the night,

1467. Paşê dengê Esferê kafir nêçîrê dihate.
1467. Then the sound of the infidel Esfer came from the hunt.

1468. Daymê, Şe'rê destê xwe girtin cotek bere,
1468. Daymê and Şe'rê held a pair of stones in their hands,

1469. Çûne pêşîya kafir Esfer e.
1469. They went before the infidel Esfer.

1470. 63. dinarete (bnb).
1470. 63. dinarete (bnb).

1471. Esfer dûr va bang didete: "Şe'rê, kes mala me ne tê?
1471. Esfer called out from afar: "Şe'rê, does no one come to our house?

1472. Ew kî ye rûniştîye bin xêbetê?"
1472. Who is that seated under the tent?"

1473. Şe'rê go: "Esfer biçûk e, biçûkekî nezan e, Rêwî ye, rîya xwe bûye sergirdan e, Eşqa put-senemê îşev me mêvan e.
1473. Şe'rê said: "Esfer, he is small, a small ignorant one, he is a traveler, he has become lost on his way, for the love of the idol-statue he is our guest tonight.

1474. Biçûk e, biçûkekî xurwet e, Rêwî ye, rîya xwe bûye xelat e, Eşqa pût-senemê îşev vir be, sibê zû diherete."
1474. He is small, a small foreigner, he is a traveler, he has become lost on his way, for the love of the idol-statue he will be here tonight, tomorrow early he will depart."

1475. Wey kafirê bêdîn e,
1475. Woe, the religionless infidel,

1476. Dilê wî gerîyabû xiyal e,
1476. His heart had wandered into suspicion,

1477. Derp û sehet dide xeberê di tehl e.
1477. Instantly he gives bitter words.

1478. Dibêje Şe'rê: "Şe'ra min bêje,
1478. He says to Şe'rê: "Tell my Şe'rê,

1479. Mêvanê xwe diçe bira here,
1479. If her guest goes, let him go,

1480. Wekî neçe, îşev kuştina wî destê mi taqet e."
1480. If he does not go, tonight his killing is in the power of my hand."

1481. Mehemed ji bavê xwe da zergûn e,
1481. Mehemed is pale from his father,

1482. Firîyabû orta zin e,
1482. He had flown to the middle of the saddle,

1483. "Gewrîmiraro -go- şer e, moletê nîne."
1483. "O you of the dead neck - he said - it is war, there is no respite."

1484. Dor hate Mehemedê lawçîn e,
1484. The turn came to Mehemed the brave youth,

1485. Dest avîtibû zilfeqarê64 hêşîn e,
1485. He had cast his hand to the blue Zulfiqar,

1486. Serê kafir du qat kir anî orta zîn e.
1486. He folded the infidel's head in two and brought it to the middle of the saddle.

1487. Dest pîyê wî jîka kevanê wî dibeste, Avîtibû qerpûza zîn, pêş Şe'rê va kiribû qest e, "Şe'rê -go- bikujim ber dilê te hest e, yan ne hest e?"
1487. He tied his hands and feet with the bowstring, he had thrown him to the pommel of the saddle, he had aimed him before Şe'rê, "Şe'rê - he said - if I kill him, is there feeling for him in your heart, or is there no feeling?"

1488. Şe'rê go: "Lao, bikuje, te ra îzn e, Berê da ew kafir ber dilê min bê şewq e, bê nûr e."
1488. Şe'rê said: "Child, kill him, you have permission, from before that infidel was without glow, without light to my heart."

1489. Gava Mehemed serê Esfer birrîye, Qendîla dolava hevt aşa tê bîye,
1489. When Mehemed cut the head of Esfer, the lamp of the wheel of seven mills was illuminated,

1490. 64. Zilfeqar: Ji bo şûrê hz. Elî tê gotin.
1490. 64. Zulfiqar: Said for the sword of His Holiness Elî.

1491. Qalibê zirço maye zeviyê, Dest avite dezmaleke guhbinexs e, Ser çevè Mehemed paqis kir tozê xubarê û terkeş e."
1491. His huge corpse remained on the field, she cast her hand to a patterned handkerchief, she cleaned the dust of dirt and quiver from Mehemed's face."

1492. Şe're go: "Ya lawik, mi ra bêje pirsa sabit, Çika tu ha dijar î, kê daym e, kê bavit?"
1492. Şe'rê said: "O little boy, tell me the firm word, since you are so fierce, who is your mother, who is your father?"

1493. Go: "Şe'rê, Mehemedê pisê Elîê Şêr im, Şûr devê xwe dilêr im, Kafirek hate rû dinê nahêlim, Şe'rê, Mehemedê pisê Elîê Şêr ez im, Şûr di devê xwe digezim, Mala me ber kafir nebezîye, ez jî nabezim."
1493. He said: "Şe'rê, I am Mehemed the son of Elî the Lion, I am brave with the sword in my mouth, I will leave no infidel upon the face of the earth, Şe'rê, I am Mehemed the son of Elî the Lion, I bite the sword in my mouth, our house has not fled before the infidels, I will not flee either."

1494. Berê sibê zer bû dahiştê, Eskerê Qewxe siltan hat gihiştê, Kesi nizanbû çend hezar sîyarê cebe rîşî li piştê.
1494. Before morning, gold descended upon the plain, the army of Qewxe Sultan arrived, no one knew how many thousand riders in armor and chainmail at their backs.

1495. Qewxe siltan qîrînekê radihişte, Go: "Şe'ra min, kê Esfer kuşte?
1495. Qewxe Sultan let out a scream, he said: "My Şe'rê, who killed Esfer?

1496. Mi birîye gaz û gerden û pişt e."
1496. It has cut my spine and neck and back."

1497. Şe'rê go: "Bavo, here tu ne vir bî."
1497. Şe'rê said: "Father, go, do not be here."

1498. "Çira -go- lao?"
1498. "Why - he said - child?"

1499. "Esfer gewrekî bêhunur bû, Hurmetek ji wî çêtir bû."
1499. "Esfer was a skill-less giant, a woman was better than him."

1500. "Şe'rê, bêje mêvanê xwe bira çadirê bê der e, Ew i mi kuştiye Esfer e, Mi birrîye gaz, gerden û pişt e, Mi ji wî ra zor xeber e."
1500. "Şe'rê, tell your guest to come out of the tent, it is he who has killed my Esfer, he has cut my spine, neck and back, I have a strong word for him."

1501. Gava Mehemed sîyar bû, Eskerê kafir pê va dîyar bû, Kasi nizanbû çend hezar bû,
1501. When Mehemed mounted, the infidel army appeared before him, no one knew how many thousands there were,

1502. Mehemed serê sed cotî birrîye, Çared coté maî ber guhastîye.
1502. Mehemed cut the heads of a hundred pairs, he changed the places of fourteen remaining pairs.

1503. Mehemed serê sed cotê din jî birrîye,
1503. Mehemed cut the heads of another hundred pairs too,

1504. Sê sid cotê maî ber guhastîye,
1504. He changed the places of three hundred remaining pairs,

1505. Welle, bille û tille, eva xeber rast e şik tê nîye,
1505. By God, by God, and by God, this word is true, there is no doubt in it,

1506. Mehemed serê sed cotê din jî birrîye,
1506. Mehemed cut the heads of another hundred pairs too,

1507. Du sid cotê mayîn hêybetê ber revîye.
1507. The two hundred remaining pairs fled before his majesty.

1508. Şe'rê serê meydanê sekinî guhbidêr î, Go: "Gewrêmirar, serê Mehemedê tifal ne bazêr î, Şe'rê mehrûmê fîncana jehrê bixwe ruh bispêrî."
1508. Şe'rê stood at the head of the square listening, she said: "O you of the dead neck, do not trade the head of the child Mehemed, deprived Şe'rê will drink the cup of poison and surrender her soul."

1509. Daymê Şe'rê ra biribû mizgîn e, Go: "Hulu Şe'ra mi tu rave, Nava kafira da bûye çevîn e, Hêja ber bavê te bûye huzn e û şîn e."
1509. Daymê took the good news to Şe'rê, she said: "Rise, my Şe'rê, a massacre has happened among the infidels, there has now become grief and mourning before your father."

1510. Qewxe sultan dike gazî:
1510. Qewxe Sultan calls out:

1511. "Maxdusimo, apê Şe'rê î,
1511. "Maxdusimo, you are the uncle of Şe'rê,

1512. Tu naêî hewara me vê carêî?
1512. Will you not come to our aid this time?

1513. Rast e, sîyarekî tenê ye,
1513. It is true, he is a single rider,

1514. Lê em anîne ber yemanê."
1514. But he has brought us to disaster."

1515. Maxdusimo divê: "Qewxe sultan, aqilê te kanê?
1515. Maxdusimo says: "Qewxe Sultan, where is your mind?

1516. Namûsa min namûseke giran e, Ew tifaleke hatîye ber zevîyan e."
1516. My honor is a heavy honor, he is a child who has come to the fields."

1517. Go: "Qewxe sultan, aqilê te ku ye?
1517. He said: "Qewxe Sultan, where is your mind?

1518. Namûsa min namûseke qewî ye, Ew tifaleke te orta meydanê dîye."
1518. My honor is a strong honor, he is a child you have seen in the middle of the square."

1519. Mehemed go: "Gewrê, beytxeber î, dûr va lehfê xwe nekirî, Ewneta Xwedê û mêra ez ê te jî bibirrim serî."
1519. Mehemed said: "O giant, you of the couplet-word, you have not made your boast from afar, by the help of God and the men I will cut your head too."

1520. Mehemed go: "Gewrê bê wehde, Tu wekî nebî Mehemedê tifal nekî şehde, Ewneta Xwedê û mêra ez ê kuştîna te jî bikim cehd e."
1520. Mehemed said: "O giant without a promise, if you do not bear witness to the child Prophet Mehemed, by the help of God and the men I will strive to kill you too."

1521. Dor hate kafirê bêmirwet e,
1521. The turn came to the merciless infidel,

1522. Derpek dani Mehemedê tifal e, Derp û sehet bin da kuştiye bor e, Dor hate kafirê bêdîn e, Derpeke din jî pey derpa xwe diparete,65 Derp û sehet dêst da bela kirîye mertal e.
1522. He landed a blow on the child Mehemed, instantly he killed the steed beneath him, the turn came to the religionless infidel, he lands another blow after his blow, instantly he destroyed the shield in his hand.

1523. Dor hate Mehemedê dijar e, Ber kafir sekinî bîna dîware, Dani serê kafir şeşperek, pê nekiribû tu car e.
1523. The turn came to fierce Mehemed, he stood before the infidel like a wall, he brought down a mace on the infidel's head, which he had never used before.

1524. [Dor hat Mehemedê lawçîn e] Dest avîtibû zilfeqarê hêşîn e, Serê kafir du qet kiribû anîbû.
1524. [The turn came to Mehemed the brave youth] He had cast his hand to the blue Zulfiqar, he had folded the infidel's head in two and brought it.

1525. Îjar Mehemed rûnişt giriya, Go: "Werin, bav-birê mino werin, Dora min kom leşker in.
1525. Now Mehemed sat down and cried, he said: "Come, my father and brothers come, around me are troops of armies.

1526. Dîsa çara min nedikirin, Dêwê firinde hatine şewkulebe çêkirin, Wê bavêjin mi bigerin mi biberin, Mertal destê mi çûye, Şeşper dest mi da bela bûye, Bor bin mi da kuştine, Ez ê vira mame peye, Bira hewara mi Mekke, Medînê bê dayme
1526. Still they could not deal with me, flying demons have come making lightning and fire, they will throw themselves upon me, surround me and take me away, the shield has gone from my hand, the mace has been destroyed in my hand, they have killed the steed beneath me, I have remained here on foot, let Mecca and Medina come to my aid always

1527. mame."
1527. I have remained."

1528. Baki hati cebero, Ne li dar da, ne li bêro, Keremper66 xeber bir çû kire guhê Elîê Şêro.
1528. A wind came mightily, it did not hit a tree, it did not hit a shovel, the tumbleweed took the news and went and put it in the ear of Elî the Lion.

1529. Eli go: "Henife, tu rabe Dundul bikişîne, Teng û bera bişidîne, Bira hazir be hesp û zîn e."
1529. Elî said: "Henife, you arise and pull up Dundul, tighten the girths and straps, let horse and saddle be ready."

1530. Henife go: "Eli pisê min û te ye,
1530. Henife said: "Elî, he is the son of you and me,

1531. 65. dinarete (bnb).
1531. 65. dinarete (bnb).

1532. 66. Keremper: Gongil. Giyayekî sivik e bi bayî ra hildibe diçe.
1532. 66. Keremper: Tumbleweed. A light plant that is lifted and carried away by the wind.

1533. Hún hewara wî neçene, Xwedê bike vê gavê kafirê wî bikujene."
1533. "Do not go to his aid, may God make it so that at this moment his infidel kills him."

1534. Eli go: "Rabe Dundulê bikşîne, Teng û bera lê bişidîne, Bira hazir be hesp û zîn e."
1534. Elî said: "Rise and pull Dundul, tighten the girths and straps on him, let horse and saddle be ready."

1535. Gava Henîfê rabû Dundul dikir zîn e, Teng bera lê dişidîne, Fetha se kit parsuê Dundul dişkênîne.
1535. When Henîfê arose she was saddling Dundul, tightening the girths and straps on him, with a sudden pull she broke three of Dundul's ribs.

1536. Elî derkete ber derê seraê, Go: "Bişêro, kanê pisê min î şêro, Qewî pêşîya te nehate lêro?"
1536. Elî went out to the door of the palace, he said: "Bişêr, where is my lion son, has he not firmly come before you here?"

1537. Bişêr go: "Elî soma û selat be, Nimêj û dia te, Ez hatim, nizanim çi bela jê ra hate."
1537. Bişêr said: "Elî, may fasting and prayer be, your prayer and supplication, I came, I do not know what trouble came to him."

1538. Malê spar bûne çarde sîyarê xumarî, Şor kirine bendê mertala, Mêrka herne şera û dehwa.
1538. The house was entrusted to fourteen armored riders, they have tied the swords to the straps of the shields, the men are to go to war and battle.

1539. Elî wê dihurmijî, Dilê Elî da heye agirekî gujî, Gote Dundulê: "Bimbarek, çi qewî îro bi mi da xwe dikujî?"
1539. Elî is panting, in Elî's heart there is a blazing fire, he said to Dundul: "O blessed one, why do you firmly kill yourself with me today?"

1540. Elî wê dinirî, Dilê Elî da heye agirekî lê gurrî, "Ya bimbarek çi qewî îro bin min da nafirî?"
1540. Elî is groaning, in Elî's heart there is a blazing fire, "O blessed one, why do you not fly beneath me firmly today?"

1541. Pê ra zar hat, go: "Jina te sê kit parsê mi şkênandîye."
1541. With that a sound came, it said: "Your wife has broken three of my ribs."

1542. Elî peye bû hate xarê, Destê xwe parxanê wê xist, Parxan cîê xwe girtin.
1542. Elî dismounted and came down, he put his hand to its ribs, the ribs took their place.

1543. Elî sîyar bû.
1543. Elî mounted.

1544. Elî şêrekî kemîn e, Sî cîzê Quran dixûne, Kumê xwe jî pê ra dertîne,
1544. Elî is a lion in ambush, he recites thirty parts of the Quran, he takes off his cap with it too,

1545. Go: "Ya binaya çeva, tu qewata jina je bistîne."
1545. He said: "O light of the eyes, you take the strength of women from it."

1546. Qudireta melkê Rehmanî, Dundulê Elîi hilanî, Niveka wî şerî jî danî.
1546. The power of the Merciful Angel, lifted Elî's Dundul, and set him in the middle of that war.

1547. Eli wê diçûye, Serê meydanè canikek diye, Canikê pirs kirîye: "Tu wî ki-go- Îlahî ye, Tu bêjî mi pirsa rastî ye, Çika çi kome zor e, zef e, dera han lev civyane?"
1547. Elî went there, at the head of the square he saw a young woman, he asked the young woman: "You are of that divine one, you tell me the true word, what is this strong, numerous group, gathered together here?"

1548. Go: "Ez wî kim Îlahî ye, Ez ê te ra bêjim pirsa rastî ye, Hergê tu Eliê Şêr î, Mehemedê pisê te wê derê ketîye tengavîyê."
1548. She said: "I am of that divine one, I will tell you the true word, if you are Elî the Lion, your son Mehemed has fallen into distress there."

1549. Elî şêrekî kemîn e,
1549. Elî is a lion in ambush,

1550. Ber xwe kişandibû zilfeqar e,
1550. He had drawn the Zulfiqar before himself,

1551. Kafir kiribû belave,
1551. He had scattered the infidels,

1552. Heta Mehemed dîbû her du çeva.
1552. Until he had seen Mehemed with both eyes.

1553. Wel Hesen e, wel Husêîn e,
1553. It is Hesen, it is Husêîn,

1554. Daberjîne bêre stûn e,
1554. They bring down shovels and pillars,

1555. Ewan jî xûn meydanê danîne.
1555. They too have spilled blood on the square.

1556. Hesen, Husêîn şerekî giran kir,
1556. Hesen and Husêîn fought a heavy war,

1557. Ne weke bav û pisa kir,
1557. Not like father and sons did they fight,

1558. Serê zîfir Sultanê mezin jî gian kir.
1558. They made the solid head of the great Sultan heavy too.

1559. ## BEYTA ŞÊX MEND, GÊLÊ
1559. ## BEYT OF ŞÊX MEND, THE GIRLS

1560. 1. Çi subekê melxûn e,
1560. 1. What a cursed morning,

1561. Şêx Mendê borê xwe dikire zîn e,
1561. Şêx Mend saddled his steed,

1562. Çûbû rawa Mîr Sêwdîn e.
1562. He had gone to the hunt of Mîr Sêwdîn.

1563. 2. Çi subekê tarîbava,
1563. 2. What a dark morning,

1564. Şêx Mendê Ferxa çûbû nêçîrê û rawa,
1564. Şêx Mend of Ferx had gone to the hunt and chase,

1565. Çar gêl dîtibû berî ava.
1565. He had seen four girls before the water.

1566. 3. Şêx Mendê Ferxa deyn li gêla dike,
1566. 3. Şêx Mend of Ferx converses with the girls,

1567. Divê: "Ewa gêla min e zarşîrin e,
1567. He says: "She is my sweet-tongued girl,

1568. Xeberê wê şekir dibîne,
1568. Her words are seen as sugar,

1569. Ez nizanim çi zimanî dixûne.”
1569. I do not know what language she speaks."

1570. 4. Gêla mezin divê: "Navê min Gul e,
1570. 4. The eldest girl says: "My name is Gul,

1571. Ez hebûb im çendî dil e,
1571. I am a beloved as much as the heart,

1572. Rêza ez fadil im.”
1572. In the rank I am virtuous."

1573. 5. Gêla duda divê: "Şêx Mendo, navê min Pa ye,
1573. 5. The second girl says: "Şêx Mend, my name is Pa,

1574. Ez hebûb im çendî dinîya ye,
1574. I am a beloved as much as the world,

1575. Ez dikrê xwe Şerq va çûm Şam va xuya ye."
1575. I took my mention to the East and it is visible in Damascus."

1576. Meha tebaxê sala 1975an li bajarê Tibilîsîyê ji zarê Tefûrê Şêx Mehmûd hatîye nivîsîn.
1576. Written down in the month of August of the year 1975 in the city of Tbilisi from the mouth of Tefûr son of Şêx Mehmûd.

1577. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".

1586. In Paradise there is abundance and portion."

1590. 9. The girl says: "Şêx Mend, come let us go among the vineyards,

1591. Tê tev di gulan baxçan û qaza,
1591. You will be entirely among the roses, gardens and geese,

1592. Tê rojê sedî bivînî weke eza."
1592. You will see a hundred a day like me."

1593. 10. Şêx Mend go: "Gêlê, ez gul im, baxçe me, rez, Pisê ezîzî Ferxedîn ez."
1593. 10. Şêx Mend said: "Girl, I am a rose, I am a garden, a vineyard, I am the dear son of Ferxedîn."

1594. 11. Ez pisê melek Ferxedîn im,
1594. 11. I am the son of Angel Ferxedîn,

1595. Behzîkî çengnûrîn im,
1595. I am a falcon with luminous wings,

1596. Ez ser textê zêrîn im,
1596. I am upon the golden throne,

1597. Hatime te bivînim."
1597. I have come to see you."

1611. 15. Şêx Mend said: "Girl, I will become a falcon with clipped wings, I will fly from above, I will cut you off from those places and dwellings."

1619. Your friends have gone, you have remained from them, upon which girl have you remained a lover?"

1620. 19. Şêx Mend go: "Gêlê, ez ne dîn im, ne sewda me, Rast e, hevalê min çûne, ez jê mame, Lê ez ser gêla biçûk maşoq mame."
1620. 19. Şêx Mend said: "Girl, I am neither crazy, nor a madman, it is true, my friends have gone, I have remained from them, but I have remained a lover upon the youngest girl."

1622. Tirsa baxvançîê mîra kes nikare bê pê va."

1623. 21. Şêx Mend go: "Gêlê, ez ê bivime nexaşekî pir giran e, Wê min bidine ser darekî dudan, sisyan û çaran e, Wê mi bivine nava wan rezan e, Hergê go, çî derman e?
1623. 21. Şêx Mend said: "Girl, I will become a very heavy sickness, they will carry me on a bier of two, three and four, they will take me among those vineyards, if it is said, what is the remedy?

1624. Ez ê bêjim sêva sor derman e."
1624. I will say the red apple is the remedy."

1627. Let the share only be for the infidel-hearted."

1629. Rast e, hoste dihat çêdikire,

1630. Lê tu bizanbe, kilît, miftê wê kelê destê mala me ne."
1630. But know you, the locks and keys of that castle are in the hands of our house."

1643. ## BEYTA ŞÊX ŞIMS
1643. ## BEYT OF ŞÊX ŞIMS

1644. 1. Wê kim, ro hiltêye,
1644. 1. That I will do, the sun rises,

1645. Manga zere pè ye,
1645. The golden moon is with it,

1646. Şêx Şims diwanbegê Xwedê ye.
1646. Şêx Şims is the court-master of God.

1647. We kim, ro hilate, Mizgîne[a] welat e, Destê Şêx Şims daye doje, Pira Selat e.
1647. That I will do, the sun rose, it is the good news of the land, the hand of Şêx Şims is upon hell and the Sirat Bridge.

1648. 3. Wê kim, hiltê roj e,
1648. 3. That I will do, the sun rises,

1649. Şêxê nûrî bişkoje,
1649. The sheikh of light blossoms,

1650. Destê Şêx Şims daye Pira Selat û doje.
1650. The hand of Şêx Şims is upon the Sirat Bridge and hell.

1651. 4. Wê kim, hiltê şems e,
1651. 4. That I will do, the sun rises,

1652. Me wê nedîye tu kes e,
1652. We have seen no one there,

1653. Weke bav e, weke pis e,
1653. Like the father, like the son,

1654. 77. Meha kanûna paş sala 1973an li gundê Aygêşatê yê li ser nehîyeya Êcmîadzina Ermenistanê ji zarê Mîrzê Şêx Ewloyî hatiye nivîsîn.
1654. 77. Written down in the month of January of the year 1973 in the village of Aygeshat in the Echmiadzin district of Armenia from the mouth of Mîrz son of Şêx Ewlo.

1655. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda."
1655. Printed in "Folklore of the Kurds."

1656. Cildê II., Moskova, r. 33-37.
1656. Volume II, Moscow, pp. 33-37.

1657. Eva beyta H. Temoyanî bi wergêra ser zimanê ermenîkî çap kiriye û negotîye ji ku hildaye.
1657. H. Temoyan printed this beyt with a translation into the Armenian language and did not say from where he took it.

1658. Binêre: H. Temoyan,
1658. See: H. Temoyan,

1659. Tekstên ola êzdiya.
1659. Texts of the Yazidi religion.

1660. Yêrêvan 2000, r. 40-51.
1660. Yerevan 2000, pp. 40-51.

1661. Wexta beyt bi kubir tê gotin, bi ser sebeqeyan da dîsgotina cêmik zêde dibe: pey rêza diduyan "Şemsê êzdînan, yano", pey rêza sisêyan: "Melkê mêrano."
1661. When the beyt is recited with pride, the twin refrain is added to the stanzas: after the second line "Şems of the Yazidis, oh", after the third line: "Angel of men."

1662. Minak sebeqeya ewilîn bi vî cureyî tê gotin: "Wê kim, ro hiltêye / Manga zere pê ye / Şemsé êzdînan yano / Şêx Şims dîwanbegê Xwedê ye / Melkê mêrano."
1662. For example, the first stanza is recited in this manner: "That I will do, the sun rises / The golden moon is with it / Şems of the Yazidis, oh / Şêx Şims is the court-master of God / Angel of men."

1663. Ji sebeqeyan 18 hem kubir tê guhastin hem cêmika wê.
1663. From stanza 18 both the pride is changed and its twin refrain.

1664. Pey rêza diduyan "Şêx Şimso, navê te mir e", pey rêza sisêyan: "Ezîzê min, navê te mîr e" zêde dibe.
1664. After the second line "Şêx Şims, your name is prince", after the third line: "My dear one, your name is prince" is added.

1665. Minaka sebeqeya 18an wiha tê gotin: "Tu bavê Alê-reş î/ Şêro, tu yî Laliş î, / Şêx Şimso, navê te mîr e,/Derge-dîwanê Xwedê te jî / Ezîzê min navê te mîr e."
1665. The example of the 18th stanza is recited thus: "You are the father of Al-Reş / Lion, you are Laliş / Şêx Şims, your name is prince / You are also the door and court of God / My dear one, your name is prince."

1666. Ji sebegeya numareya 34an Mirzê Şêx Ewloyî ritma teqla qewlê guhast, sebeqe bé cémik, kubir ji recitatif got.
1666. From stanza number 34 Mîrz son of Şêx Ewlo changed the rhythm of the qewl's imitation, he recited the stanza without the twin refrain, pridefully as recitative.

1790. 1. Me yarek dibê me bike minetê,
1790. 1. A friend tells us to make entreaty,

1791. Şerqê bixûn, Şamê her vê xetê,
1791. Read it in the East, in Damascus go to this writing,

1792. Ew mezela cudê me tê.
1792. That station comes as our separation.

1793. 2. Werin bixûnin vê xetê,

1794. Ew tehlîya ser qurbetê,
1794. That bitterness upon exile,

1795. Bira her pênc terêqê wî rûnên hidretê."
1795. Let all five of his tarîqas sit in the presence."

1806. 91. Hidret: Hizûr.
1806. 91. Hidret: Presence.

1810. hevt sala mabû Şamê hevsa.

1811. 7. At that time I was a rose garden,

1812. The opportunity for travel had come, it was time,

1815. 8. Mexsus hate Somaê,
1815. 8. Especially he came to Soma,

1816. Dengê dûr qe[t] wî naê,

1817. Ez hatime dengê dûr xwe ra biveme.

1818. 9. Îlahio, te em nivîsîn,

1820. Dilê qurbetîya qewî tîsî.

1821. 10. The heart of exile is an ache,

1833. Ez í miskînî her awa bûm.

1920. ## BEYTA ELÎ ŞÊRÊ XWEDÊ
1920. ## BEYT OF ELÎ THE LION OF GOD

1921. Sahba kir leşker e, Çû ser kela kafir e, Dîna xwe daê gewrekî wê hazir e.
1921. Morning broke over the army, they went to the castle of the infidel, they noticed a giant is ready there.

1922. Gewrekî çim-çim dibijartin, Serê rîya vedişartin, Hin dikuştin, hun diperatin.
1922. A giant chose them little by little, hid at the top of the paths, killed some, crushed some.

1923. Hesen, Husêîn girtin, Gelîya warkirin, Kela mêzîn da xar kirin, Go: "Hûn ê vira da bin, heta roja dimirin."
1923. He caught Hesen and Husêîn, pitched camp in the valleys, brought them down into the castle of scales, and said: "You will be here, until the day you die."

1924. Çi sibekê nehîn e, Digri Eyş, Fat û Zîn e, Seva herd' kurê Elî ne.
1924. What a morning of mourning, Eyş, Fat and Zîn cry, for both sons of Elî.

1925. Elî dihate mal e Fatimê pê ra şer û qal e, Gote: "Te girtî kirine zîndan e" Ew Fatma dêmşelale.
1925. Elî came home, Fatimê quarrels and argues with him, she said: "You have imprisoned them," that Fatma with a waterfall-face.

1926. Ew Fatma dêmbiçûk e, Digere sûk bi sûk e, Unda kirîye du biçûk e.
1926. That Fatma with a small face, wanders market to market, she has lost two little ones.

1927. Çi sibekê zû ye, Elî şûştîye des û çev û rû ye.
1927. What an early morning, Elî has washed hands, eyes and face.

1928. Ço cem nebî ye,
1928. He went to the prophet,

1929. Go: "Ya Eli ye, Xebera xwe bêje hêdî ye."
1929. He said: "O Elî, speak your word slowly."

1930. Go: "Xebera min nave hêdî, Feleka min mihêdî, Ez ê herme xiraba Amêdî."
1930. He said: "My word does not become slow, my fortune is unhurried, I will go to the ruins of Amêdî."

1931. Go: "Neçe, leşkera te bide me."
1931. He said: "Do not go, give us your army."

1932. Go: "Leşker naêne birinê, Kafirê min binzilzil in.
1932. He said: "The army cannot be taken, my infidels are troublemakers.

1933. Wê derê kala è mi bigrin, We Hesen, Husêîn yan bikujin, Yan jî tê da wê bimirin."
1933. There they will capture my old ones, either they will kill Hesen and Husêîn, or they will die in it."

1934. Eli anî bîraste,
1934. Elî arranged it rightly,

1935. Çil sandoq pîvaste,
1935. Prepared forty boxes,

1936. Heyştê eshebe nav nivaste,
1936. Eighty companions slept in them,

1937. Gemî çêdikir, rûê behrê dixeste.
1937. He built a ship, and set it on the face of the sea.

1938. Elî sîyarê Werdekê, Bar dike êrdekê, Datîne mêrga mîr, dusekê.
1938. Elî mounts Werdek, he loads a camp, he sets down at the prince's meadow, straight away.

1939. Badin wê da dihate,
1939. Badin came there,

1940. Şer e, qateqat e,
1940. It is a battle, layer by layer,

1941. Divê: “Ew ki ya mêrga mîr danîye?
1941. He says: "Who has set down in the prince's meadow?

1942. Teyr teyrtîya xwe difire,
1942. Even a bird in its birdness if it flies,

1943. Ez baska lê dibirrim."
1943. I cut its wings."

1944. Eli go: "Gewrîmezino, Bes tehna bidi mino, Xo tu ne mér í, ez jin o?"
1944. Elî said: "Big giant, stop taunting me, aren't you a man, and I a woman?"

1945. Eli ber xwe cewandi pişt e,
1945. Elî turned him to his back,

1946. Badî erdê dixiste, Sê kit parasî zik da dişkênande, Dest da hemla, dest da bisulman bû.
1946. He threw Badî to the ground, broke three ribs into his belly, gave his hand to the effort, gave his hand and became a Muslim.

1947. Elî go: "Welle, bille û tillê, Tişte destê min hilê, Ez ê te tê kime mîr, daynime serê kelê."
1947. Elî said: "By God, by God, and by God, pick up the things of my hand, I will make you a prince, and put you at the head of the castle."

1948. Go: "Here bêje mîr ew e Misirê qazî, Digere çerx û bazî, Ça kêfa mîr bixazî.
1948. He said: "Go tell the prince he is the judge of Egypt, he wanders in circles and games, however the prince desires.

1949. Bêje mîr ew e Misirê qata, Digere çerx welata, Mîrê bîna te jî didinê maş û xelata."
1949. Tell the prince he is the layer of Egypt, he wanders circling the lands, princes like you also give him salary and gifts."

1950. Badî diçe mîr dipirsîye,
1950. Badî goes and asks the prince,

1951. Go: "Mîrê min ew e Misirê qazî, Digere çerx û bazî, Ça kêfa mîr bixazî.
1951. He said: "My prince, he is the judge of Egypt, he wanders in circles and games, however the prince desires.

1952. Ew e Misirê qata, Digere çerx welata, Mîrê bîna te dibine maş û xelata."
1952. He is the layer of Egypt, he wanders circling the lands, princes like you take him salary and gifts."

1953. Mîr go: "Here bêje pelewanî, Bira xwe neke zor e, Bira bar ke were jor e."
1953. The prince said: "Go tell the champion, let him not exert himself, let him load and come up."

1954. Go: "Here bêje pelewanî, Bira xwe neke bargiranî, Bira bar ke bê xan û manî."
1954. He said: "Go tell the champion, let him not make himself a heavy burden, let him load and come to the house and dwelling."

1955. Hat gotê, Elî ber kir hat, Go: "Ew hêstire bavkulab e,
1955. He came and told him, Elî loaded and came, he said: "He is a mule of a hook-father,

1956. Xwe da dergê derab e, Tè da nirrîya Emerî bin Xeteve.
1956. He put himself to the heavy door, in it roared Emer son of Xetev.

1957. Ew hêstira bavker e, Xwe da dergê der e, Tê da nirriya Emer e.
1957. He is a mule of a donkey-father, he put himself to the outside door, in it roared Emer.

1958. Dergevan dengê Emer nas kir, Go: "Ne gurrîna ewra bû, Ne nirrîna şêra bû, Lê dengê Emerê cêyran bû."
1958. The gatekeeper recognized Emer's voice, he said: "It was not the rumbling of clouds, nor the roaring of lions, but the voice of Emer the neighbor."

1959. Elî ser milê xwe ra fikirî, Badi xulqê xwe kirî.
1959. Elî looked over his shoulder, Badî showed his nature.

1960. Elî ço cem dergevanî,
1960. Elî went to the gatekeeper,

1961. Go: "Tu xayê xwe û çend serîyan î?
1961. He said: "Are you the owner of yourself and how many heads?

1962. Tu divêjî evi bisurman î?"
1962. Do you say you are a Muslim?"

1963. Qudreta yekê xefûr e, Elî du tilî dane jûr e, Serê dergevan firand avîte gelîyê kûr e.
1963. By the power of the Forgiving One, Elî gave two fingers upwards, he made the gatekeeper's head fly and threw it into the deep valley.

1964. Mir Elî pirsîye: "Hila te çî ye?
1964. The prince asked Elî: "What is your trick?

1965. Te serê dergevanê min firîye?"
1965. You made the head of my gatekeeper fly?"

1966. Eli go: "Mîrê min, kemker têne kaşa, 'Hedê keran û ceşa, Yê usa çi na ber dergê mîran û paşa?"
1966. Elî said: "My prince, bad donkeys come to the slopes, the limit of donkeys and foals, what do such ones do before the door of princes and pashas?"

1967. "Mirê min -go- yê kemker têne zevîya, Pir diçinê doxteşîya, Yê usa digrin tînin dikine tewaşê îgrmîya."
1967. "My prince - he said - the bad donkeys come to the fields, many go to the steep paths, they catch such ones and bring them to be a spectacle for the twenty."

1968. Elî deh û du gul hildavêtin, Tilîyê xwe pê ra dimêtin, Kafira xelat dirêtin.
1968. Elî threw up twelve roses, sucking his fingers with them, the infidels poured out gifts.

1969. Kafir Elî şik ketîye, Got: "Hunurê wî bîna hunurê Elî ye, Lê Elî carek e, ez du carê Elî me."
1969. The infidel became suspicious of Elî, he said: "His skill is like the skill of Elî, but Elî is once, I am twice Elî."

1970. Elî go: “Mîrê min tu bawarî nayne yêqîn e, Here du cêjkê misurmana mi ra bîne, Ez serê wan pêş te va hilqetînim."
1970. Elî said: "My prince, if you do not bring certain belief, go bring two Muslim cubs to me, I will cut off their heads before you."

1971. Çon Hesen, Hûsêîn anîn wê va, Qeyd û zincîr pê va.
1971. They went and brought Hesen and Husêîn there, with fetters and chains on them.

1972. Go: "Mîrê min, girtîyê te ev in?
1972. He said: "My prince, are these your prisoners?

1973. Ella neke evana ber şûrê min kevin, " Evan bive himamê himamîş ke."
1973. God forbid they fall before my sword," take these to the bath and wash them."

1974. Naz û nemet pê de, Şûrê hêşîn hespa lê de, Subekê min û wana rûê hev de.
1974. Give them grace and blessing, give them blue swords and horses, in the morning set them and me face to face.

1975. Hesen Hûsêîn birin hemamê, hemamış kirin, Naz û nemet lê dan, Hespê bedew pê dan.
1975. They took Hesen and Husêîn to the bath, washed them, gave them grace and blessing, gave them beautiful horses.

1976. Kafir go: "Elî reşekî min heye mixarê, Diorre mîna ewrê baharê.
1976. The infidel said: "Elî, I have a black one in the cave, he roars like a spring cloud.

1977. Hevt dikişînin ser e, Hevt dikişînin hevsar e, Hevt jî ji mixarê derdixine der e,
1977. Seven pull his head, seven pull his halter, and seven bring him out of the cave,

1978. 107. Himamış kirin: Ji bo şûştin û veşûştina kesekî tê gotin.
1978. 107. Himamış kirin: Said for washing and bathing someone.

1979. Pak bike.
1979. Make clean.

1980. Eliê nizanim lê bike çare?"
1980. I do not know if Elî will make a remedy for it?"

1981. Eli go: "Berde min qalê, Heki Eli kire çare, Yanê na, Elî ber wî bêzar e."
1981. Elî said: "Leave the talk to me, either Elî makes a remedy, or else, Elî is helpless before him."

1982. Sibekî heta êvarê, Kafira meydan bijarê,
1982. From morning until evening, the infidels chose the square,

1983. Hevta kişand ser e,
1983. Seven pulled his head,

1984. Hevta kişand hevsar e,
1984. Seven pulled his halter,

1985. Hevta jî mixarê derxist der e,
1985. And seven brought him out of the cave,

1986. Berdane Elî şer e.
1986. They released him to Elî for battle.

1987. Elî, reş rabûne hev e, Eli ber xwe kişand zilfeqar e, Rehnê kafir qut kir yek car e.
1987. Elî and the black one rose against each other, Elî drew the Zulfiqar before himself, he cut the infidel's root at once.

1988. Ew kafirê dînmû ye, Rehnê xwe ra diçûye, Rehnê xwe Elî werdikire.
1988. That hair-religion infidel, went to his root, Elî was turning his root upside down.

1989. Ew kafirê dînsist e, 108 Rehnê xwe ra diheriste, Gihişte Eli kolemist e.
1989. That weak-religion infidel, attacked his root, he reached Elî with a fist.

1990. Quran, kitêba hebû, Weki Eli çil şevi ber wî guhî kerr bû.
1990. The Quran, the book was there, so that Elî was deaf in that ear for forty nights.

1991. Kafir çû hîlê kir,
1991. The infidel went and made a trick,

1992. Hevt hodeziri li xwe kir,
1992. He put on seven armors,

1993. Beraşeki mermerkirî ser kir,
1993. He put a marbled millstone on top,

1994. Teze hat Elî ra şer kir.
1994. Freshly he came and fought with Elî.

1995. 108. Dinsist: Kesê ku ji alîyê bawerîya xwe ve sist e.
1995. 108. Dinsist: A person who is weak in his faith.

1996. 109. Kolemist: Kulmist.
1996. 109. Kolemist: Fist.

1997. 110. Hodeziri: Cilen zirxi.
1997. 110. Hodeziri: Armored clothes.

1998. Zeripúş.
1998. Armor-clad.

1999. Elî kafir teze rabûne hev rik e,
1999. Elî and the infidel freshly rose against each other in stubbornness,

2000. Elî avîte kafir zilfeqarê kinik e,
2000. Elî threw the short Zulfiqar at the infidel,

2001. Hevt hodeziri, beraşê mermerkirî birrî heta gelîyê berik e.
2001. He cut the seven armors and the marbled millstone down to the valley of the bullet.

2002. Elî go: "Elle û ekber î, Wekî te neda ber şeşperê zerî, Min ê qut kira pişta ga û mehsî, Wekî dinîya serî."
2002. Elî said: "God is great, since you did not yield to the golden mace, I would have cut the back of the bull and the fish, on which the world rests."

2003. Elî gotê Emer e: "Tu derge bike sefer e, Xwe bide ber e."
2003. Elî said to Emer: "You make the door travel, put yourself before it."

2004. Kafir anî hîle kir,
2004. The infidel brought and made a trick,

2005. Pîrek kire dêleke gurrî çêkir,
2005. He made an old woman into a mangy bitch,

2006. Toximê kafir 'hûrê genî kir,
2006. The infidel's seed made the stomach rotten,

2007. Anî ber Emer ra derge ra derbaz kir,
2007. He brought it before Emer and passed it through the door,

2008. Toximê kafir dinê werkir.
2008. The infidel's seed overturned the world.

2009. Elî hate ba Emer e, Go: "Te derge rind kire sefer e?"
2009. Elî came to Emer, he said: "Did you make the door travel well?"

2010. Go: "Dêleke gurrî 'hûrekî gurrî, Derge ra tenê derketine der e."
2010. He said: "A mangy bitch with a mangy stomach, only came out through the door."

2011. "Aha, Elî -go- te toximê kafir, Dîsa dinê bela kir."
2011. "Aha, Elî - he said - you have made the infidel's seed spread trouble in the world again."

2012. Elî kir nekir îdî çar pê nekir.
2012. Whatever Elî did, he could no longer make a remedy for it.

2013. Hesen, Husêîn hatin wê va, Elî, Emer şa bû pê va, Badîn kirine mîr danîne serê kelê va.
2013. Hesen and Husêîn came there, Elî and Emer rejoiced at it, they made Badîn a prince and put him at the head of the castle.

2014. Reş revî kete pişt demir qapı da, Wekî reş rave ji mixarê, derî serder, binder pola ne.
2014. The black one fled and fell behind the iron gate, so that if the black one runs from the cave, the door's upper and lower frame are steel.

2015. Gava serderê ber nizdê tivinga bimaşe, Bindarê ber gizmê sola bimeşe, Hingê kafir ê dîsa dinê alt ke.""
2015. "When the upper frame marches before the barrels of rifles, the lower frame marches before the boots of shoes, then the infidel will defeat the world again."

2016. Gava serderê ber nizdê tivinga bimaşe, Bindarê ber gîzmê sola bimeşe, Hingê kafir ê dîsa dinê alt ke.
2016. When the upper frame marches before the barrels of rifles, the lower frame marches before the boots of shoes, then the infidel will defeat the world again.

2017. Elî dengê xwe weke ziremisqalekê dide quling,
2017. Elî gives his voice to the crane like an armor-scale,

2018. baharê wexta diçe zozana dike qîrîn,
2018. in spring when it goes to the highlands it cries out,

2019. birîna kafir diaxive, divê: "Elî hê sax e."
2019. the infidel's wound speaks, it says: "Elî is still alive."

2020. Payîzê quling dadigere berrîyê dîsa dike qîrîn,
2020. In autumn the crane returns to the plain and cries out again,

2021. kafir dîsa divê: "Eli sax e," ditirse û ji mixarê dernaê.
2021. the infidel again says: "Elî is alive," he fears and does not come out of the cave.

2022. 111. Demir qapi: Derrîyê hesin.
2022. 111. Demir qapi: Iron door.

2023. Gotin bi tirkî ye.
2023. The saying is in Turkish.

2024. 112. Alt ke: Tê bibe.
2024. 112. Alt ke: To defeat.

2025. Peyv bi tirkî ye.
2025. The word is in Turkish.

2303. ## QEWLÊ ASOQ, MASOQÊ SURÊ
2303. ## QEWL OF THE LOVER AND BELOVED OF THE MYSTERY

2304. 1. Aşoq maşoqê surrê,
2304. 1. Lover and beloved of the mystery,

2305. Yarek divê vê herfê me mukurê,
2305. A friend must confess these words of ours,

2306. Hûn binêrin çika durr e ji padşê ye, yan padṣayî ji durrê?
2306. Look whether the pearl is from the king, or the kingship from the pearl?

2307. 2. Aşiqê êrfê çê ye,
2307. 2. The lover of the good custom,

2308. Timtêşa me vê cavê ye,
2308. Our manner is this answer,

2309. Hûn binêrin çika durr e ji padşê ye, yan padşayî ji durrê ye?
2309. Look whether the pearl is from the king, or the kingship from the pearl?

2310. 3. Aşiqo, ‘êrfê zana,
2310. 3. O lover, the custom of the wise,

2311. Yarek divê vê herfê me bide beyan e,
2311. A friend must declare these words of ours,

2312. Durr text e, padşaê min lê girtîye mikan e.
2312. The pearl is a throne, my king has taken a place upon it.

2313. 4. Padşaê min durr ji xwe çêkir,
2313. 4. My king created the pearl from himself,

2314. Sêwirand, kewirand, ber vê kir,
2314. Designed it, sculpted it, put it before this,

2315. Seîdî, se[y]îran dey lê kir.
2315. He made bliss and wandering upon it.

2316. 5. Padşaê min durr ji xwe wevare,
2316. 5. My king separated the pearl from himself,

2317. Qendîla me ye dar e,
2317. It is our lamp of wood,

2318. Ew qendîle nûr sitar e.
2318. That lamp is a star of light.

2319. 130. Meha nîsana sala 1976an li gundê Şamîranê yê li ser nehîyeya Aştaraka Ermenistanê ji zarê Zaîlê Şêx Keleşî hatîye nivîsîn.
2319. 130. Written down in the month of April of the year 1976 in the village of Shamiran in the Ashtarak district of Armenia from the mouth of Zaîl son of Şêx Keleş.

2320. Çap bûye bi navê “Qewlê Şêxûbekir"î li "Zargotina kurda".
2320. Printed under the name "Qewl of Şêxûbekir" in "Folklore of the Kurds".

2321. Cild. I., Yêrêvan, r. 378-381.
2321. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 378-381.

2322. 131. Me mukurê: Let him confess to us, let him tell.

2323. 132. Cav: Answer.

2324. 133. vavare (bnb).
2324. 133. vavare (bnb).

2325. 6. Durr e ji kilima padşê,
2325. 6. The pearl is from the word of the king,

2326. Xerqê Şix Adî derketîye jê,
2326. The cloak of Şix Adi has emerged from it,

2327. 'Ewlinde mêra silam e lê.
2327. First the men greet it.

2328. 7. Ji durrê derketîye xerq e,
2328. 7. From the pearl emerged a cloak,

2329. Pê Şam zeînandîye hetanî Şerq e,
2329. By it Damascus was adorned all the way to the East,

2330. Şix Adi dey li Şêxûbekir kir, go: "Hilîl û ber[k] ke."
2330. Şix Adi called to Şêxûbekir, he said: "Make it lawful and blessed."

2331. Şêxûbekir go: "Ezîzê min, ez vê yekê hewce me, Hemû mal zêrê xwe bide me, Hemû oxira xerqê Şîx Adî heq nezer bide min."
2331. Şêxûbekir said: "My dear one, I am in need of this one, give us all wealth and your gold, for the sake of the cloak of Şîx Adî give me a true glance."

2332. Şêxûbekir go: "Ezîzê min, ez yekê gudêr im, Çendîk mal zêrê xwe pê bidêrim, Hemû oxira xerqê Şix Adî heq nezer bispêrim."
2332. Şêxûbekir said: "My dear one, I am a manager of one, however much wealth and your gold I offer to it, for the sake of the cloak of Şix Adî I will entrust a true glance."

2333. 10. Padşaê min vê yekê diqebiland,
2333. 10. My king accepted this one,

2334. Îndlîsî Xeyat xerqe anî fesiland,

2335. Feqîra vê ra diniqiland.

2336. 11. Vê ra diniqiland feqîra,
2336. 11. He was embroidering it for the faqir,

2337. Herçi kesê berê xwe bide xirava, fêrya, 'êrya,
2337. Whoever turns his face to the ruins, learning, wandering,

2338. Wê xelat bike wan mifta, wan kilîla.
2338. He will gift those keys, those locks.

2339. 12. Ew kilil in, ew mifte ne,
2339. 12. They are locks, they are keys,

2340. 134. Dieqbiland: Qebûl dikir.

2341. Qebilandin.

2404. 1. Destûrî malê bava,

2418. Xasa hay kir, xafila kor bûn, agirê xezebê da disojin.

2548. ## QEWLÊ BEHRA
2548. ## QEWL OF THE SEA

2549. 1. Rojekê difikirim şevan û roja,
2549. 1. One day I think nights and days,

2550. Damamekê digrim li ber xwe da.
2550. I hold a breath before myself.

2551. 2. Çi behreke mezin e,
2551. 2. What a great sea,

2552. Qendîleke je bê bin e,
2552. A lamp from it is bottomless,

2553. Çar cewê jê çûne.
2553. Four streams have gone from it.

2554. 3. Çi behreke qeyas e,
2554. 3. What an immense sea,

2555. Ruknek e, çar asas e,
2555. It is a pillar, four foundations,

2556. Çar asas e, rûknekî,
2556. Four foundations, one pillar,

2557. Xaliqê xasê dîwanê Şîx Adî kuzivetê livas e.
2557. The special Creator of the court of Şîx Adî is the adornment of dress.

2558. 4. Çi behreke bêhed e,
2558. 4. What a limitless sea,

2559. Padşê mêrayî semend e,
2559. The king of men is eternal,

2560. Medeta şêxê xwe me,
2560. I am the help of my sheikh,

2561. 151. Meha kanûna paş sala 1973an li gundê Mûradtepeyê yê li ser nehîyeya Abovyana -niha ser nehîyeya Naîrîyê- Ermenistanê ji zarê Eylazê Pîr Reşoyî hatîye nivîsîn.
2561. 151. Written down in the month of January of the year 1973 in the village of Muradtepe in the Abovyan district -now the Nairi district- of Armenia from the mouth of Eylaz son of Pîr Reşo.

2562. Ev qewl, qewlê Mala Omer Xalan e, Omer Xalan hemû ji malên Şêxan tên hesabkirin wekî mala mezin.
2562. This qewl is the qewl of the House of Omer of Xala, all of Omer of Xala are counted among the houses of the Sheikhs as a great house.

2563. Loma jî mala Omer Xalan ra dibêjin Mala Bava.
2563. Therefore, the house of Omer of Xala is called the House of Fathers.

2564. Şaxeka vî qewlî bi sernivîsara "Beyta Be'ra" sala 1956an me ji zarê Cerdoê Esedî nivîsî, yê ko cimaet hesab dike wekî afirandineka Feqîyê Teyranî.
2564. A variant of this qewl under the title "Beyt of the Sea" we wrote down in the year 1956 from the mouth of Cerdo son of Esed, which the community considers as a creation of Feqîyê Teyranî.

2565. Cudatî di nava van her du afiranan da hem ji alîyê cureyê nivîsarê û hem jî ji alîyê nîyeta wê ve heye.
2565. There is a difference between these two creations both in terms of the type of writing and in terms of its intention.

2566. Dibe ku Feqîyê Teyranî "Qewlê Be'ra" veçêkiribe û di nava cimaetê da ew afirandin bi vî cureyî belav bûbe û gihîştibe me.
2566. Perhaps Feqîyê Teyranî remodeled the "Qewl of the Sea" and among the community that creation spread in this form and reached us.

2567. Dibe ku cimaetê bi xwe ew qewl veguhastibe û navê Feqîyê Teyranî lê kiribe?
2567. Perhaps the community itself transmitted that qewl and attached the name of Feqîyê Teyranî to it?

2568. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda."
2568. Printed in "Folklore of the Kurds."

2569. Cildê. II., Moskova, r. 51-53; Her ew qewl bi tîpên latînî û bi wergêra ser zimanê îngilîzî çap bûye: Kreyenbroek P.G, Yezidism, 1995, r. 202-207.
2569. Volume II, Moscow, pp. 51-53; This same qewl has been printed in Latin letters and with an English translation: Kreyenbroek P.G, Yezidism, 1995, pp. 202-207.
