2954. Heça cihalê nevsa xwe bike xeza,
2954. Whoever makes an expedition against his ignorant ego,

2955. Mîrê qelendera, mîr hereher e,
2955. Prince of qalandars, prince forever,

2956. Laliş ya bor, dîwan ya bor, merge ya bor, ya bor, ya bor,
2956. Laliş is the grey horse, the court is the grey horse, the meadow is the grey horse, the grey horse, the grey horse,

2957. Ya hêkimî pîrano,
2957. O ruler of the pirs,

2958. Dîwanê Şîx Alê Şemsa heq û ciza,
2958. In the court of Şîx Al of Şems is truth and penalty,

2959. Ax, li min e.
2959. Oh, woe is me.

2960. Çima dibêjin: Şêx Zeydîn yeka bêwusul kir,
2960. Why do they say: Şêx Zeydîn did a thing without method,

2961. Ne bi qewlê Xwedê û resûl kir,
2961. He did neither by the word of God nor the messenger,

2962. Kêwrûşk ji bin 'hulê merebî derxist û şerjê kir.
2962. He brought out the rabbit from under the cloak of the guide and slaughtered it.

2963. Lew merebî nifir lê kir,
2963. Therefore the guide cursed him,

2964. Şîx Adî nifira merebî qebûl kir,
2964. Şîx Adî accepted the curse of the guide,

2965. Şêx Zeydîna avîte pişt heft behrê şîna,
2965. He threw Şêx Zeydîn behind seven blue seas,

2966. Ma li hizreta Lalişa Nûranîya.
2966. He remained longing for Laliş the Luminous.

2967. Bavê Şêx Zeydin, Şêx Hesen bû.
2967. The father of Şêx Zeydîn was Şêx Hesen.

2968. Wextê Eyda Hecîya da, dikevê cûmaya Şix Adî, Şêx Zeydin Zendîn rabû mektub nivîsî şande bavê xwe ra.
2968. During the time of the Festival of Pilgrims, which falls on the Friday of Şîx Adî, Şêx Zeydîn Zendîn rose and wrote a letter and sent it to his father.

2969. Şîx Adî û Şêx Hesen li gelîyê Lalişê bûn, ew li zîndanê bû, pişt heft behra.
2969. Şîx Adî and Şêx Hesen were in the valley of Laliş, he was in prison, behind seven seas.

2970. Çima ketibû hebsê?
2970. Why had he fallen into prison?

2971. Şêx Zeydîn nêçîrvan bû, da pey kewrûşkê, Şêxûbekir li devê Kanîya Spî bû, 'hulê xwe danîbû, dest rûyê xwe cuwan dikir.
2971. Şêx Zeydîn was a hunter, he chased a rabbit, Şêxûbekir was at the edge of the White Spring, he had placed his cloak, he was washing his hands and face.

2972. Kêwrûşk hat kete bin 'hulê Şêxûbekir.
2972. The rabbit came and fell under the cloak of Şêxûbekir.

2973. Şêx Zeydîn hat kewrûşk ji bin 'hulê derxist û serê wê jê kir.
2973. Şêx Zeydîn came, brought the rabbit out from under the cloak and cut off its head.

2974. Şêxûbekir gilîyê wî cem Şîx Adî kir.
2974. Şêxûbekir complained about him to Şîx Adî.

2975. Şîx Adî gilîyê wî qebûl kir û avîte pişt heft behra.
2975. Şîx Adî accepted his complaint and threw him behind seven seas.

2976. Şêxê şemsa teyrê wanî bazî hebû.
2976. The Sheikh of Şems had a falcon bird.

2977. Her car gava Şêx Zeydîn kevokê xwe bi mektûbê dişand, ew bazî dadida pey kevoka û nedihişt mektub bînin bidin destê Şêx Hesen.
2977. Every time when Şêx Zeydîn sent his pigeon with a letter, that falcon swooped after the pigeons and did not let them bring the letter and give it to the hand of Şêx Hesen.

2978. Roja eydê bû bazê xwe bernedan, kevok hat li ber Şêx Hesen sekinî, mektub jê vekir û xwand.
2978. It was the day of the festival they did not release their falcon, the pigeon came and stood before Şêx Hesen, he opened the letter from it and read it.

2979. Hêsirek ji çavê wî ket.
2979. A tear fell from his eye.

2980. Şîx Adî
2980. Şîx Adî

2981. got: "Ma tu divê ez wî bînim?"
2981. said: "Do you want me to bring him?"

2982. Go: "Bine."
2982. He said: "Bring him."

2983. Wextê ku Şêx Zeydin anîn, Şêx Zeydin çû destê bavê xwe, necu deste Şix Adi.
2983. When they brought Şêx Zeydîn, Şêx Zeydîn went to the hand of his father, he did not go to the hand of Şîx Adî.

2984. Dilê Şix Adi jè ma, bù komek ax ù werya ser erde.
2984. The heart of Şîx Adî was offended by him, he became a pile of earth and scattered on the ground.

2985. Şêx Hesen rabu rahişte wê axê û pê leist, mijúl bû.
2985. Şêx Hesen rose, picked up that earth and played with it, he became occupied.

2986. Rabu Şix Adi dey li wè axê kir, bù deqê mêra.
2986. Şîx Adî rose, struck that earth, it became the spot of men.

2987. Şêx Zeydin go: "Heta ez heme, ez deqê mêra me, ez li gèdûkê me, ez nahèlim şêxê şemsa saxi ser mi ra derbaz bin."
2987. Şêx Zeydîn said: "As long as I exist, I am the spot of men, I am at the pass, I will not let the sheikhs of Şems pass over me alive."

2988. Û rastî divên ji wê gèdûkê va şemsani nikare derbaz be, ji derba deqê mêra dikevin.
2988. And truly they say from that pass a Şemsanî cannot pass, they fall from the blow of the spot of men.

2989. Li Şengalê, li gèduka ber bi Simoqiya, nêzîkî hidûdê Sûryayê.
2989. In Sinjar, at the pass towards Simoqîya, near the border of Syria.

2990. Ziyaretek heye bi qube, jê ra divên Quba Deqê Mêra. 176
2990. There is a shrine with a dome, they call it the Dome of the Spot of Men.

2991. Şaxeka vê efsaneyê ya nû, ku gelekî balkêş e Babe Feqîr anîye ser zar û di kovara "Roj"è da çap kirîye.
2991. A new variant of this legend, which is very interesting, Babe Feqîr has brought to the tongue and printed in the magazine "Roj".

2992. Naveroka wê ev e:
2992. Its content is this:

2993. Dibêjin, Şêx Zendîn Zeydin, kurê Şêx Hesen, rokê bêy dilê bavê xwe hespê wî yê qudretê sîyar bû, jê ra sura hespê vebû: Erş û kursi, ga û mehsî xuya bûn.
2993. They say, Şêx Zendîn Zeydin, son of Şêx Hesen, one day without his father's heart rode his horse of power, the mystery of the horse opened to him: Throne and pedestal, bull and fish appeared.

2994. Ji vê xwe mezin dît, kubar bu, ji Lalişê derket çû pişt ava mezin Diclê cîkî, ser erdekî rûnişt, sê qube ava kirin, dorê gundek ava kir, naka jî ew gund heye, jê ra divêjin Zendin, xelqê ra got: "Lalişa pîroz ev der e û êzdî divê li vir tewafa xwe bikin."
2994. From this he saw himself as great, became proud, left Laliş, went behind the great water of the Tigris to a place, sat on a land, built three domes, built a village around it, even now that village exists, they call it Zendin, he said to the people: "Holy Laliş is this place and Yazidis must make their pilgrimage here."

2995. Şêx Zendîn her gav diçû nêçîrê.
2995. Şêx Zendîn always went hunting.

2996. Rokê kêwrûşkek ji ber wî direve.
2996. One day a rabbit flees before him.

2997. Direve tê Lalişa pîroz.
2997. It flees and comes to Holy Laliş.

2998. Şêx Zendîn dide pey tê.
2998. Şêx Zendîn follows and comes.

2999. Ber hewed avê Pîr Omer Xala, merebîyê Şêx Zendîn, serçavê xwe dişûşt, kêwrûşk tê dikeve bin hilê wî, xwe vedişêre.
2999. By the pool of water Pîr Omer Xala, the guide of Şêx Zendîn, was washing his face, the rabbit comes and falls under his cloak, hides itself.

3000. Şêx Zendin bêy dilê merebîyê xwe, kêwrûşkê ji binê hilê derdixe û serê wî jê dike.
3000. Şêx Zendin without the heart of his guide, brings the rabbit out from under the cloak and cuts off its head.

3001. Pîr Omer Xala ser kirina Şêx Zêndîn gazinê xwe ber Şîx Adî dike.
3001. Pîr Omer Xala makes his complaint before Şîx Adî about the action of Şêx Zendîn.

3002. Şîx Adî wî sirgûn dike, davêje hebsa Misiré.
3002. Şîx Adî exiles him, throws him into the prison of Egypt.

3003. Şêx Zendîn ji hebsê bi kevotkên xwe nama dişîne bavê xwe ra, dixwaze ser rewşa xwe bavê xwe agahdar ke, ku ber Şîx Adi bigere û ji zindanê xilas ke.
3003. Şêx Zendîn from the prison sends a letter to his father with his pigeons, he wants to inform his father about his situation, so that he pleads before Şîx Adî and saves him from prison.

3004. Kurê Şêx Şims, her cara dibûn baz û xwe berdidan ezmana kevotka digirtin, nedihîştin nama bighînin Şêx Hesen.
3004. The sons of Şêx Şims, every time became falcons and threw themselves from the sky and caught the pigeons, they did not let them deliver the letter to Şêx Hesen.

3005. Carêkê roja cijna serê nîsanê, gava lawê Şê x
3005. Once on the day of the New Year festival in April, when the sons of Şê x

3006. 176. Go Pir Ali, pîrê çêlka, 03.03.1992 di mala pêşîmamî da, li Weyldenhauzê, Almanyayê.
3006. 176. Said Pîr Ali, the pir of the branch, 03.03.1992 in the house of the peshimam, in Wildeshausen, Germany.

3007. Şims cijne va giro bûn Şêx Zêndîn kevotka xwe bi nama berdide, kevotk tê dighîje Şêx Hesen.
3007. Şims were occupied with the festival, Şêx Zendîn releases his pigeon with the letter, the pigeon comes and reaches Şêx Hesen.

3008. Bav nama dixûne, diçe ber Şîx Adi lawa dike, kur jê ra xuya bike.
3008. The father reads the letter, goes before Şîx Adî and pleads, that the son appears to him.

3009. Şix Adî Şêx Zêndîn jê ra xuya dike, lê aza nake.
3009. Şîx Adî makes Şêx Zendîn appear to him, but does not free him.

3010. Şêx Hesen di fikra da bi axa ber xwe dikola, mijûl bû.
3010. Şêx Hesen in thought was digging the earth before him, he became occupied.

3011. Şîx Adî ew ax dike qalibek û ruhê kurê wî dike navê, divê eva kurê te ye.
3011. Şîx Adî makes that earth into a mold and puts the soul of his son into it, he says this is your son.

3012. Ji wê hingê jê ra divên Hesen Deqîq.
3012. From then on they call him Hesen Deqîq.

3013. Deqîq bi erebî mi mana ar, wê axê ra divên deqîq.
3013. Deqîq in Arabic means flour, they call that earth deqîq.

3014. Gorî çavkanîya Şêx Zeydîn kesekî dîrokî ye û gelekî jî navdar bûye.
3014. According to sources, Şêx Zeydîn is a historical person and became very famous.

3015. Zanyarên ola îslamî li ser wî gelek nivîsîne.
3015. Scholars of the Islamic religion have written much about him.

3016. Divên şêxekî zana bûye û jiyana xwe bi derwêşî derbaz kirye.
3016. They say he was a knowledgeable sheikh and spent his life as a dervish.

3017. Ew kurê Şêx Mehmedê kurê Şêx Hesenê kurê Şîx Adîyê dudya bûye.
3017. He was the son of Şêx Mehmed son of Şêx Hesen son of Şîx Adî the second.

3018. Li sala 697 H. 1297/98 li hebsê mirye.
3018. He died in prison in the year 697 A.H. / 1297-98 A.D.

3019. Gorâ wî li bajarê Qahirê ye û ziyaretgeheka naskirî ye.
3019. His tomb is in the city of Cairo and is a well-known shrine.

3020. Çima Şêx Şims ra dibêjin, Şêx Şimsê Teter yan jî Şêx Şimsê Tewrêzî?
3020. Why do they call Şêx Şims, Şêx Şims the Tatar or Şêx Şims of Tabriz?

3021. Ji xelkê Azirbeycanê ra berê digotin teter, yan jî azerî.
3021. To the people of Azerbaijan they formerly said Tatar, or Azeri.

3022. Tewrêz bajarekî bingehîn bûye ji bona azerîyan.
3022. Tabriz was a foundational city for the Azeris.

3023. Şêx Şims yan gelek sala li Tewrêzê jîye, yan jî bi xwe ji wî welatî ji Îranê hatîye Lalişê.
3023. Şêx Şims either lived many years in Tabriz, or he himself came from that country from Iran to Laliş.

3024. Dibêjin carekê Şêx Şims qehirî ji Lalişê çû Tewrêzê.
3024. They say once Şêx Şims became angry and went from Laliş to Tabriz.

3025. Seva çi?
3025. For what?

3026. Şêx Hesen go: "Êzîdî berê xwe bidin qubletê."
3026. Şêx Hesen said: "Let Yazidis turn their faces to the Qibla."

3027. Şêx Şims go: "Lazim e êzîdî berê xwe bidine Şerq, dia xwe bikin."
3027. Şêx Şims said: "It is necessary that Yazidis turn their faces to the East, make their prayers."

3028. Deng li Şemsanîyê kir.
3028. He called upon the Şemsanîs.

3029. Heftê hezar şemsanîyê rakir çû Tewrêzê danî.
3029. He raised seventy thousand Şemsanîs and went and settled in Tabriz.

3030. Heft sala li Tewrêzê ma.
3030. He remained in Tabriz for seven years.

3031. Piştî heft sala mêr çûne hizûra Şîx Adî, gotine Şix Adî, go: "Ezîzê me, Şêx Şims mêrê dîvanê heke neê dayîrê, dîwan nakamile."
3031. After seven years the men went to the presence of Şîx Adî, they said to Şîx Adî, they said: "Our dear one, Şêx Şims the man of the court, if he does not come to the circle, the court is not complete."

3032. Evdilqadir Rehman, birayê Şêx Ş ims
3032. Evdilqadir Rehman, brother of Şêx Ş ims

3033. 177. Binhêre Al-Domloci; Dr.Al-Sami Seyid al-Ehmed, Roj, Num. 2. r. 23.
3033. 177. See Al-Domloci; Dr. Al-Sami Seyid al-Ehmed, Roj, No. 2, p. 23.

3034. Efsaneya ku me li jorê anî, rastîyekê li ber me vedike, ku bi xwe gelekî balkêş e, ji ber ku di bingehê da bûyereka dîrokî heye.
3034. The legend that we brought above opens a truth before us, which in itself is very interesting, because at its base there is a historical event.

3035. Ji vê efsaneyê ji me ra xuya dibe ku di navbera mala Adiyan û Şemsanîyê da li ser rêberîya diyanetê nakokiyeka mezin hebûye.
3035. From this legend it appears to us that between the house of the Adîs and the Şemsanîs there was a great conflict over the leadership of the religion.

3036. Adanîyan xwestîye mezinahîya li ser ola êzdîyan bigirin destê xwe.
3036. The Adanîs wanted to take the greatness over the Yazidi religion into their own hands.

3037. Şêx Zendîn dîtîye ku şemsanî di Lalişa pîroz da xurt in, xwestiye bingeheka nû ya diyanetê veke û bala Êzdîxanê ji Lalisa pîroz bikişîne ser ziyareta nu.
3037. Şêx Zendîn saw that the Şemsanîs are strong in holy Laliş, he wanted to open a new base of religion and draw the attention of Êzdîxan from holy Laliş to the new shrine.

3038. Xuya ye, ev kirin ne bi dilê Êzdîxanê bûye û Şêx Zêndîn mecbur bûye ji Kurdistanê dûr bikeve, here Misirê û li wê derê ji ber bîr û bawerîya xwe ketiye hepsê.
3038. It is apparent, this action was not to the heart of Êzdîxan and Şêx Zendîn was forced to move away from Kurdistan, go to Egypt and there because of his thoughts and beliefs fell into prison.

3039. i axretê bû.
3039. of the hereafter.

3040. Wê hingê Şix Adi deng kir Ebdilqadir Rehmani, go: "Evdilqadir Rehmani?"
3040. At that time Şîx Adî called out to Evdilqadir Rehmanî, he said: "Evdilqadir Rehmanî?"

3041. Go: "Belê."
3041. He said: "Yes."

3042. Go: "Tê herî dû Şêx Şims."
3042. He said: "You will go after Şêx Şims."

3043. Go: "Nae".
3043. He said: "He will not come."

3044. Go: "We were."
3044. He said: "He will come."

3045. Go: "Naê."
3045. He said: "He will not come."

3046. Go: "Heke nehat, tê çi bêji?"
3046. He said: "If he does not come, what will you say?"

3047. Go: "Ezê çi bêjim?"
3047. He said: "What will I say?"

3048. Go: "Tè bêjî, roke çî ye? Go, wê hingê Şex Şims were."
3048. He said: "You will say, what is the day? He said, then Şêx Şims will come."

3049. Evdilqadir Rehmanî bûye teyrê baz, çû serê xwe da ser kevirê derîyê Şêx Şims.
3049. Evdilqadir Rehmanî became a falcon bird, went and put his head on the stone of the door of Şêx Şims.

3050. Go: "Ya Şêx Şimsê Êzdîna."
3050. He said: "O Şêx Şims of Êzdîn."

3051. Go: "Belê."
3051. He said: "Yes."

3052. Go: "Sedil seûdê member gotye bira nesekine bê.”
3052. He said: "The lord of happiness of the pulpit has said let him not stop, let him come."

3053. Go: "Naêm."
3053. He said: "I will not come."

3054. Go: "Te weri."
3054. He said: "You must come."

3055. Go: "Ez naêm."
3055. He said: "I will not come."

3056. Go: "Roke ji çî ye?
3056. He said: "What is the day of?"

3057. Go: "Here, ez ê hatim."
3057. He said: "Go, I am coming."

3058. Gava Evdilqadir Rehmani hate hizûra Şîx Adî, bala xwe da Şêx Şimsi berî wî li hizûra Şîx Adî ye.
3058. When Evdilqadir Rehmanî came to the presence of Şîx Adî, he noticed Şêx Şims before him is in the presence of Şîx Adî.

3059. Şêx Şims û Şêx Hesen avîtine ber hevdu.
3059. Şêx Şims and Şêx Hesen argued with each other.

3060. Şêx Hesen go: "Lazim e êzîdî berê xwe bidine qubletê."
3060. Şêx Hesen said: "It is necessary that Yazidis turn their faces to the Qibla."

3061. Şêx Şims go: "Wê berê xwe bidne Şerq, dua xwe bikin.
3061. Şêx Şims said: "They will turn their faces to the East, make their prayers.

3062. Şeva 12ê şebanê, eva eydekî miqedes e, ew pênc hezar sal e vê eydê em dikine eyd, em êvar da radibin, ranazên heta sibê em dikine eyd, ser me ferz e.
3062. The night of the 12th of Sha'ban, this is a sacred festival, it is five thousand years we make this festival a festival, we rise in the evening, we do not sleep until morning we make festival, it is obligatory upon us.

3063. Şeva 15ê şebanê şêxê Şêx Hesena wê berê xwe bidne qubletê, nimêja xwe bikin, qewalê defê lê bixerînin, şêxê şemsa sicadê ji bin birevînin, heta roja îro şêxê Şêx Hesena wê şevê heyra wan newêrin herin zîyareta, nimêja xwe bikin.
3063. On the night of the 15th of Sha'ban the sheikhs of Şêx Hesen will turn their faces to the Qibla, make their prayer, the Qawals will play the tambourine, the sheikhs of Şems will snatch the prayer rug from underneath, until today the sheikhs of Şêx Hesen that night do not dare to go to the shrines, to make their prayer.

3064. Li vê sebabê Şêx Şimsî Tewrêzî bû hate Lalişê.
3064. For this reason Şêx Şims became of Tabriz and came to Laliş.

3065. Sebeb ev e."
3065. The reason is this."

3066. ## QEWLÊ BOREBORÊ-II
3066. ## QEWLÊ BOREBORÊ-II

3067. 1. Şêx Hesen sultan e,
3067. 1. Şêx Hesen is a sultan,

3068. Bavêje qelpekî rehman e,
3068. He casts a merciful heart,

3069. Şîx Adî hemû derdan [y]î derman e.
3069. Şîx Adî is the cure for all pains.

3070. 2. Şêxê Hesen feqîr e,
3070. 2. Şêx Hesen is a faqir,

3071. Bavêje qelpekî mîr e,
3071. He casts a prince's heart,

3072. Şîx Adî hemû derdan [y]î xebîr e.
3072. Şîx Adî is aware of all pains.

3073. 3. Şêxê Hesen mezin e,
3073. 3. Şêx Hesen is great,

3074. Bavêje qelpekî momin e,
3074. He casts a faithful heart,

3075. Miraza mirazxaza qapîya melek Şîxisn e, cîyê gilî, gazina.
3075. The wish of the wish-seekers is the gate of Melek Şîxisn, the place of complaints and grievances.

3076. 4. Şêxê Hesen sehîd e,
3076. 4. Şêx Hesen is a lord,

3077. Bavêje qelpekî mirîd e,
3077. He casts a disciple's heart,

3078. Miraza mirazxaza qapıya sultan Êzîd e.
3078. The wish of the wish-seekers is the gate of Sultan Êzîd.

3079. 5. Şêxê Hesen emer e,
3079. 5. Şêx Hesen is a commander,

3080. Xaliqekî min î herbiher e,
3080. My Creator forever and ever,

3081. Bê ferwara Şix Adî cizareta ruh nehate ber e.
3081. Without the decree of Şîx Adî the body of the soul does not come forth.

3082. 6. Şêxê Hesen esed e,
3082. 6. Şêx Hesen is a lion,

3083. Bavêje qelpekî semend e,
3083. He casts an eternal heart,

3084. Bê ferwara Şîx Adî cizareta ruh nehete ber e.
3084. Without the decree of Şîx Adî the body of the soul does not come forth.

3085. 178. Meha tebaxê sala 1975an li bajarê Tibilîsîyê ji zarê Tefûrê Şêx Mehmûd hatîye nivîsîn.
3085. 178. Written down in the month of August of the year 1975 in the city of Tbilisi from the mouth of Tefûr son of Şêx Mehmûd.

3086. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".

3199. ## QEWLÊ BOREBORÊ-III
3199. ## QEWLÊ BOREBORÊ-III

3200. 1. Şêxe Heseni sultan e,
3200. 1. Şêx Hesen is a sultan,

3201. Bavêjî qelpè rehman e,
3201. He casts a merciful heart,

3202. Sultan Êzdîd hemû derda yî derman e.
3202. Sultan Êzdîd is the cure for all pains.

3203. 2. Şêxê Heseni cî de,
3203. 2. Şêx Hesen in his place,

3204. Bavêjî qelpê mirîd e,
3204. He casts a disciple's heart,

3205. Qapîyê miraza qapîyê sultan Êzdîd e.
3205. The gate of wishes is the gate of Sultan Êzdîd.

3206. 3. Şêxê Heseni feqîr e,
3206. 3. Şêx Hesen is a faqir,

3207. Bavêjî qelpê mîr e,
3207. He casts a prince's heart,

3208. Sultan Êzdîd hemû derda yî xebîr e.
3208. Sultan Êzdîd is aware of all pains.

3209. 186. Meha sibata sala 1973an li gundê Quruerezê -niha Yêrazxavûn- yê li ser nehiyeya Hoktembêryana Ermanistanê ji zarê Ahmedê Şêx Osêyî hatîye nivisin.
3209. 186. Written down in the month of February of the year 1973 in the village of Quruerez -now Yeraskhavun- in the Hoktemberyan district of Armenia from the mouth of Ahmed son of Şêx Osê.

3210. Evê qewlê tim du-sê tirêq tevahî dibêjin, çinku kubra wê zehf giran tê gotin.
3210. Always two or three paths say this qawl completely together, because its gravity is very heavy to recite.

3211. Ji bona tirêqekê zehf çetin e li pey hev gotin.
3211. For one path it is very difficult to recite it consecutively.

3212. Bi gotina Ahmedê Şêx Osêyî, sebeqeyên Qewlê Boreborê gelek hene.
3212. According to the words of Ahmed son of Şêx Osê, there are many stanzas of Qewlê Boreborê.

3213. Qewl bi xwe gelek dirêj e.
3213. The qawl itself is very long.

3214. Qewlê Boreborê feqi Dûko hînî Ahmedê Osêyî kirîye.
3214. Faqi Duko taught Qewlê Boreborê to Ahmed son of Şêx Osê.

3215. Ewî pêncî sebeqe hîn kirine, deh-duwazdeh sebeqe ji bîra Ahmedê Osêyî kûvî bûne.
3215. He taught fifty stanzas, ten to twelve stanzas have gone wild (escaped) from the memory of Ahmed son of Şêx Osê.

3216. Feqi Dúko li gundê Qerxûnê li ser nehîyeya Êçmîadzîna Ermenistanê dima, eva 30-40 sal e ew çûye rehmetê.
3216. Faqi Duko lived in the village of Qarkhun in the Echmiadzin district of Armenia, it has been 30-40 years since he went to mercy.

3217. Sebeqeya Qewlê Boreborê wexta bi kubir tê gotin, gotinên dîsgotinên wê ji sedî zêdetir dibin.
3217. When a stanza of Qewlê Boreborê is recited with gravity, the words of its refrains become more than a hundred.

3218. Mesela sebeqeya ewilîn weha tê gotin: "Şêxê Heseni sultan e, ay sultan e / Ezîzî mala bavê mino / Bavêjî qelpê rehman e / Mîrî qelendera, mîr her e, mîr her e / Laliş ya bor, merge ya bor, diwan ya bor/Ya bor, ya bor / Ya bi hekîmî mêra / Sultan Êzdîd hemû derda yî derman e."
3218. For example, the first stanza is recited thus: "Şêx Hesen is a sultan, oh a sultan / Dear of my father's house / He casts a merciful heart / Prince of qalandars, prince forever, prince forever / Laliş is the grey horse, the meadow is the grey horse, the court is the grey horse / The grey horse, the grey horse / O with the healing of men / Sultan Êzdîd is the cure for all pains."

3219. Qewlê Boreborê li ser mirîyan tê gotin, lê ne li ser hemû mirîyan.
3219. Qewlê Boreborê is recited over the dead, but not over all the dead.

3220. Mesela li ser kulfetan, li ser zaran, li ser cahilan nayê gotin.
3220. For example, it is not recited over women, over children, over the young.

3221. Ew her li ser mirovén binavûdeng, mirovên mêrxas û egid, mirovên biqedir tê gotin.
3221. It is only recited over renowned people, brave and valiant men, respected people.

3222. Evî qewlî bêyî xwestina xweyîyê mirîya nabêjin, qewlekî deman e, çetin e, kifş e, nav e, giran e.
3222. They do not recite this qawl without the request of the owner of the deceased, it is a qawl of times, difficult, well-known, famous, heavy.

3223. Kê mirîyê xwe layiq dit, ji tirêq dipirse, ku ew Qewlê Boreborê dizane bila li ser miriyê wî bibêje.
3223. Whoever deems his dead worthy, asks a path, that if he knows Qewlê Boreborê, let him recite it over his dead.

3224. Paşê xweyîyê mirîyî derdixe zêrekî yan tiştekî dide tirêq.
3224. Then the owner of the deceased brings out a gold coin or something and gives it to the path.

3225. Bi vî teherî jî "Qewlê Bav Bekirê Omera"yê tê gotin.
3225. In this manner, "Qewlê Bav Bekirê Omera" is also recited.

3226. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda."
3226. It has been printed in "Folklore of the Kurds."

3227. Cildê. II., Moskova, r. 40-43.
3227. Volume II, Moscow, pp. 40-43.

3228. 4. Şêx Hesen is great,

3229. He casts a faithful heart,

3231. 5. Şêx Hesen is a commander,

3232. My king forever and ever,

3233. The soul without the decree of God, its beauty and body do not come forth.

3248. 187. Semed e (bnb)

3250. 11. Wê quvé kim, surr e, ezmîn e,

3253. 12. We quvê kim, ser hemû quvan e,

3254. In it shine three hundred and sixty-six lamps,

3256. 13. Lalişa nûrîn xemê min dibirin,
3256. 13. Laliş the Luminous took away my sorrows,

3640. The branches of the qawl are distinguished from each other by the sentence of the first stanza.

3641. Pey sebeqeyekê yan jî pey sebeqeyan teşirma wê tê gotin: "Sultan e, Sultan e /Sultan Sultanê hey mêran e."
3641. After a stanza or after the stanzas its refrain is recited: "He is a Sultan, he is a Sultan / The Sultan is the Sultan of men."

3737. 1. Husêyîn e, Husêyînî Hellac e,

3740. 2. Xecê go: "Husêyîno, birao, vir mereve, Wê sive vira bive qal û ceng û şer e, Rev heye mêra ra 'êv e, 232 Serê te serîkî berhesêv e. 233"

3747. Pey her sebeqeyê tim tê gotin: "Çake, çake, çake cûda / Husêyîn çûye ser atqat, îmana xwe da."

3748. Ji sebeqeya 22an kubir tê guhastin, dîsgotin jî tê guhastin: "Zênar e, zênar e/ Şêxûbekiro, zênar e, hukumê feqîrîyê."
3748. From the 22nd stanza the rhythm is changed, the refrain is also changed: "It is a rock, it is a rock / O Şêxûbekir, it is a rock, the rule of the faqirs."

3749. Şêx gava gihîşt sebeqeya 22an, av ku radibe heyfê derxe, Şêx Mîrzeyî got: "Ji vê derê jî di nava cimaetê da bi pêş da hatîye gotina: "Heyfa Husêyînî Hellac e."

4123. Erefat e guşguş e,
4123. It is Arafat, it is roaring,

4124. Melek Ferxedîn halekî xaş e.
4124. Melek Ferxedîn is in a pleasant state.

4125. 2. Rojekê Hekarê, 260
4125. 2. One day in Hakkari,

4126. Mêr cema' dibûne mixare,
4126. The men were gathered in the cave,

4127. Melek Ferxedîn hatye ber ferwarê.
4127. Melek Ferxedîn came before the decree.

4128. 3. Rojekê me dînê,
4128. 3. One day in our religion,

4129. Mêr cema' dibûn xezînê,
4129. The men were gathered at the treasury,

4130. Sev xatirê bavê Stî Xatunê.
4130. For the sake of the father of Stî Xatun.

4131. 4. Rojekê xirûr e,
4131. 4. One day it is pride,

4132. Mêr cema' dibûne cindîyêd nûr e,
4132. The men were gathered as riders of light,

4133. Melek Ferxedîn hatye ber hizûr e.
4133. Melek Ferxedîn came into the presence.

4134. 5. Rojekê rojan e,
4134. 5. One day of days,

4135. Mêr cema' dibûne alimî zana ne,
4135. The men were gathered as knowing scholars,

4136. Werin mirinê bidin beyan e.
4136. Come and declare the death.

4137. 6. Dilê min î bi xem e,
4137. 6. My heart is with sorrow,

4138. 259. Meha tebaxê sala 1975an li bajarê Tibilîsîyê ji zarê Tefûrê Şêx Mehmûdî hatiye nivîsîn.
4138. 259. It was written down in the month of August of the year 1975 in the city of Tbilisi from the mouth of Tefûr son of Şêx Mehmûd.

4139. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".
4139. It has been printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

4140. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 329-337.

4141. 260. Heq warê (bnb).
4141. 260. Heq warê (bnb).

4142. Ez alima diperseme,
4142. I ask the scholars,

4143. Melek Ferxedin çarşemê bîye, çarşemê guhast qedem e. 261
4143. Melek Ferxedîn was born on Wednesday, on Wednesday he moved his step.

4144. 7. Rojekê Şam e,
4144. 7. One day it is Damascus,

4145. Dikir geriya çendî 'am e,
4145. The dhikr circulated among however many public,

4146. Melek Ferxedîn ser qudibê 262 temam e.
4146. Melek Ferxedîn is complete upon the pole.

4147. 8. Melek Ferxedîn ser qudibê bedhal e,
4147. 8. Melek Ferxedîn is in a bad state upon the pole,

4148. Mêr cema' dibûne wêlî û xal e,
4148. The men were gathered as saints and maternal uncles,

4149. Şêx Şims dibêje: “Ferxo ber mêra hilîne çev e."
4149. Şêx Şims says: "O Ferxo, lift your eyes before the men."

4150. 9. Şêx Şims divê, ji te mêra :
4150. 9. Şêx Şims says, from you men:

4151. "Eziz melek Ferxedîn bal lêra,
4151. "Dear Melek Ferxedîn is here,

4152. Vegerînin boy me xêra."
4152. Return the goodness for us."

4153. 10. Şêx Şims dibêje, we mêrsera: 263
4153. 10. Şêx Şims says, you chief men:

4154. "Berb' mal û zêrê xwe werne dera,
4154. "Leave your wealth and gold outside,

4155. Ezîz melek Ferxedîn vegerînin boy me ra."
4155. Return dear Melek Ferxedîn for us."

4156. 11. Sica deyn 264 dike vê ra:
4156. 11. Sica calls out to this:

4157. "Herge mal e, herge zêra,
4157. "Whether it is wealth, whether it is gold,

4158. Ez ê vegerînim boy xwe tenê ra."
4158. I will return him for myself alone."

4159. 12. Biraê nav Sica ye,
4159. 12. The brother whose name is Sica,

4160. Kewgirî û dama ye,
4160. He is weeping and mourning,

4161. 261. Gedeme (bnb).
4161. 261. Gedeme (bnb).

4162. 262. qudûmê (bnb).

4164. 264. Deng.
4164. 264. Deng (Voice).

4165. Şêx Ferxê Adya ra ta ye.
4165. He is a thread for Şêx Ferx of the Adîs.

4166. 13. Biraê nav Nasirdîn e,
4166. 13. The brother whose name is Nasirdîn,

4167. Hêsir rûya da ruhîne:
4167. Tears flow down his face:

4168. "Birao, biratî çiqas şêrîn e!?"
4168. "Brother, how sweet is brotherhood!?"

4169. 14. Biraê nav Nasir e,
4169. 14. The brother whose name is Nasir,

4170. Rûya da hat hêsir e:
4170. Tears came down his face:

4171. "Birao, bira kafira nemîne bêbira."
4171. "Brother, let not the infidels remain without a brother."

4172. 15. [Melek Fexredîn got:] "Birao, hûn biraê min in,
4172. 15. [Melek Fexredîn said:] "Brothers, you are my brothers,

4173. Tu nedra min negrin,
4173. Do not make any vows for me,

4174. Sehî ke ez ê bimirim."
4174. Know that I will die."

4175. 16. [Got:] "Mirin heqî ye,
4175. 16. [He said:] "Death is truth,

4176. Heçî kesê xo zanîye,
4176. Whoever has known himself,

4177. Ber mirinê nabin sergêrî ye."
4177. Before death they do not become dizzy."

4178. 17. "Ber mirinê nabin sergêr e,
4178. 17. "Before death they do not become dizzy,

4179. Heçî kesê vê ra,
4179. Whoever is with this,

4180. Ezîz melek Ferxedîn fihol kirin boy kinarê Xwedê ra."
4180. They made dear Melek Ferxedîn lawful for the edge of God."

4181. 18. [Got:] "Îlahîo, tu me bikî debra,
4181. 18. [He said:] "O Divine, may You give us patience,

4182. Bana da qebûl bikî nadra,
4182. May You accept the vows in the cries,

4183. Me sebir naê bê bira,"
4183. Patience does not come to us without a brother,"

4184. 19. [Got:] "Îlahio, mi ceber î,
4184. 19. [He said:] "O Divine, You are my restorer,

4185. Sebreke bana da bihenêrî,
4185. Send a patience in the cries,

4186. Şêx Ferxê Adya pê bihejmêrî."
4186. Count Şêx Ferx of the Adîs with it."

4187. 20. "Birao, hûn biraê min e zergûn in, 265
4187. 20. "Brothers, you are my pale brothers,

4188. Xatirê dilê min têk bivînin,
4188. Bring together the sake of my heart,

4189. Paşî min Şêx Mendê Ferxa neêşînin."
4189. After me do not hurt Şêx Mend of the Ferxs."

4190. 21. [Got:] "Birao, hûn biraê min e asasa,
4190. 21. [He said:] "Brothers, you are my foundational brothers,

4191. Bira Şêx Mendê Ferxa rûnî dîwanêd xasa,
4191. Let Şêx Mend of the Ferxs sit in the courts of the special ones,

4192. Eşqê her pênc terêqê wî bigerînin doran û kasa."
4192. For the love of his all five paths, pass around the rounds and the bowls."

4193. 22. Çi lawekî dêmur î,
4193. 22. What a boy of pearl-like face,

4194. Serê birrî naê kirrî, 266
4194. The cut head cannot be bought,

4195. Ezeta bavê bikin boy kurî.
4195. Do the honor of the father for the son.

4196. 23. Hetani ezî xaş bûm,
4196. 23. As long as I was well,

4197. Ez Ferxê reş bûm,
4197. I was the black Ferx,

4198. Ez berat û bexş bûm.
4198. I was a mandate and a gift.

4199. 24. Bexş bûme berat,
4199. 24. I was a gift and a mandate,

4200. Mi deng da çiqa welat,
4200. I gave voice to however many lands,

4201. Mi aşiq zor anî hatin kirin xelat.
4201. I brought much love, they were made a reward.

4202. 265. Zergún: Kesê ku rûyê wî/wê zerî ye.
4202. 265. Zergûn: The person whose face is yellowed.

4203. 266. démdurr (bnb).
4203. 266. dêmdurr (bnb).

4204. 25. [Got:] "Birao, hûn bira ne,
4204. 25. [He said:] "Brothers, you are brothers,

4205. Nik yek rewastane,
4205. Standing next to one another,

4206. Anemetî we sunetxan e.
4206. Your trust is the house of tradition.

4207. 26. Sunet rez e, hûn rezvan in,
4207. 26. Tradition is a vineyard, you are the vineyard keepers,

4208. Sunet rezê miqîmî ye,
4208. Tradition is a permanent vineyard,

4209. Tijî xox, tijî bî ye,
4209. Full of peaches, full of willows,

4210. Ber medne sûretê gulî ye.
4210. Before the meanings is the image of the rose.

4211. 27. Gulîya sunetê bigrin,
4211. 27. Grasp the lock of hair of the tradition,

4212. Heq rîya dînê sultan Êzîd bifikirin,
4212. Consider the true path of the religion of Sultan Êzîd,

4213. Hûn ê sêfîl Mala Adya pê bidebirin.
4213. You will sustain the orphans of the House of Adî with it.

4214. 28. Brao, hûn bira ne,
4214. 28. Brothers, you are brothers,

4215. Nik yek rawastane,
4215. Standing next to one another,

4216. Anemetî we malê xelîfetan e,
4216. Your trust is the house of the caliphs,

4217. Sev xatirê şerbik û çira ne."
4217. For the sake of the pitcher and the lamp."

4218. 29. [Got:] "Malêd xelîfeta bira mîr be,
4218. 29. [He said:] "Let the houses of the caliphs be a prince,

4219. Navmalîyê wana feqîr be,
4219. Let their household be a faqir,

4220. Pêşqedemê wanê bira şêx û pîr be."
4220. Let their vanguard be sheikh and pîr."

4221. 30. Divêjime we gelî şêxa û pîra,
4221. 30. I say to you, O sheikhs and pîrs,

4222. Bernedne fêrîêd mîra,
4222. Do not let go of the ways of the princes,

4223. 'Ebabetî kin feqîra.
4223. Serve the faqirs.

4224. 31. Ebabeti bikin xerqe ye,
4224. 31. Serve the cloak,

4225. Xizmeteke çek boy bikeye,
4225. Do a good service for it,

4226. Ew libsê bavê me ye.
4226. It is the garment of our father.

4227. 32. Bavê me ew libsî ber bû,
4227. 32. Our father had that garment on,

4228. Tacê nûranî ser bû,
4228. The luminous crown was on his head,

4229. Wê nûrê neder bû.
4229. That light did not disappear.

4230. 33. Dilê min î be ye,
4230. 33. My heart is a wind,

4231. Destê mi bigrin rakin ser qedemê me ye,
4231. Take my hand, raise me upon our feet,

4232. Birao, mi destûr e boy we ye.
4232. Brother, I have permission for you.

4233. 34. Dilê min bey dibêye,
4233. 34. My heart calls the wind,

4234. Ruh kişîya desta û pîya,
4234. The soul withdrew from the hands and feet,

4235. Ma çevnhêrîyê kesa û wêlîya.
4235. It remained anticipating the people and saints.

4236. 35. Qasidê rûhê min delal e,
4236. 35. The messenger of my soul is beloved,

4237. Sata ruhê min bire misqal misqal e,
4237. It took the time of my soul grain by grain,

4238. Sata ruhê min ma qalibekî vala.
4238. The time of my soul remained an empty body.

4239. 36. Qasidê rûhê min têcir e,
4239. 36. The messenger of my soul is a merchant,

4240. Sata rûhê min dibirre,
4240. He cuts the time of my soul,

4241. Birao, min destûr e, we xatir e.
4241. Brother, I have permission, you have farewell.

4242. 37. Borê minî beza,
4242. 37. My steed is running,

4243. Qasidê minî leza,
4243. My messenger is quick,

4244. Lezê xilaz nebim eza.
4244. Quickly I cannot be saved.

4245. 38. Lezê nabim xilaz,
4245. 38. Quickly I am not saved,

4246. Yek ser mi ra sekinîye, çevê wî weke tas,
4246. One has stood over me, his eyes like bowls,

4247. Tilî weke risas,
4247. Fingers like lead,

4248. Avrîyê wî weke almas,
4248. His tears like diamonds,

4249. Sed xazlîya min xelqê cahilî, bêgune î bêmisas.
4249. A hundred blessings upon the ignorant, sinless and flawless people.

4250. 39. Aqil bin xelqê cahêl,
4250. 39. Be wise, ignorant people,

4251. ‘Ebabet bikin quba helêl.
4251. Worship the lawful dome.

4252. 40. ‘Ebabet bikin quba nûr,
4252. 40. Worship the dome of light,

4253. 'Ebabet bikin ew şûr.
4253. Worship that sword.

4254. 41. Wê şûrê bikin 'ebabet,
4254. 41. Worship that sword,

4255. Çi maleke zoran hizret.
4255. What a house of great presence.

4256. 42. Eva mala mala baban e,
4256. 42. This house is the house of the fathers,

4257. Serekanîya çendî beran e,
4257. It is the source of however many rams,

4258. Dewra şêxan û pîran e.
4258. It is the era of the sheikhs and pîrs.

4259. 43. Caveke rast e, ne derew e,
4259. 43. It is a true eye, it is not a lie,

4260. Çevê ezîz melek Ferxedîn ma li hewa,
4260. The eyes of dear Melek Ferxedîn remained in the air,

4261. Bira tirê melek Ferxedîn wê li xewa.
4261. The brother thought Melek Ferxedîn is in sleep.

4262. 44. Sata melek Ferxedîn teyr difirî,
4262. 44. At the time of Melek Ferxedîn a bird was flying,

4263. Erd û ezman yek dixurî,
4263. Earth and sky were trembling together,

4264. Sitîya bedenê xwe dibirrî.
4264. The lady of his body was cutting herself.

4265. 45. Dibêjime we geli sitiya,
4265. 45. I say to you, O ladies,

4266. Dest nevêjine xûnmirîya,
4266. Do not lay hands upon the blood of the dead,

4267. Neherifinin kofiya,
4267. Do not ruin the headdresses,

4268. Şemsanî rabine pîya.
4268. Let the Şemsanîs rise to their feet.

4269. 46. Wê dibû şabaş e,
4269. 46. It was a praise,

4270. Mér cema' dibûn mîr û paşa,
4270. The men were gathered as princes and pashas,

4271. Melek Ferxedîn çû serdarê hemû neqaşa.
4271. Melek Ferxedîn went as the leader of all painters.

4272. 47. Wê dibû gişt e,
4272. 47. It was all,

4273. Qalibê melek Ferxedîn anîn şûşte,
4273. They brought the body of Melek Ferxedîn to the wash,

4274. Welgerandin ser tenişt e.
4274. They turned it on its side.

4275. 48. They turned it on its side,

4278. 49. They brought my shroud to measure,

4279. Qerqerê min gaz û nîva,
4279. My stature is an ell and a half,

4280. Beniademo, jaro, çi dinêke bîma.
4280. O son of Adam, poor one, what a moonless world.

4281. 50. Kefenê min hijde gaz e,
4281. 50. My shroud is eighteen ells,

4282. Danîn ser cinîyaze,
4282. They placed it upon the corpse,

4283. Ser digrîn wêlî û biraze.
4283. Over it weep the saints and nephews.

4284. 51. They founded my tomb,

4285. 267. bê hív e (bnb).

4286. They straightened my body within it,

4287. Wê rojê mala heqîyê xwe nas kir.

4288. 52. Birao, hûn biraê min e heqetê,
4288. 52. Brothers, you are my brothers of truth,

4289. Wê dikim nesîlhetê,
4289. I make this advice,

4290. Pêşîmamekî boy mi biketê,

4298. 55. The lovers say:

4301. 56. The brothers joined together and came home,

4329. ## QEWLÊ MELEK FERXEDÎN-II
4329. ## THE QAWL OF MELEK FERXEDÎN-II

4330. 1. Rojekê Laliş e,
4330. 1. One day it is Laliş,

4331. Erefat e, gujguj e,
4331. It is Arafat, it is roaring,

4332. Ezîz melek Ferxedîn halekê xaş e.
4332. Dear Melek Ferxedîn is in a pleasant state.

4333. 2. Rojekê me dînê,
4333. 2. One day in our religion,

4334. Mêr cema' bûn xezînê,
4334. The men were gathered at the treasury,

4335. Ser bavê Stî Xatunê.
4335. Upon the father of Stî Xatun.

4336. 3. Rojekê rojan e,
4336. 3. One day of days,

4337. Pirs kin kesekî 'êlimî zanan e,
4337. Ask someone who is a knowing scholar,

4338. Werin mirinê bidin beyan e.
4338. Come and declare the death.

4339. Rojekê xirûr e, lê cema' bûye cindîyê mîr e, ezîz melek Ferxedîn hatye ber hidûd e.
4339. One day it is pride, but the riders of the prince have gathered, dear Melek Ferxedîn has come before the boundary.

4340. 5. Dilê minî xem e,
4340. 5. My heart is with sorrow,

4341. We 'elema pirs bikene,
4341. You ask the scholars,

4342. Ezîz melek Ferxedîn çarşemê bû, çarşemê hilda qedem e.
4342. Dear Melek Ferxedîn was born on Wednesday, on Wednesday he lifted his step.

4343. 6. Rojekê li Şam e,
4343. 6. One day in Damascus,

4344. 269. Meha tebaxa sala 1975an li bajarê Tibilîsîyê ji zarê pîr Dodoê Xidirî hatîye nivîsîn.
4344. 269. It was written down in the month of August of the year 1975 in the city of Tbilisi from the mouth of Pîr Dodo son of Xidir.

4345. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".
4345. It has been printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

4346. Cildê I., Yêrêvan, r. 353-360; Eva qewla Hesen Temoyan bi wergera ser zimanê ermeni çap kiriye û negotîye ji ku hildaye.
4346. Volume I, Yerevan, pp. 353-360; Hesen Temoyan printed this qawl with a translation into the Armenian language and did not say where he took it from.

4347. Binêre: H. Temoyan Têkstên ola êzdîya.
4347. See: H. Temoyan, Texts of the Yezidi religion.

4348. Yêrêvan 2000, r. 6-23.
4348. Yerevan 2000, pp. 6-23.

4349. 270. gedem e (bnb).
4349. 270. gedem e (bnb).

4350. Dikir geriyabû hindî 'am e, ezîz melek Ferxedîn qulbê temam e.
4350. The dhikr had circulated among however many public, dear Melek Ferxedîn is the complete pole.

4351. 7. Şêx Şimso zerbav e,
4351. 7. Şêx Şims is the golden father,

4352. Ferxo, ber mêra hilîn çeve,
4352. O Ferxo, lift your eyes before the men,

4353. Te li me sot dil û hinav e.
4353. You have burned our heart and insides.

4354. 8. Şêx Şims divêje te mêra:
4354. 8. Şêx Şims says from you men:

4355. "Ezîz melek Ferxedîn wey lêra,
4355. "Dear Melek Ferxedîn is here,

4356. Hûn vegerin boy me gele xêra."
4356. Return much goodness for us."

4357. Şêx Şims divêje mêrsera: "Ezîz melek Ferxedîn wey lêra, Hûn vegerin boy me gele xêra."
4357. Şêx Şims says to the chief men: "Dear Melek Ferxedîn is here, return much goodness for us."

4358. 10. Biraê nav Sica ye,
4358. 10. The brother whose name is Sica,

4359. Kewgirî ye û dama ye,
4359. He is weeping and mourning,

4360. Biramo, qewî îro ezîz melek Ferxedînî ta ye.
4360. O my brother, indeed today dear Melek Ferxedîn is a thread.

4361. 11. Biraê nav Sicadîn e,
4361. 11. The brother whose name is Sicadîn,

4362. Hêsira rûya da ruhîne,
4362. Tears flow down his face,

4363. Biramo, biratî ça şîrin e?
4363. O my brother, how sweet is brotherhood?

4364. 12. Biraê nav Nasir e,
4364. 12. The brother whose name is Nasir,

4365. Rûya da hat hêsir e,
4365. Tears came down his face,

4366. Go: "Biramo, kafira jî nemire bira."
4366. He said: "O my brother, let not even the infidels die without a brother."

4367. 271. Biramo: Birayê mino!
4367. 271. Biramo: O my brother!

4368. 13. Go: "Îlahîo, tu ceber e,
4368. 13. He said: "O Divine, You are a restorer,

4369. Sebrekê baya bihinêre,
4369. Send a patience in the wind,

4370. Bira Şêx Mendê Ferxa pê bejmêre."
4370. Let Şêx Mend of the Ferxs be counted with it."

4371. 14. Go: "Îlahîo, tu me bikî debre, ban da qebûl bikî nedr e, me bê bira naê sebr e."
4371. 14. He said: "O Divine, may You give us patience, may You accept the vows in the cries, patience does not come to us without a brother."

4372. 15. Sica deng kire zêr e:
4372. 15. Sica called out to the gold:

4373. "Herke mal e, herke zêr e,
4373. "Whether it is wealth, whether it is gold,

4374. Ez ê ezîz melek Ferxedîn vegerînim boy xwe tenê ra."
4374. I will return dear Melek Ferxedîn for myself alone."

4375. 16. Melek Ferxedîn go: "Birao, biraê min in, tu nedra mi negirin, sihîd ez ê bimirim."
4375. 16. Melek Ferxedîn said: "Brothers, you are my brothers, do not make any vows for me, know that I will die."

4376. 17. [Go]: "Biramo, go, mirin heqî ye,
4376. 17. [He said]: "O my brother, he said, death is truth,

4377. Çi kesekî xwezanî ye,
4377. Whoever has known himself,

4378. Sergêr bo mirinê nîye.
4378. He is not dizzy for death.

4379. 18. Ber mirinê nave sergêr e,
4379. 18. Before death he does not become dizzy,

4380. Çi kesekî vê ra,
4380. Whoever is with this,

4381. Ezîz melek Ferxedîn ferhaê bikin boy kinarê Xwedê ra."
4381. Make dear Melek Ferxedîn joyful for the edge of God."

4382. 19. Nasiro go: "Biraê min e dêmdurr î,
4382. 19. Nasiro said: "My brother of pearl-like face,

4383. Serê birrî naê kirrîn,
4383. The cut head cannot be bought,

4384. 'Ezeta bavê bikin boy kurî."
4384. Do the honor of the father for the son."

4385. 20. [Go]: "Birao, go, biraê min e esasa,
4385. 20. [He said]: "Brothers, he said, you are my foundational brothers,

4386. Bira Şêx Mendê Ferxa rûnî dîwanê xasa,
4386. Let Şêx Mend of the Ferxs sit in the courts of the special ones,

4387. Eşqa yar-birê, axretê bigerîne dolyan û kasa."
4387. For the love of the friend-brother, let him pass around the ewers and the bowls of the afterlife."

4388. 21. Nasiro go: "Biraê min tu [y]î, xeysetê bi xu [y]î, paşî min Şêx Mendê Ferxa disûî."
4388. 21. Nasiro said: "You are my brother, you are with character, after me you will take care of Şêx Mend of the Ferxs."

4389. 22. Heta ez xaş bûm,
4389. 22. As long as I was well,

4390. Ez Ferxê reş bûm,
4390. I was the black Ferx,

4391. Berat û bexş bûm.
4391. I was a mandate and a gift.

4392. 23. Bexş bûm berat,
4392. 23. I was a gift and a mandate,

4393. Teg da çendî welat,
4393. I gave voice to however many lands,

4394. Mi zor aşiq dinê da kirine xelat.
4394. I made many lovers into a reward in the world.

4395. 24. [Go]: "Biramo, go, em bira ne,
4395. 24. [He said]: "O my brother, he said, we are brothers,

4396. Nik yêk da wastane,
4396. Standing next to one another,

4397. Anemetê we sunetxan e.
4397. Your trust is the house of tradition.

4398. 25. Sunet rez e, hûn rezvan in,
4398. 25. Tradition is a vineyard, you are the vineyard keepers,

4399. Sunet rezê ji dêr e,
4399. Tradition is a vineyard from long ago,

4400. Tije naz nehmet û xêr e,
4400. Full of grace, blessing and goodness,

4401. Heq riya Şîx Adî ew e şêxî lê bive sexbêr e.
4401. The true path of Şîx Adî is that the sheikh becomes its caretaker.

4402. 272. eşq yar (bnb).
4402. 272. eşq yar (bnb).

4403. 273. durran (bnb).
4403. 273. durran (bnb).

4404. 274. di sú yi (bnb).
4404. 274. di sú yi (bnb).

4405. 275. Lê bive sexbêr: Xweyîtîyê lê bike.
4405. 275. Lê bive sexbêr: To take care of it.

4406. 26. Sunet rezê qedîmî ye,
4406. 26. Tradition is an ancient vineyard,

4407. Tije xox e, tije bî ye,
4407. Full of peaches, full of willows,

4408. Bernedne sunetê gulî ye.
4408. Do not let go of the lock of hair of the tradition.

4409. 27. Gulîya jê vegrin,
4409. 27. Grasp the lock of hair from it,

4410. Heqîya rîya Şîx Adî tê bifikirin,
4410. Consider the truth of the path of Şîx Adî,

4411. Roja bandê sêfîl jarê me tê bidebirin.

4412. 28. Biramo, em bira ne,
4412. 28. O my brother, we are brothers,

4413. Nik yêk da wastane,

4414. Anemetê we malê xelîfeta ne."
4414. Your trust is the houses of the caliphs."

4415. 29. Go, "Bira malê xelîfeta mîr bin,
4415. 29. He said, "Let the houses of the caliphs be princes,

4416. Navmalîyê wan feqîr bin,
4416. Let their household be faqirs,

4417. Pêşqedemê wana şêx û pîr bin."
4417. Let their vanguard be sheikh and pîr."

4418. 30. Divêjime we gelî şêxan û pîra:
4418. 30. I say to you, O sheikhs and pîrs:

4419. "Bernedne fênîyêd mîra,
4419. "Do not let go of the ways of the princes,

4420. 'Ebabet bikin feqîra.
4420. Serve the faqirs.

4421. 31. ‘Ebabet bikin xerqe ye,
4421. 31. Serve the cloak,

4423. It is the garment of our father.

4424. 32. Bavê me ew libsî ber bû,
4424. 32. Our father had that garment on,

4425. Tacê nûrînî ser bû,
4425. The luminous crown was on his head,

4426. Wê nûrê va neder bû."
4426. By that light he did not disappear."

4427. 33. Dilê min î be ye,
4427. 33. My heart is a wind,

4428. Deste mi bigrin, mi rakine ser qedemê me ye,
4428. Take my hand, raise me upon our feet,

4429. Biramo, mi destûr e, xatirî cem we ye.
4429. O my brother, I have permission, the farewell is with you.

4430. 34. Dilê min î benduhî ye,
4430. 34. My heart is tied,

4431. Ruh çû ji destan û pî ye,
4431. The soul left the hands and feet,

4432. Qalib çevnihêrî bû kesan û wêlî ye.
4432. The body became expectant of the people and saints.

4433. 35. Caveke rast e ne derew e,
4433. 35. It is a true eye, it is not a lie,

4434. Çevê ezîz melek Ferxedîn mabû hewa
4434. The eyes of dear Melek Ferxedîn had remained in the air

4435. Bira tirê hê li xew e.
4435. The brother thought he is still in sleep.

4436. 36. Sata ruhê ezîz melek Ferxedîn tê dibirrî,
4436. 36. At the time the soul of dear Melek Ferxedîn was being cut,

4437. Erd û ezman lê dixurî,
4437. Earth and sky were trembling for it,

4438. Stîya hingê berîya xwe didirrî.
4438. The lady then was tearing her collar.

4439. 37. Divêjime we gelî stîya,
4439. 37. I say to you, O ladies,

4440. Dest nevêjine kofiya,
4440. Do not lay hands upon the headdresses,

4441. Neherifînin xwe mirîya,
4441. Do not ruin yourselves for the dead,

4442. Bira Şemsanî rabe pîya.
4442. Let the Şemsanîs rise to their feet.

4443. 38. Li wê bû şabaş e,
4443. 38. There it was a praise,

4444. Lê cema' bû mîrek û paşe,
4444. A prince and a pasha gathered there,

4445. Go: "Birin ezîz melek Ferxedîn nexaşê serê çendî nexaş e."
4445. They said: "They took dear Melek Ferxedîn the painter over however many painters."

4446. 39. Go: "Qasidê min têcir e, sata ruhê mi dibirre, ruh çû qalib ma vala."
4446. 39. He said: "My messenger is a merchant, he cuts the time of my soul, the soul went and the body remained empty."

4447. 40. Qasidê mi delal e,
4447. 40. My messenger is beloved,

4448. Ruhê mi kişande misqal misqal e,
4448. He drew my soul grain by grain,

4449. Ruh çû qalib ma vala.
4449. The soul went and the body remained empty.

4450. 41. Qasidê me lez e,
4450. 41. Our messenger is quick,

4451. Borê min î bez e,
4451. My steed is running,

4452. Bezê xilaz nabim ez e.
4452. By running I cannot be saved.

4453. 42. Bezê navime xilaz,
4453. 42. By running I am not saved,

4454. Yê ser mi ra sekinîye çevê wî weke tas,
4454. The one who has stood over me, his eyes are like bowls,

4455. Tilîyê wî weke risas,
4455. His fingers are like lead,

4456. Neynûk weke almas,
4456. Nails like diamonds,

4457. Sed xazil evdê cahilî bêsûc î bêgune î bêbinîyas,
4457. A hundred blessings upon the ignorant, faultless, sinless and flawless servant,

4458. Bandê Şêxê xwe bive xilaz.
4458. In the call of his Sheikh may he be saved.

4459. 43. Kefenê min înan û pîva,
4459. 43. They brought my shroud and measured it,

4460. Qerqere gaz û nîv e,
4460. The stature is an ell and a half,

4461. Benîademo çi dinyake bê hîv e.
4461. O son of Adam, what a moonless world.

4462. 44. Kefenê mi pîva hîjde gaz e,
4462. 44. They measured my shroud at eighteen ells,

4463. Avîte ser cinîyaze,
4463. They threw it upon the corpse,

4464. Ser min digrî êlî û biraze."
4464. Over me weep the saint and the nephew."

4465. 45. Qalibê melek Ferxedîn danîne dişûşte,
4465. 45. They placed the body of Melek Ferxedîn in the wash,

4466. Weldigerînine ser tenişte.
4466. They turn it on its side.

4467. 46. Lê cema' bibû gişt e,
4467. 46. All had gathered there,

4468. 276. Velî (bnb).
4468. 276. Velî (bnb).

4469. Sata qalibê ezîz melek Ferxedîn danîne dişûşte, weldigerînine ser tenişt e.
4469. At the time they placed the body of dear Melek Ferxedîn in the wash, they turn it on its side.

4470. 47. Ser teniştê weldigêre,
4470. 47. They turn him on his side,

4471. Heçê kesê wê ra,
4471. Whoever is with this,

4472. Ezîz melek Ferxedîn ferha bikin boy kinarê Xudê ra.
4472. Make dear Melek Ferxedîn joyful for the edge of God.

4473. 48. Ez dame ser du darê hişk,
4473. 48. They placed me upon two dry pieces of wood,

4474. Revandin sisîya û çara,
4474. Three and four rushed me away,

4475. Birme meskene mehr û mişk.
4475. They took me to the dwelling of dowry and musk.

4476. 49. Birak divê rastî,
4476. 49. A brother says in truth,

4477. Tirba min birastî,
4477. Truly my tomb,

4478. Kevrê selma mi diguhastî.
4478. They moved my slab stone.

4479. 50. Birak divê taqet bî,
4479. 50. A brother says may there be strength,

4480. Girîya serê min vediket bî,
4480. So that the knot of my head opens,

4481. Pêşîmamekê boy mi diket bî.
4481. Make an imam forward for me.

4482. 51. Tirba min tevav kin,
4482. 51. Complete my tomb,

4483. Serê mi di nav kin,
4483. Put my head inside,

4484. Mala qedîmê silav kin.
4484. Greet the ancient house.

4485. 52. Pev ketin çûne mal e, mezin biçûk, tifal e, go: "Şemso baqî xaş bin înşala."
4485. 52. They joined together and went home, adult, child, infant, they said: "O Şemso, may the eternal be pleasant, God willing."

4486. 53. We da hebû efendî û qadî, go: "Ji nav me çûye melek Ferxedînê pisê Adî,
4486. 53. Among you there were gentlemen and qadis, they said: "Melek Ferxedîn the son of Adî has gone from among us,

4487. Hatye nav me Şerfedînê madî."
4487. Şerfedîn the Mahdi has come among us."

4488. 54. Aşiqa go: "Hîne, ha bi hîn e, yê bîna melek Ferxedîn nav me çûne, em kîa kî ne?"
4488. 54. The lovers said: "Since, oh since, ones like Melek Ferxedîn have gone from among us, who are we then?"

4489. 55. Eva sindrûka sor e,
4489. 55. This is the red chest,

4490. Tê da Ferxê more,
4490. Inside it is the sealed Ferx,

4491. Meleka kişande erşê jor e,
4491. The angels drew him to the high throne,

4492. Ber melkê Qubil dor e.
4492. Before the angel of Qubil dor.

4493. 56. Rabe bavo, hey rabe,
4493. 56. Arise father, oh arise,

4494. Çarşem roja hesave,
4494. Wednesday is the day of account,

4495. Şêx Mend maye bêbav e.
4495. Şêx Mend has remained fatherless.

4496. 57. Ewe sindrûka zer e,
4496. 57. That is the yellow chest,

4497. Ewe tabûta zer e,
4497. That is the yellow coffin,

4498. Meleka kişandibû erşê ser e,
4498. The angels had drawn him to the highest throne,

4499. Ber melkê Yekber e.
4499. Before the Unique angel.

4500. 58. Ewe sindrûka reş e,
4500. 58. That is the black chest,

4501. Ewe tabûta reş e,
4501. That is the black coffin,

4502. Tê da Ferxê keleş e,
4502. Inside it is the handsome Ferx,

4503. Meleka kişandibû erş e,
4503. The angels had drawn him to the throne,

4504. Ber melkê mirazbexş e.
4504. Before the angel who grants wishes.

4505. 59. Ewe sindrûka sipî ye,
4505. 59. That is the white chest,

4506. 277. mahdi (bnb).
4506. 277. mahdi (bnb).

4507. 278. Qubet il-Bidore (bnb).
4507. 278. Qubet il-Bidore (bnb).

4508. 279. ekber e (bnb).
4508. 279. ekber e (bnb).

4509. Ewe tabûta sipî ye,
4509. That is the white coffin,

4510. Tê da Ferxê gulî ye,
4510. Inside it is the rosy Ferx,

4511. Meleka kişandibû erşê 'êlî ye,
4511. The angels had drawn him to the lofty throne,

4512. Ber melkê Bêrî ye.
4512. Before the Innocent angel.

4513. 60. Rabe bavo, hey rabe,
4513. 60. Arise father, oh arise,

4514. Çarşem roja hesave,
4514. Wednesday is the day of account,

4515. Şêx Mend maye bêbav e.
4515. Şêx Mend has remained fatherless.

4516. Temametî Şîx Adî.
4516. The completion is of Şîx Adî.

4517. 280. Melek Ferxedîn Şêx Fexrê Adîya kurê Êzdîna Mîr, birayê Şemsedîn Şêşims, Nasirdîn û Sicadînî ye.
4517. 280. Melek Ferxedîn Şêx Fexr of the Adîs is the son of Êzdîna Mîr, the brother of Şemsedîn Şêşims, Nasirdîn and Sicadîn.

4518. Hemdemê Şêx Hesenî, kurê Şîx Adîyê diduyan, ji gundê Mikêrsê, dikeve bakurê rojhilatê Lalişê.
4518. He is a contemporary of Şêx Hesen, the son of the second Şîx Adî, from the village of Mikêrs, which falls to the northeast of Laliş.

4519. Şêşims û Fexredîn, li gorî gotina gotîyan, dîya wan Stî Zîn bûye, lê dîya Nasirdîn û Sicadînî - Stî Ereb xûşka Şêx Hentûşî.
4519. For Şêşims and Fexredîn, according to the words of the narrators, their mother was Stî Zîn, but the mother of Nasirdîn and Sicadîn was Stî Ereb the sister of Şêx Hentûş.

4520. Du kur û keçeka melek Ferxedîn hebûne: Şêx Mend û Şêx Bedir, Xatûna Ferxa.
4520. Melek Ferxedîn had two sons and a daughter: Şêx Mend and Şêx Bedir, Xatûna Ferxa.

4521. Hin kes dibêjin, na, navê keça wî Xezal bûye, hin jî dibêjin Eyşê bûye.
4521. Some people say, no, the name of his daughter was Xezal, and some say it was Eyşê.

4522. Melek Fexredîn zana û fîlozofekî dînê êzdîyan yê xuya bûye.
4522. Melek Fexredîn was a prominent scholar and philosopher of the Yezidi religion.

4523. Li gorî efsaneya dewra wî di belavkirin û bingehgirtina ola êzdîyan di nava kurdên gelek deveran da pir mezin bûye.
4523. According to legend, his role in spreading and establishing the Yezidi religion among the Kurds of many regions was very great.

4524. Ew gerîyaye li nava miletî û xelq hînî ra û rişmê dîyanetê kirîye.
4524. He traveled among the nation and taught the people the path and customs of the religion.

4525. Gelek qewl û beyt hûnandine.
4525. He composed many qawls and beyts.

4526. Lêkolîner Xêyrî Bozanî di wûtareka balkêş da derbarê melek Ferxedînî da, navê 25 qewl û beytan tîne ber çavan, ku li gorî zanîna wî, hostayê wan melek Ferxedîn e.
4526. The researcher Xêyrî Bozanî, in an interesting article about Melek Ferxedîn, brings to attention the names of 25 qawls and beyts, of which, according to his knowledge, their master is Melek Ferxedîn.

4527. Qewl ev in: 1. Qewlê Zebûnî Meksûr, 2. Qewlê Padşayî, 3. Qewlê Texta, 4. Qewlê Erd û Esman, 5. Qewlê Silav û Sed Silav melek Şîxisin, 6. Qewlê Qîyametê, 7. Qewlê Silavêt Melek Ferxedîn, 8. Qewlê Şêx û Aqub, 9. Qewlê Ez ji Hindav da Çûme Bani, 10. Qewlê Gêla Çar Ziman, 11. Qewlê Şeqe Serî, 12. Qewlê Qerefirqan, 13. Qewlê Xudanê Malê, 14. Qewlê Miskîn Tajdîn, 15. Qewlê Şîrê Rastîyê, 16. Qewlê Meha, 17. Qewlê Omer Xale, 18. Qewlê Ferwarê, 19. Qewlê ji Şamê Tem Meclisê, 20. Qewlê Beygoya, 21. Qewlê Dayik û Baba, 22. Qewlê Axretê, 23. Beyta Cindî, 24. Beyta Sibê, 25. Beyta Bilbila.
4527. The qawls are these: 1. Qewlê Zebûnî Meksûr, 2. Qewlê Padşayî, 3. Qewlê Texta, 4. Qewlê Erd û Esman, 5. Qewlê Silav û Sed Silav melek Şîxisin, 6. Qewlê Qîyametê, 7. Qewlê Silavêt Melek Ferxedîn, 8. Qewlê Şêx û Aqub, 9. Qewlê Ez ji Hindav da Çûme Bani, 10. Qewlê Gêla Çar Ziman, 11. Qewlê Şeqe Serî, 12. Qewlê Qerefirqan, 13. Qewlê Xudanê Malê, 14. Qewlê Miskîn Tajdîn, 15. Qewlê Şîrê Rastîyê, 16. Qewlê Meha, 17. Qewlê Omer Xale, 18. Qewlê Ferwarê, 19. Qewlê ji Şamê Tem Meclisê, 20. Qewlê Beygoya, 21. Qewlê Dayik û Baba, 22. Qewlê Axretê, 23. Beyta Cindî, 24. Beyta Sibê, 25. Beyta Bilbila.

4528. Binhêre Kovara "Laliş"ê, Num. 10, 1999 Dihok, r. 108 -131.
4528. See "Laliş" Magazine, No. 10, 1999 Duhok, pp. 108-131.

4529. Eger em ji hemû 25 qewl û beytan yek-didu hebin, ku bêjin belkî yê wî ne, lê bi xwe ev navnîşana mezin êdî bi xwe şahidetîya wê yekê dide, wekî melek Ferxedîn qewlhûnanekî mezin bûye.
4529. If out of all 25 qawls and beyts we only have one or two that we can say are perhaps his, still, this great title itself bears witness to the fact that Melek Ferxedîn was a great composer of qawls.

4530. Dûrî aqilan nîne, ku gelekên ji qewl û beytan ku wî çêkirine, negihîştine ber destê me jî û winda bûne.
4530. It is not far from reason that many of the qawls and beyts that he created have not reached our hands and have been lost.

4531. ## QEWLÊ MIZGÎNA MÊRA
4531. ## THE QAWL OF THE GOOD NEWS OF THE MEN

4532. 1. Kengê me bête mizgîn e,
4532. 1. When the good news comes to us,

4533. Coqetê tê da rihîn e,
4533. The troops will flow into it,

4534. Ber bi Gelîyê Lalişê diçîne.
4534. They go towards the Valley of Laliş.

4731. ## QEWLÊ MÛSA PÊXEMBER
4731. ## THE QAWL OF THE PROPHET MOSES

4732. 1. Rojekê bû taqet,
4732. 1. One day it was strength,

4733. Riya axî Cibrahîl mala Mûsa ket,
4733. The path of the brother Gabriel fell to the house of Moses,

4734. Mûsaê min pirs bike axîê çi qismet e.
4734. My Moses asks what destiny the brother has.

4735. 2. [Mûsa go:] Ez wî kim yekê xefûr î,
4735. 2. [Moses said:] I will make him a forgiving one,

4736. Ez ruhê xwe te ra nakim destûrî,
4736. I will not give permission for my soul to you,

4737. Ez tenê me, kulfetê min î hûrî.
4737. I am alone, my family is small.

4738. Go: "Mûsaê bin emrano,
4738. He said: "O Moses son of Imran,

4739. Go, roja negir ne înano,
4739. He said, do not complain of days nor believe it,

4740. Risqê kulfet ser milê min te nîne, kefa Xudaê min e."
4740. The provision of the family is not upon my or your shoulder, it is in the palm of my God."

4741. 4. Mûsa Cibrahîl va behrê kiribûne qeste,
4741. 4. Moses and Gabriel had intended for the sea,

4742. Devê behrê kevirek, taşek wê derê ye, qamçî lê dixiste.
4742. At the edge of the sea there is a stone, a rock there, he struck it with a whip.

4743. 5. Ewî taşî waraya, bû baş e,
4743. 5. That rock split open, it became good,

4744. Kurmekî çîlîqerqaş nav e,
4744. A brilliantly shining worm is inside,

4745. Hero serê sibê belgekê şîn jê ra dibû maş e.
4745. Every early morning a green leaf became food for it.

4770. 310. Dixwazin Músa bikeve gorê û bipîve hela ka mezelê ku jê ra kolane û haya wî jê tune ye li gorî qama wî ye yan na.
4770. 310. They want Moses to enter the grave and measure whether the tomb they have dug for him and of which he is unaware is according to his stature or not.

4774. By the honor of Şîx Adî, he said, this is my tomb, but it is a trick."

4775. 14. Go: "Berê vê tirbê reş e,
4775. 14. He said: "The stones of this tomb are black,

4777. The scent and fragrance of this tomb are very pleasant to me."

4778. 15. He said: "The stones of this tomb are yellow,

4779. Earth and stones have come out of it,

4780. Deher bû şêxê min î neder e."

5063. ## QEWLÊ SULTAN ÊZÎD
5063. ## THE QAWL OF SULTAN ÊZÎD

5064. 1. Êzîd didim medê,
5064. 1. I give praise to Êzîd,

5065. Laliş e, helêl e xudanê qubê,
5065. It is Laliş, it is the crescent, the owner of the dome,

5066. Ez xelat kirim Steyra Sibê.
5066. I was rewarded by the Morning Star.

5067. 2. Steyra Sibê xelat kirim,
5067. 2. The Morning Star rewarded me,

5068. Sê herfa ez xebîr kirim,
5068. It informed me of three letters,

5069. Ez hatim rabuhurim.
5069. I came and passed away.

5070. 3. Ez ê rabim herime pêş,
5070. 3. I will rise and go forward,

5071. Wê herfê dikim temtêş,
5071. I will consider that letter,

5072. Herfa jev dikirim heşam, kurêş.
5072. I separated the letters into Hashim, Quraish.

5073. 4. Heşam, kurêş jev dikirin,
5073. 4. They separated Hashim, Quraish,

5074. Qal û qîr deher dikirin,
5074. They manifested the talk and argument,

5075. Feqîr hingê midqîn dikirin.
5075. The faqirs then made certainty.

5076. 5. Feqîra û midqîn e,
5076. 5. It is the faqirs and the certainty,

5077. Heq rîya xwe razî ne,
5077. They are satisfied with their path of truth,

5078. Dest sultan Êzîd da wedanî ne.
5078. They are placed into the hand of Sultan Êzîd.

5079. 329. Meha tebaxê sala 1975an li bajarê Tibilîsîyê ji zarê Tefûrê Şêx Mehmûdî hatîye nivîsîn.
5079. 329. It was written down in the month of August of the year 1975 in the city of Tbilisi from the mouth of Tefûr son of Şêx Mehmûd.

5083. 331. tewtêş (bnb).

5085. 6. Kivs bûme nasebirim,

5153. ## QEWLÊ ŞÊX EREBBEGÎ 'INTÛZÎ
5153. ## THE QAWL OF ŞÊX EREBBEGÎ 'INTÛZÎ

5154. Rojekê sultan Êzîd diçe derê dîwana begê Erebistanê vedike divê: "Selam elêkim, ya Erebbegi."
5154. One day Sultan Êzîd goes, opens the door of the court of the bey of Arabia and says: "Peace be upon you, O Erebbeg."

5155. Begê ereba êzdî bû Şêx Erebbegî 'Intûz pisê Şêxûbekir e, go:
5155. The bey of the Arabs was a Yezidi, Şêx Erebbegî 'Intûz, the son of Şêxûbekir, he said:

5156. 1. Padşayê min, tu yî yeke temam,
5156. 1. My king, you are the complete one,

5157. Sultan Êzîde, elêkime selam.
5157. O Sultan Êzîd, upon you be peace.

5158. Eslê xafila ji hedîd,
5158. The origin of the ignorant is from iron,

5159. Xafil kor bûn, ew surr nedît.
5159. The ignorant were blind, they did not see that mystery.

5160. 2. Eslê xafila ji hesin,
5160. 2. The origin of the ignorant is from iron,

5161. Xafil dîwanê tûj in, weke almas,
5161. The ignorant are sharp in the court, like diamonds,

5162. Xafil kor bûn, rîya sultan Êzîdê min heq nenas.
5162. The ignorant were blind, they did not recognize the true path of my Sultan Êzîd.

5163. 3. Zêr bavêje nava agirî,
5163. 3. Throw gold into the fire,

5164. Xilte venaşêrî,
5164. It does not hide the dross,

5165. Zêr ê bê ser eslê xwe yî berî.
5165. The gold will come to its original form.

5166. 4. Zêr, midhêkî çê ye,
5166. 4. Gold is a good material,

5167. Osta lê dinhêre,
5167. The master looks at it,

5168. Seraf zane bihê ye.
5168. The moneychanger knows its price.

5169. 334. Meha kanûna paş sala 1973an li gundê Mûradtepeyê, li ser nehîyeya Abovyanê -niha li ser nehîyeya Naîrîya Ermanistanê- ji zarê Biroê Şêx Dewrêşî hatiye nivîsîn.
5169. 334. It was written down in the month of December of the year 1973 in the village of Mûradtepe, in the district of Abovyan - now in the district of Naîrî in Armenia - from the mouth of Biro son of Şêx Dewrêş.

5170. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".
5170. It has been printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

5174. 5. Mehnîya zêrîn va ye
5174. 5. The golden meaning is this,

5175. Zêr, ku safira kutaye,
5175. Gold, when the craftsman has hammered it,

5176. Osta lê dinhêrte, seraf zane çi bihête.
5176. The master looks at it, the moneychanger knows what its price is.

5177. 6. Divêjime we alê kitavê,
5177. 6. I say to you, people of the book,

5178. Pirs bikim ji alê Medînê, ji alê Kavê,
5178. Let me ask the people of Medina, the people of the Kaaba,

5179. Çikanî ew kî bû, dot helal kir li bavê?
5179. Who was it then, who made the daughter lawful for the father?

5180. 7. Berê qîl û qar kir,
5180. 7. In the past he did the talk and argument,

5181. Ew Adem bû, dot lê helal kir,
5181. That was Adam, he made the daughter lawful for him,

5182. Şira'ne lê wesal kir.
5182. He made the law reach him.

5183. 8. Newêrim bikêlimim,
5183. 8. I do not dare to speak,

5184. Wekî ez bêjim, sunete[a] berî Adem e,
5184. If I say, the sunnah is before Adam,

5185. Ez ê [şir'eta] biricimim.
5185. I will stone the [sharia].

5186. 9. Sunete[a] berî Adem e,
5186. 9. The sunnah is before Adam,

5187. Ew mehnîke mezin e,
5187. It is a great meaning,

5188. Hidreta mîrê min e.
5188. It is the presence of my prince.

5189. 10. Divêjime we sunete,
5189. 10. I say to you the sunnah,

5190. Rojê heyştê hezar tehlî-tengî li ser we tê,
5190. In a day eighty thousand bitterness and hardship come upon you,

5191. Hûn hewsûdî menhêrin malê şile'tê.

5205. Sive ye, ro hiltêye,

5210. 16. Talib, sofi, ew melle ne,

5211. A derewa xengere ne,

5213. 17. Çi aşekî hûr binyam e,
5213. 17. What a finely grinding mill it is,

5214. God Almighty placed the stone of that mill from wrath,

5215. Roja axretê serê talib, sofî û mella tê hêrane.

5216. 18. Your book is a guide,

5217. God Almighty gave the stone of that mill from wrath,

5249. ## QEWLÊ ŞÊX Û AQÛB
5249. ## THE QAWL OF ŞÊX AND AQÛB

5250. 1. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, çendî roj e, çendî şev e, Min ecêvek dîtîye ew e, Mehsîkî behrê da ye, durrek e [di] deve, Ewî mehsî, ew behr, dikişand xwe ve."
5250. 1. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, for so many days, so many nights, I have seen a wonder, it is this, a fish is in the sea, a pearl is in its mouth, that fish was pulling that sea towards itself."

5251. 2. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, tu xudanê surrê, Qe ne ji wê mehsîyê, ne ji wê behrê, ne ji wê durrê, Kesî nedîdyê kişmiş ser berrê."
5251. 2. Aqûb said: "My master, you are the owner of the mystery, it is neither from that fish, nor from that sea, nor from that pearl, no one has seen pulling on the land."

5252. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, peza stewrî medos, 344 Reza pola mefroş, Meve mişterîyê îmankoş."
5252. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, do not milk the barren sheep, 344 do not sell the steel vines, do not become a faith-killing buyer."

5253. 4. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, zêra navêje nav zikaka,
5253. 4. Aqûb said: "My master, do not throw gold into the streets,

5254. Jev meke gulan û çeka,
5254. Do not separate the roses and the petals,

5255. Ewled naçin eslê maka."
5255. Children do not go to the origin of the mothers."

5256. 5. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, nekî dînî, Toximê xwe hişkebeyanîya mereşînî, Tê roja bandê strîya jê hilînî."
5256. 5. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, do not act crazy, do not sow your seeds on dry lands, on the day of calling you will gather thorns from it."

5257. 343. Meha gulana sala 1982an li gundê Qîbarê Erşîqibar li ser qeza Efrînê Sûrîyeyê ji zarê Şêx Elîyê Şêx Şemoyî hatiye nivîsîn.
5257. 343. It was written down in the month of May of the year 1982 in the village of Qîbarê Erşîqibar in the district of Afrin in Syria from the mouth of Şêx Elî son of Şêx Şemo.

5258. Çap bûye: "Zargotina kurda."
5258. It has been printed: "Folklore of the Kurds."

5259. Cildê II., Moskova, r. 44-49.
5259. Volume II, Moscow, pp. 44-49.

5260. 344. Raz. (ne)
5260. 344. Raz. (ne)

5261. 3. Aqub go: "Seydayê mino, zevîya dewlet e,
5261. 3. Aqûb said: "My master, the field is prosperity,

5262. Tiji naz û nehmet e,
5262. It is full of grace and blessings,

5263. Xwey lê têr bîye muhubet e."
5263. The owner is satisfied with it, it is love."

5264. 7. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, zeviya ji zevîyane zêde, Heft gisna lê de, Hew paştir, paşê toximê xwe pê de."
5264. 7. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, the field is more than fields, strike seven plowshares on it, just further back, then give your seed to it."

5265. 8. Aqub go: "Seydayê mino, zevîya ser-seda dirêj, Bê toz e, bê xubar e, bê niqêş, Sêrî heye, ferz û te'yat û nimêj."
5265. 8. Aqûb said: "My master, the field is hundreds long, it is without dust, without dirt, without pattern, it has a mystery, obligations and devotions and prayers."

5266. 9. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, sere sar û germ in,
5266. 9. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, the secrets are cold and hot,

5267. Serakanîya binî anî ber me,
5267. You brought the bottom spring before us,

5268. Xwekirîya tu lê nave derman."
5268. For what you did to yourself, you will not be a cure for it."

5269. 10. Aqûb go: “Seydayê mino, jev dûr in hişkelî û serakanî,
5269. 10. Aqûb said: "My master, dry lands and springs are far from each other,

5270. Heta hişkelîya av jê bê,
5270. Until water comes from the dry land,

5271. Serakanîyê here ber cewla Şîx Adî, ber cewlê."
5271. The spring will go before the stream of Şîx Adî, before the stream."

5272. 11. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, ez pişta bavê xuliqîm, Berê dayê tiviqîm, Hingê ez merîfetê gilîya şiviqîm."
5272. 11. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, I was created in the back of the father, I took form in the womb of the mother, then I slipped into the wisdom of words."

5273. 12. Aqub go: "Seydayê mino, ez pişta bavê hewyam,
5273. 12. Aqûb said: "My master, I took refuge in the back of the father,

5274. Berê dayê rivyam,
5274. I grew in the womb of the mother,

5275. Hingê ez merîfetê gilîya hisîyam."
5275. Then I felt the wisdom of words."

5276. 13. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, ez pişta bavê pîr bûm, Berê dayê şîr bûm, Hingê ez merîfetê gilîya xebîr bûm."
5276. 13. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, I became old in the back of the father, I became milk in the womb of the mother, then I became informed of the wisdom of words."

5277. 14. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, ez pişta bavê kal bûm, Berê dayê tifal bûm, Hingê ez merîfetê xîyal bûm."
5277. 14. Aqûb said: "My master, I became an old man in the back of the father, I became a child in the womb of the mother, then I became a thought of wisdom."

5278. 15. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, şuxula Xwedê weku anî, weku çêkir,
5278. 15. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, the work of God as He brought it, as He made it,

5279. Ruh nava ser û dest û pê kir,
5279. He put the soul into the head and hands and feet,

5280. Ew kijan mêr bû, kasa qudretê lê kir?”
5280. Which man was that, who poured the bowl of power for him?"

5281. 16. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, ew şuxula Xwedê weku anî, Ruh nava ser û dest û pê danî, Ew ezîz melek Ferxedîn bû, kas pê anî."
5281. 16. Aqûb said: "My master, that work of God as He brought it, placed the soul into the head and hands and feet, it was the dear angel Ferxedîn, who brought the bowl to him."

5282. 17. Şêx ji Aqûb pirsîye: "Husnîkî cisnîyê,
5282. 17. The Şêx asked Aqûb: "Of good lineage,

5283. Melekê bêrîyê,
5283. Angel of longing,

5284. Tê bêjî mi rastîyê,
5284. You will tell me the truth,

5285. Çika ew roja rukna dinê danîne, çika ew kî roj bîye?"
5285. What day was that when they placed the pillars of the world, what day was it?"

5286. 18. Aqûbî ber şêxî zebûn e, Deyn kir, eynata ezîz melek Ferxedîn e, Go: "Roja rukna dinê danîne, şem û în e.
5286. 18. Aqûb is wretched before the Şêx, he spoke, the mirror is the dear angel Ferxedîn, he said: "The day they placed the pillars of the world, it is Saturday and Friday.

5287. 19. Şemîyê danîn asas e,
5287. 19. On Saturday they placed the foundation,

5288. Çarşemê birrîn kiras e,
5288. On Wednesday they cut the shirt,

5289. Înîyê dinîya pê bû xilas e. »>
5289. On Friday the world was finished by it. »>

5290. 20. Sex go: "Aqubè mino, hisnîkî cisnîyê, Melekê bêrîyê, Tê bêjî mi rastîyê, Çikaně jehra mehrî ji çi ye?"
5290. 20. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, of good lineage, angel of longing, you will tell me the truth, what is the poison of the snake from?"

5291. 21. Aqubî ber şêxi zebûn e, Deyn kir, eyneta ezîz melek Ferxedîn e, Go: "Jehra mehrî xaziya Firêc e. 345
5291. 21. Aqûb is wretched before the Şêx, he spoke, the mirror is the dear angel Ferxedîn, he said: "The poison of the snake is the spittle of Firêc. 345

5292. 22. Firêc xaziya xwe dirête,
5292. 22. Firêc spits his spittle,

5293. Mehr dighîştê dimête,
5293. The snake reaches it and sucks it,

5294. Dest fihal, jehra xwe pê girê dide."
5294. Instantly, it ties its poison with it."

5295. 23. Şêx ji Aqubî pirsîye: "Husnîkî cisnîyê,
5295. 23. The Şêx asked Aqûb: "Of good lineage,

5296. Melekê bêrîyê,
5296. Angel of longing,

5297. Tê bêjî mi rastîyê,
5297. You will tell me the truth,

5298. Hinek ax ber qalibê Adem pêxember ma, ma li ku yê?”
5298. Some earth remained from the mold of Prophet Adam, where did it remain?"

5299. 24. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, Axa ber qalibê Adem pêxember ma, Pê ava kirin Qurs û Xelîl e."
5299. 24. Aqûb said: "My master, the earth that remained from the mold of Prophet Adam, with it they built Jerusalem and Hebron."

5300. 25. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, Hindeki dinê jî ber mabû."
5300. 25. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, some more of it had also remained."

5301. 26. Aqúb go: "Seydayê mino,
5301. 26. Aqûb said: "My master,

5302. 345. filen (bnb).
5302. 345. filen (bnb).

5303. 'Êrifa jê nemabû, Qubil, Sibil jê peyda bû."
5303. Knowledge of it did not remain, wheat and barley appeared from it."

5304. 27. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, Hindekî dinê jî jê ber mabû."
5304. 27. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, some more of it had also remained."

5305. 28. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, 'Erifa jê nemabû, Dara temenê jê peyda bû."
5305. 28. Aqûb said: "My master, knowledge of it did not remain, the tree of wishes appeared from it."

5306. 29. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, Hindekî dinê jî jê mabû."
5306. 29. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, some more of it had also remained."

5307. 30. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, 'Êrifa jê nemabû, Av û agir jê peyda bû."
5307. 30. Aqûb said: "My master, knowledge of it did not remain, water and fire appeared from it."

5308. 31. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, Hindekî dinê jî jê mabû."
5308. 31. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, some more of it had also remained."

5309. 32. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, Pembu jê peyda bû."
5309. 32. Aqûb said: "My master, cotton appeared from it."

5310. 33. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, Hindekî dinê jî jê mabû."
5310. 33. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, some more of it had also remained."

5311. 34. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino,
5311. 34. Aqûb said: "My master,

5312. Çira jê peyda bû,
5312. The candle appeared from it,

5313. Ser bane Kabetullaye46 dane bû,
5313. It was placed on the roof of the Kaaba, 46

5314. Cin Teyar dadayê rivabû,
5314. Jinn Tayyar flew from it,

5315. Para hemû kesî jê nedabû."
5315. A share for everyone was not given from it."

5316. 35. Şex go: "Aqûbê mino,
5316. 35. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb,

5317. Bêje, çika ewê behrê xeriqi, kî ye?
5317. Tell me, who is that one who drowned in the sea?

5318. Ewê behrê tiviqîye, kî ye?"
5318. Who is that one who took form in the sea?"

5319. 36. Aqub go: "Seydayê mino,
5319. 36. Aqûb said: "My master,

5320. Ewê behrê xeriqî, Şibhûn e,
5320. That one who drowned in the sea, is Şibhûn,

5321. Yê behrê tiviqîne, her heft mêrê Kaf û Nûn e."
5321. Those who took form in the sea, are all seven men of Kaf and Nun."

5322. 37. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, Em xever din Adem pêş va, Hebû, av ne diçû cewa êş va, Xwerin-vexwarina wana cimlet û cêş va."
5322. 37. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, let us speak of before Adam, there was, water did not flow into the streams of pain, their eating and drinking was in gathering and army."

5323. 38. Aqub go: "Seydayê mino, nevî ne, nevîyê cebêr in, Xandinê wane ji dêr in, Xarina wana şikrûm e, Vexwarina wana, erhemdulla, rehma Xwedê a têr in."
5323. 38. Aqûb said: "My master, they are grandchildren, grandchildren of the almighty, their reading is from the church, their food is gratitude, their drink, praise be to God, is the plentiful mercy of God."

5324. 39. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, ez im serê sara, Min gogek revandîyê nava bîst û çar hezara, Hila hê min saxîke dilê xwe negotîyê tu biran û yara,
5324. 39. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, I am the head of the secrets, I snatched a ball among twenty-four thousand, yet I have not spoken an honesty of my heart to any brothers and friends,"

5325. 346. K'abet ilahîyê (bnb).
5325. 346. K'abet ilahîyê (bnb).

5326. 40. Aqub go: "Seydayê mino, ez im Aqûbê Mûsa,
5326. 40. Aqûb said: "My master, I am Aqûb of Musa,

5327. Ferxan û fêriza,
5327. Of the young and the learned,

5328. Yê mîna şêx, wê rûnîn miclîsa,
5328. The one like the Şêx, will sit in the councils,

5329. Yê mîna Aqûb, wê jê bikin pirsîyar û pirsa."
5329. To the one like Aqûb, they will ask questions and inquiries from him."

5330. 41. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, çendî roj hiltêye, Min deste goşt te dibêye, Ne nêr be, ne jî mê ye."
5330. 41. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, for so many rising suns, a handful of flesh tells you, let it be neither male, nor is it female."

5331. 42. Aqub go: "Seydayê mino, çendî roj zeriqî, Nûr, ji nûrê tiviqî, Hingê Şibhûnî pak bû, behrê xuliqî."
5331. 42. Aqûb said: "My master, for so many shining suns, light took form from light, then the pure Şibhûn was created in the sea."

5332. 43. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, dilê min kelat e, Agirek tê da hildihate, Dişewitî welat û berb' welat e."
5332. 43. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, my heart is a fortress, a fire rose in it, it burned the country and towards the country."

5333. 44. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, dilê min kela dinijî,
5333. 44. Aqûb said: "My master, my heart boils and seethes,

5334. Agirek tê da dihilmijî,
5334. A fire breathes within it,

5335. Dişewitî welat berb' welat, welatê di[n] jî.
5335. It burned the country towards the country, and the other country too."

5336. 45. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, 'Êrifo, serxweşo, Helalê xwe, heramê xelqê meşo."
5336. 45. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, knowledgeable one, intoxicated one, go to your lawful, do not go to the forbidden of the people."

5337. 46. Aqûb go: "Seydayê mino, Aqûbî xudan neder e,
5337. 46. Aqûb said: "My master, Aqûb is the owner of the unseen,

5338. Eyneta ezîz melek Ferxedîn deyn dikere,
5338. He borrows the mirror of the dear angel Ferxedîn,

5339. Îşalla, helalê xwe, heramê xelqê nadere."
5339. God willing, to his lawful, to the forbidden of the people he does not go."

5340. 47. Şex go: "Aqube mino,
5340. 47. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb,

5341. Deşta Kerbelayê,
5341. The plain of Karbala,

5342. Heta şêx dindara xwe nedayê,
5342. Until the Şêx gave his calling,

5343. Aqube Músa ne ruhyabû pişta dayê."
5343. Aqûb of Musa was not conceived in the mother's back."

5344. 48. Aqub go: "Seydayê mino,
5344. 48. Aqûb said: "My master,

5345. Deşta Kerbe deştê,
5345. The plain of Karbala is a plain,

5346. Raste heta dîndara şêx negîhîşte,
5346. It is true, until the calling of the Şêx reached,

5347. Aqúbè Músa neruhyabû piştê."
5347. Aqûb of Musa was not conceived in the back."

5348. 49. Şêx go: "Aqûbê mino, Qewatek 347 heye mehele, Xarina wî qewmî xerdel e."
5348. 49. The Şêx said: "My Aqûb, there is a force 347 in a place, the food of that people is mustard."

5349. Aqûb wê herfê caw nedabû.
5349. Aqûb had not given an answer to that letter.

5350. 50. Şêx borê xwe dimismisand, Nava dîwanê meleka da direqisand, Go: "Min herfekê da Aqûbê Mûsa tirsand."
5350. 50. The Şêx made his steed restless, he made it dance in the court of the angels, he said: "With one letter I frightened Aqûb of Musa."

5351. 51. Şêx borê xwe hilkende,
5351. 51. The Şêx spurred his steed,

5352. Lê hilda toq û zende,
5352. He raised the collar and wristband on it,

5353. Go: "Min herfekê da Aqûbê Mûsa kire bend e."
5353. He said: "With one letter I bound Aqûb of Musa."

5354. 347. A people. (bnb).

5552. 1. Dewrêşo, serê xwe xema hilîne,
5552. 1. O dervish, lift your head from sorrow,

5553. Borê niga betilîne,
5553. The steeds of the legs tired,

5554. Cindî çûne dîwana mîr hasilîne.
5554. The riders went and reached the court of the prince.

5555. 2. Hasilîn ji qudretê,
5555. 2. They reached it from power,

5556. Xas natirsin ji hêwetê,
5556. The pure ones do not fear the awe,

5557. Milkê xasa, baxê cinetê.
5557. The property of the pure ones is the garden of paradise.

5558. 3. Cinet e maşxur bû,
5558. 3. It is paradise, it was engaged,

5559. 'Eyneta dayn nekiribû,
5559. The mirror had not been borrowed,

5560. Piştî yarê xwe yî gogir bû.

5561. 4. I make a ball, I spin it,

5562. I become joyful, I raise my voice,

5563. O Sultan Êzîd, I am longing for you,

5565. 5. I see that calling,
