5567. The friend and brother of the afterlife have come to the bargain.

5575. 7. What a dervish he is,

5581. 9. What a dervish of the path he was,

5582. He was the diver of the sea,

5583. He was longing for Sultan Êzîd, for that pearl.

5584. 10. Çi dojeke xedar e,
5584. 10. What a cruel hell it is,

5585. It is full of fire and inferno,

5586. Cîyê xelqê selefxurî inkar e.
5586. It is the place of the people of usury and denial.

5587. 11. Çi dojeke teng e,
5587. 11. What a narrow hell it is,

5588. Tijî agir û piling e,
5588. It is full of fire and leopards,

5589. Cîyê xelqê selefxurî, inkarî leng e.
5589. It is the place of the people of usury, denial and the lame.

5590. 12. Go: "Gelî bira kar kin, neçine wê ye,
5590. 12. He said: "O brothers, work so as not to go there,

5595. 13. Pleasant Arfut, Dervish Adam manifested in it,

5596. Momina dil pê kesirî,
5596. The believers were broken-hearted by it,

5597. Roja axretê heqê wan dest sultan Êzdîd neheqîyê da betilî.
5597. On the day of the afterlife their right in the hand of Sultan Êzîd nullifies the untruth.

5599. He said: "Sultan Êzîd read the sealed writing,"

5634. 1. Dewrêşo, serê xwe ji xema hilîn,
5634. 1. O dervish, lift your head from sorrow,

5635. Borê lenga betilîn,
5635. The steeds of the legs tired,

5636. Cindî çûn dîwana mîr wesilîn.
5636. The riders went and reached the court of the prince.

5637. 2. They reached that presence,

5641. They borrowed the mirror,

5643. 4. They played ball in the square,

5644. My king is the owner of patience and steering,

5649. 6. Let me truly see that calling,

5650. I became a green flower at the start of spring,

5654. Yar-birê axretê ra bikim vê bazarê.
5654. Let me make this bargain with the friend-brother of the afterlife.

5655. 7. The bargain is for the prince,

5656. I speak of meanings and actions,

5658. 8. What a dervish of state I am,

5659. Sometimes I am a market, sometimes I am a question,

5661. 9. I am a dervish of the path,

5664. 10. I am a golden dervish,

5667. 11. Dewrêşekî ha me,
5667. 11. Such a dervish I am,

5668. Tilifek nûr baha me,
5668. I am a shoot worth light,

5669. Mêr û meleka ha reng didame.
5669. Men and angels gave me such color.

5670. 12. Men and angels say such color,

5671. Before them is fire, hell, blazing flame,

5682. 15. Sultan Êzîd came and settled,

5683. Momino dil kesirî,
5683. O believers, broken-hearted,

5688. 17. The path of Sultan Êzîd is straight, it is not hidden,

5698. ## QEWLÊ XAFILÊ BÊNASÎN
5698. ## THE QAWL OF THE IGNORANT WITHOUT RECOGNITION

5699. Xafilê bênasîn e,
5699. He is the ignorant without recognition,

5700. Hatye ser me kerb î kîn e,
5700. He has come upon us with anger and hatred,

5701. Ew heye dijminê dîn e.
5701. He is the enemy of religion.

5702. 2. Xafilo, tu axirîyê gul ve,
5702. 2. O ignorant one, open a rose in the end,

5703. Kaxeza berîyê şil ve,
5703. Moisten the paper of the beginning,

5704. Rohilatê rave, tehrîstanê hilve.
5704. Rise in the East, arise in the dawn.

5705. 1. Xafilê bêedev e,
5705. 1. He is the ignorant without manners,

5706. Hatye ser me xezev e,
5706. He has come upon us as wrath,

5707. Îlahîyo, morkeva xafila rast neve.
5707. O God, may the mount of the ignorant not be straight.

5708. Îlahîyo, morkeva xafila rast nebûyî,
5708. O God, the mount of the ignorant was not straight,

5709. Bandê hewca mêrekî xerqe bûyî.
5709. On the day of calling he was in need of a man with a garment.

5710. 5. Hewce me da ji motac,
5710. 5. We were in need from necessity,

5711. Banga xwe dikin feqîrê dilqê bitac.
5711. The faqirs of the crowned cloak make their call.

5712. 6. Banga xwe dikin feqîrê tacî kulik,
5712. 6. The faqirs of the crown and cap make their call,

5713. Dîwana Şîx Adî kemilî bi nik,
5713. The court of Şîx Adî was perfected nearby,

5714. 374. It was written down in the month of December of the year 1973 in the village of Tolk - now Ciraşên - in the district of Masîs in Armenia from the mouth of Lezgî son of Şêx Etar.

5715. It has been printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

5717. 375. Hilbibe.
5717. 375. Arise.

5718. 376. merkeba (bnb).
5718. 376. mount (bnb).

5719. Îlahîyo, tu mirazê mêra bikî bê şik.
5719. O God, may you fulfill the wishes of the men without a doubt.

5720. 7. Xafilo, ji mal bezî,
5720. 7. O ignorant one, you ran from home,

5721. Tirêqa xwe ra daneherizî,
5721. You did not follow your path,

5722. Bandê nav agirê cehnimê da venegevizî.

5723. 8. O ignorant one, you run from home,

5724. Tirêqa xwe ra nekî qal e,
5724. Do not argue with your path,

5725. So that on the day of calling you do not remain empty.

5726. 9. Xafilo, dibezî berî stêr e,
5726. 9. O ignorant one, you run before the star,

5727. Do not fight with your path,

5728. Bandê neyê rûyê te nevû û çêr e.

5729. 10. Herça feqîra ra dijmin dibûyî,
5729. 10. Whoever was an enemy to the faqirs,

5730. Their load was iron,

5731. As high as Mount Sîpanê Xelatê it was,

5733. 11. Xwezila biçûma dîwana Şîx Adî, cîyê sola,
5733. 11. I wish I had gone to the court of Şîx Adî, the place of shoes,

5734. Bowls and cups at the pool of buckets,

5735. Herça nuxte xarîye, bîye safîkî pola.

5736. 12. Safîkî pola me,
5736. 12. I am pure like steel,

5737. Bavekî berbihêrî me,

5742. 13. Xaliqo, rengê te divînim lora rengê behara,
5742. 13. O Creator, I see your color, therefore it is the color of spring,

5897. ## SILEMAN-PÊXEMBER Û BUM
5897. ## PROPHET SOLOMON AND THE OWL

5898. 1. Teyr û tuyê Beyt' il-Farê,
5898. 1. The birds of Beyt' il-Farê,

5899. Derbaz dikin li rû dinîyaê,
5899. They pass over the face of the world,

5900. Silo gote jina xwe Belqîzayê:
5900. Silo said to his wife Belqîza:

5901. 2. "Ji perê teyrê ber bi welat,
5901. 2. "From the feathers of the birds towards the country,

5902. Em ê koçkekê çêkin du qat,
5902. We will build a palace of two floors,

5903. Bi wê bivne xinê û xelat."
5903. With it they will become ornament and reward."

5904. 3. Ewî bi morê hukum da,
5904. 3. He gave a command with the seal,

5905. Teyr top kirin ji çar qulba,
5905. The birds gathered from the four corners,

5906. Ew hukumeki zehf giran e,
5906. That command is very heavy,

5907. Li ser hemû teyr û tûyan e.
5907. It is upon all the birds.

5908. 4. Ew teyr û tûya dicivîne,
5908. 4. He gathers the birds,

5909. Per baska li wan birûçkîne,
5909. He plucks their feathers and wings,

5910. Wana bihêlê bê cî û war,
5910. He leaves them without place and home,

5911. Koçkê çêke xwe ra sitar.
5911. He builds a palace for himself as a shelter.

5912. 5. Çarinkal civyan teyrê feqîr, Ew cema' bûn li dîwana mîr.
5912. 5. From four sides the poor birds gathered, they assembled at the court of the prince.

5913. Sekinîn li ber Beyt' il-Farê,

5944. 13. "Mîrê min hukmê te giran e,

5948. 14. Mîr [go]: "Tu li çeva binêr çewan e?”

5949. Bûm [go]: "Çevê min yê mêran e,"

5951. Bûm [go]: "Serê min yê şêran e.”

5956. 400. Balçemoke.
5956. 400. Bat.

5957. Li gorî vê efsaneyê balçîmok xwe berîya hemû teyr û tûyan dirûçikîne, paşê piştî ku Silêman pêxember guh dide teyr û tuyan û bûm gazinan dike li ser vê meseleyê û poşman dibe, balçîmok rûçikandî dimîne.
5957. According to this legend, the bat plucks itself before all the birds, then after Prophet Solomon listens to the birds and the owl complains about this matter and he repents, the bat remains plucked.

5958. Dibêjin loma ji ber wê ye bi roj fedî dike derkeve û bifire, loma bi şevan derdikeve û difire.
5958. They say therefore because of this it is ashamed to come out and fly by day, therefore it comes out and flies by night.

5959. 16. Bona te û Belqîzayê,
5959. 16. For you and Belqîza,

5960. Em ê hişk bin li dinyayê,
5960. We will become dry in the world,

5961. Tu bawerîya bîne yeqîm,
5961. Bring your belief to certainty,

5962. Per û bask te ra navne hîm.
5962. Feathers and wings will not become a foundation for you.

5963. 17. Sibê bakê li koçka te rabe,
5963. 17. Tomorrow a wind will rise at your palace,

5964. Her perekî wê cîkî da bela be,
5964. Every feather will scatter in a place,

5965. Em teyr û tûyê behz,
5965. We birds of prey,

5966. Em ê bimînin sêfîl belengaz.
5966. We will remain wretched and poor.

5967. 18. Hê gotina bûme li devî,
5967. 18. The word of the owl was still in its mouth,

5968. Qijika reş qeîdê va revî,
5968. The black crow fled with the chain,

5969. Silêman selawet veda,
5969. Solomon offered a blessing,

5970. Destûra teyr û tûya da.
5970. He gave permission to the birds.

5971. 19. Lê şîrînê bilbil dila,
5971. 19. But the sweet nightingale of hearts,

5972. Dîsa vegerîya nava gula,
5972. Returned again among the roses,

5973. Nav gula bû şayî û deng,
5973. Among the roses there was joy and sound,

5974. Bona bilbilê bask reng.
5974. For the colored-winged nightingale.

5975. 20. Teyr û tû aza bûn,
5975. 20. The birds became free,

5976. Ji hev bela bûn,
5976. They scattered from each other,

5977. Rûyê gotina bûm da,
5977. For the sake of the owl's word,

5978. Mîr destûra teyra da.
5978. The prince gave permission to the birds.

5979. ## ŞEHDETIYA DÎNÊ ÊZDYA
5979. ## THE TESTIMONY OF THE YEZIDI RELIGION

5980. 1. Serê min belgî,
5980. 1. My head is a pillow,

5981. Belgîyê min şivakê,
5981. My pillow is a nightcap,

5982. Sêrî çûme zikakê,
5982. I went up to the alley,

5983. Bidî xatirê Êzîd makê.
5983. Give it for the sake of the mother Êzîd.

5984. 2. Serê min qulbe, Berê min rohilat, Ser mi ra sekinî du celat, Go: "Miskino, Tacdino, benîo, Şehdetîya dînê xwe bîne, ez ê serê te hilînim."
5984. 2. My head is a dome, my front is the East, two executioners stood over me, he said: "O poor one, O Tacdîn, O slave, bring the testimony of your religion, I will lift your head."

5985. 3. Go: "Şehdetîya dînê min mikîn Ella, Şix Isin hebûb Ella, Mergaê Meqlûbê selaê, Selaê binîmaê, cîyê Şerq, Şam lê diçe taê sûcûdaê."
5985. 3. He said: "The testimony of my religion is firm by God, Şîx Isin was the beloved of God, the meadow of Maqlub is the prayer, the prayer we establish, the place of the East, Damascus goes to it in the thread of prostration."

5986. 4. Sicûda me diçe bal Şîx Adî,
5986. 4. Our prostration goes to Şîx Adî,

5987. Şîx Adî redaê,
5987. Şîx Adî in the path,

5988. Şêx Şims melkê mêraê,
5988. Şêşims is the king of men,

5989. Şix Adî ser kursi westaê,
5989. Şîx Adî was tired upon the chair,

5990. Şehderîya dînê xwe heq navê Êzîd daê.
5990. The testimony of his religion truly gave the name of Êzîd.

5991. 5. Şîx Adî nûr e,
5991. 5. Şîx Adî is light,

5992. 401. Meha nîsana sala 1976an li gundê Şamîranê yê li ser nehîyeya Aştaraka Ermenistanê ji zarê Zaîlê Şêx Keleşî hatiye nivîsîn.
5992. 401. It was written down in the month of April of the year 1976 in the village of Şamîran in the district of Ashtarak in Armenia from the mouth of Zaîl son of Şêx Keleş.

5993. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda".
5993. It has been printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

5994. Cildê I., Yêrêvan, r.377.
5994. Volume I, Yerevan, p. 377.

5995. Melek Ferxedîn xefûr e, Şehdetîya dînê xwe heq navê Êzîd qebûl e.
5995. Angel Ferxedîn is forgiving, the testimony of his religion truly accepts the name of Êzîd.

5996. 6. Sinî me, sinî nevî me,
5996. 6. I am a Sunni, I am a Sunni descendant,

5997. Silavkêşê Kanya Sipî me,
5997. I am the greeter of the White Spring,

5998. Mirîdê Şêxê 'Edî me.
5998. I am the disciple of Şêx Adî.

5999. 7. Qelema melek Şîx Isin nivîsî me,
5999. 7. I am written by the pen of angel Şîx Isin,

6000. Erhemdille şêx, pîr, oste, merhebî,
6000. Praise be to God, the Şêx, pir, master, and the welcoming one,

6001. Yar-birê axretê,
6001. The friend-brother of the afterlife,

6002. Her pênc tirêqê xwe razî me.
6002. I am satisfied with all five of my paths.

6003. 8. Celatê ruhê min Nasirdîn,
6003. 8. The executioner of my soul is Nasirdîn,

6004. Atqata min sultan Êzîd,
6004. My belief is Sultan Êzîd,

6005. Dînê min Şerfedin,
6005. My religion is Şerfedîn,

6006. Rehmel ruhê ostaê min,
6006. Mercy upon the soul of my master,

6007. Şîx Adî yek Ella,
6007. Şîx Adî is one by God,

6008. Êzîd hebûb Ella.
6008. Êzîd is the beloved of God.

6009. ## TEMEDİYA ŞIX ADÎ
6009. ## THE MEDITATION OF ŞÎX ADÎ

6010. 1. Babilko, tu rave rehmanî,
6010. 1. O Babilko, you arise mercifully,

6011. Diwan geriya qeynter e,
6011. The court wandered at the arch,

6012. Şix Adî zane, kî li pêş e, kî li ber e.
6012. Şîx Adî knows, who is in front, who is before.

6013. 2. Binatara vî qewli girê da 'Eynz-Beynzayê,
6013. 2. The foundation of this qawl was tied to 'Eyn il-Beyza,

6014. Yar û birê axretê hûn ravne simayê,
6014. O friend and brother of the afterlife, run to the face,

6015. Kereme xudanê keremê,
6015. It is the grace of the owner of grace,

6016. 3. Cêşê Gelîyê Lalişê,
6016. 3. The army of the Valley of Laliş,

6017. Gulbanîke rehmetê, yeka axretê,
6017. A prayer of mercy, one of the afterlife,

6018. Rehmel li dê û bavê hadir-gudêra.
6018. Mercy upon the parents of the present and absent.

6019. 4. Mirîd momina, pîr hostayê me jî pê ra,
6019. 4. Believing disciples, our pir and master also with it,

6020. Mal-mezelê em tê da,
6020. The house and room we are in,

6021. Rehmel gora seydayê mi ve.
6021. Mercy open upon the grave of my master.

6022. 402. Meha kanûna paş sala 1973an li gundê Tolkê yê -niha Ciraşên- li ser nehiyeya Masisa Ermenistanê ji zarê Lezgîê Şêx Etarî hatîye nivîsîn.
6022. 402. It was written down in the month of December of the year 1973 in the village of Tolk - now Ciraşên - in the district of Masîs in Armenia from the mouth of Lezgî son of Şêx Etar.

6023. Çap bûye li "Zargotina kurda."
6023. It has been printed in "Folklore of the Kurds".

6024. Cildê. II., Moskova, r. 23.
6024. Volume II, Moscow, p. 23.

6025. E'yn il-Beyzayê (bnb).
6025. E'yn il-Beyza (bnb).

6026. Gêşê (bnb).
6026. The army. (bnb).
